<pb n="b001"/>
<head>bṛhatī</head>
<head>prabhākaramśriviracitā ।।</head>
<head> prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ ।।</head>
<p>uktaṃ kāryamarthaṃ pratipādayato vedasya prāmāṇyam । yasya punaḥ kāryeṃ'-
rthe'nvayo nāvagamyate'kāryatayā, tasya yaḥ pratipādakaḥ tasya kathaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ
so'rodīdityevamādeḥ ? । mā bhūttasya prāmāṇyaṃ; na tadapramāṇatayā pramāṇa-﻿<pb n="b002"/>
mapramāṇaṃ bhavati । pramāṇasya hi anapekṣatvamuktam; na cānyasyāprāmāṇyāt
pramāṇe tadapaiti । atha manyase sakalasya vedasya prāmāṇyaṃ na prāpnotīti,﻿<pb n="b003"/>
kenedaṃ pratijñātaṃ ? yato'rthāvagatiḥ tasya tallakṣaṇataiveti pratijñā । sā
cānapekṣatayā sādhitā । yatastvarthāvagatireva nāsti tadapramāṇameva । yato
vā pramāṇāntarapramitaviṣayaivāvagatiḥ tasyāpi tata eva prāmāṇyamityuktaṃ,﻿<pb n="b004"/>
viparyaye cāprāmāṇyamiti । tasmādasaṃbaddhaiveyaṃ cintā—akriyārthānāṃ katha-
miti ।</p>
<p>tadviparyayāt svādhyāyavidherānarthakyamiti cet, na svādhyāyaśabda-
vācyasyādhyayanaṃ vidhīyate nārthavato'narthakasya vā humityevamādīnāmiva ।
tasmātko'yamupālaṃbhaḥ ? । svādhyāyavidheḥ prayojanaśūnyatā prāpnotīti cet ?﻿<pb n="b005"/>
tanna, niyogārthanirvṛtteḥ kimanyat prayojanaṃ sarvavidhīnāṃ, sa cākṣaragrahaṇenaiva
nirvṛttaḥ । arthajñānaṃ cārthājjātaṃ, na niyogataḥ pratipannam । na hi artha-
jñānakāmasya niyogaḥ, nahi paśvādīnāmiva vedārthasyānyataḥ prasiddhirasti
yena tatkāmasyādhyayanaṃ vidhīyate । nanu ca vedavadvedārthasyāpi svādhyāyādanya-
taḥ prasiddhirasti । na hyaprasiddhasya kāraṇatā śakyate vaktum । prasiddhaścet﻿<pb n="b006"/>
sutarāmevaṅkāmasya vidhānaṃ nopapadyate jñeyatayaiva hi tat kāmyate । jñātasya ca
jñeyatayā kāmyatvaṃ nopapadyate । niyamārtho vidhiriti cet । na । anyataḥ
parijñānābhāvāta । grahaṇāntataiva svādhyāyaśabdenocyata iti cet । kena
coktaṃ svādhyāyaśabdena grahaṇāntatocyata iti । agṛhītāttarhyarthajñānamasti;﻿<pb n="b007"/>
nāgṛhītādarthajñānamasti agrahaṇe varṇamātragrahaṇāt । vākyāvagamāditi cet,
gṛhītaṃ tarhi vākyam । na hyagṛhītaṃ vākyatvenāvagamyate । tasmānna niyamasyāyaṃ
gocaraḥ । nāpyarthajñānakāmasyāyaṃ vidhiḥ ataḥ prāmaṇaṃ pramāṇameva, apramāṇa़ṃ
apramāṇamastu । satyamevaṃ yathoktaṃ pitṛmatā—tadeva tu prāmāṇyamakāryārthasaṃba-
ndhamavagamyate । tataḥ kim ? idaṃ tataḥ akāryārthatā vedasya prāpnoti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b008"/>
<p>nanu ca kāryārthatāpyasti । na । akāryapūrvakatvāt । akāryo hyartho
hetutāṃ pratipadyate kāryārthasya । pradarśita caitat—rudraḥ kila ruroda ।
ato'nyenāpi roditavyamiti । tasmāttatprabhavaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ tacca pramāṇāntarāpekṣa-
miti anapekṣatvamevākṣipyate ।</p>
<p>nanu caitat prāmāṇyasiddhyarthamupanyastaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa । kimityanyatraivopa-﻿<pb n="b009"/>
nīyate । satyam । siddhasya sādhyaikavākyatā pradarśyate । tadekavākyatve
ca kāryārthatā nāstītyetadeva pradarśyate ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ tarhyayaṃ granthaḥ adhyāhāreṇa veti ? kiṃ vāsya granthasya ? ida-
masya, kartavyatvānekavākyatvādaprāmāṇyaṃ na punarakartavyataikavākyatvāditi ।﻿<pb n="b010"/>
uktam-anekavākyatve acintanīyo'yamartha iti । atrāpi cānarthajño bhavān ।
atredamevākṣipyate । nahi siddharthānugamāt kartavyatā'vasātuṃ śakyate—
yathā asminneva tāvat—kiṃ śakyante rodanādayaḥ kartum ।</p>
<p>nanvaśakyatayā na śakyante na punaḥ siddhānugamāt । siddhatayaiva
hyaśakyatoktā । siddhasya pramāṇāntarāpekṣatvāt tasya cātrāsambhāvādiṣṭa-﻿<pb n="b011"/>
gādeḥ prameyasya sambandhino'sambhavāta; rudrasambandhīṣṭaviyogādigrāhakapramāṇāntarābhāvāditi
yāvat । <q>tathā ca pramāṇāntarābhāvaṃ darśayati</q> । <quote>“na hyātmano vapāmutkhidya tatastasyā vapāyāḥ
prahṛtāyā utthitena tūpareṇa śakyate yāgaḥ kartuṃ”</quote> iti ।</p>
<p>yadyatrāpi siddhānugamādevāśakyatā, kimiti <q>tarhyavāntaravākyopanyāsaḥ mahāvākya
evaitat</q> sidvānugamenāśakyatvaṃ kimiti punarna darśitam । uttaram&mdash;<q>avāntavākyakalpanā-
yāmapi etasmātsiddhānugamānna <note n="1"><dn>A mucyāmahe</dn></note>mucyata</q> ityabhiprāyaḥ । sarvaprakāramaprāmāṇyaṃ darśayituṃ
avāntaravākyopanyāsaḥ । yadi mahāvākyaṃ yathāśrutamāśrīyate tathāpi siddhānugamaḥ; athā-
śrutamapyavāntaravākyamāśritaṃ tathāpi sa eva siddhānugama iti sarvathaivāprāmāṇyāt । <q>tadidaṃ</q>
siddhānugamenāprāmāṇyaṃ <q>ucyate&mdash;āmnāyasya kriyārthatvādānarthakyamatadarthānāmiti</q> ।</p>
<p>atra codayati&mdash;<q>kimidamatadarthānāmiti viśeṣābhidhānam</q> । ekagranthenāha&mdash;
<q>nanu ca sarva evedānīmatadartho vedaḥ</q> । sarva evākāryārtha ityaktam । <quote>‘<q>vasantāya kapiñjalā-
nālabhata iti nāsti siddhānugama iti cet</q> । vasantāya kapiñjalānālabhata iti siddhārthānu-﻿<pb n="b012"/>
<p>gamābhāvāt <note n="1">C <dn>kāryārthameva ।</dn></note>kāryārthametat; tenaitadvyudāsāya <quote>‘ava/?/darthānā’</quote>miti viśeṣābhidhānam ।
ākṣeptā āha&mdash;<note n="2">A <dn>āyāta ।</dn></note><q>tadevedamāpatitamacintanīyo'yamartha iti</q> । yadi kiñcitkāryārthaṃ kiñci-
ccākāryārthaṃ tadā nedamadhikaraṇamārabdhavyam । yasyaiva kāryārthatvaṃ tadviṣayatvenāpi codanā-
lakṣaṇapratijñopapatteḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu yadi siddhārthānugamābhāvādānarthakyaṃ kapiñjalānālameta ityādivākyānāmacinta-
nīyamidaṃ, tadā bhavatvacintanīyaṃ; naitāvatā <note n="3">C <dn>siddhānugamaḥ ।</dn></note>siddhārthānugamaḥ kapiñjalādivākyānāṃ śakyate
<note n="4">A <dn>avagantuṃ ।</dn></note>vaktumityāśaṅkyāha&mdash;<q>na kapiñjalādivākyānāmapi kāryārthatvam; teṣāmapi siddhārthenaika-
vākyatvāt</q> । <quote>‘vasantāya kapiñjalānālamata’</quote> ityaṅgavidhaya ete । aṅgavidhayaśca pradhāna-
vidhinaikavākyatāpannāḥ । pradhānavidhiśca siddhārthenaikavākyatāpanna iti sarveṣāmapi
sākṣādekavākyatāpannaṃ vidhyantaragataṃ vā siddhārthamastyevaikavākyatāpannaṃ <note n="5">C <dn>padamiti ।</dn></note>padajātamiti
sarva evākāryārtho vedaḥ । <q>ato'tadarthānāmiti na nivartyaṃ kiñcidavasīyate</q> ।
samādhātā āha&mdash;<q>idamavasīyate-siddhasādhyārthatayā vākyānāṃ siddhārthamukhena ayamākṣepaḥ</q> ।
yenaiva rūpeṇāsāvākṣepaḥ tadeva dyotayituṃ atadarthānāmityuktam, na punaḥ kasyacidvyā-
vṛttyartham । <q>ata idamuktam ānarthakyamatadarthānāmiti । yathā ca siddhārthāpekṣitayā''kṣepaḥ
tathoditam;</q> vivṛtaṃ ca bhāṣyakāreṇa <quote>‘tānyekadeśākṣepeṇākṣipyanta’</quote> iti । eka&mdash;﻿<pb n="b013"/>
vākyatve hi sati ekadeśatā bhavatyarthavādānām<note n="1">C <dn>vādapadānāṃ ।</dn></note> । anyathā <note n="1">C <dn>svātantryeṇaikadeśatvānupapatteḥ ।</dn></note>svatantrasyaikadeśānupapatteḥ ।
tena ekadeśaśabdaṃ prayuñjānena bhāṣyakāreṇa ekavāktāśrayaṇenāyamākṣepa iti vivṛtam ।
yadyekavākyatvāśrayaṇenāyaṃ pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ, <q>kathaṃ tarhi rāddhānte ekavākyatāṃ prati praśnottare</q> ।
pṛcchati&mdash;ko'bhiprāyastava kathaṃ tarhi rāddhānta ekavākyatāṃ prati praśnottare iti vadataḥ ।
<q>uttaram&mdash;ayamabhiprāyo mama; ekavākyatānibandhano'yaṃ prāmāṇyākṣepo na bhavati;</q>
kintu <q>bhinnānāṃ vākyānā</q>marthavādātmakānāṃ <q>kā pratipattiḥ</q> ? kīdṛśī varṇanā ? iti
cintāyāṃ pūrvapakṣe akriyārthatvenā<q>narthakyamabhidhāya atra rāddhānte stutyarthatve</q>naikavākyatvā-
<q>darthavattoditeti</q> । yadi hyekavākyatāśrayaṇenākṣepo bhaveta naikavākyatāśrayaṇena samādhānaṃ syāt;
tasmāt bhinnavākyatvena pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ekavākyatvena rāddhānta ityavagamyate । pariharati&mdash;﻿<pb n="b014"/>
<q>aho ajñānakātaryamāyuṣmataḥ pradarśitamasmābhiḥ&mdash;tānyekadeśākṣepeṇākṣipyanta iti</q> ।
ekavākyatvāśrayaṇenāyamākṣepa ityetatpradarśanaparaṃ bhāṣyam । tena ekavākyatvāśrayaṇenaivāyaṃ
kṛtsnasya vedasya prāmāṇyākṣepaḥ । <q>rāddhānte tu ye praśnottare tatraiva</q> rāddhānta eva <q>codanīye</q>
kathamete praśnottare iti । bhavatā tu ajñānakātareṇa pūrvapakṣāvasthāyāmeva yaccoditaṃ tat tava
kātaryaṃ kevalam । kiñca <q>parihartavye ca</q> samādhātavye ca ete praśnottare rāddhāntakāla evā-
smābhiḥ । tena codyāvakāśa evātra nāsti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b015"/>
<p><q>yatpunaridānīṃ udāharaṇabhedenānarthakyamuktam śāstradṛṣṭavirodhācca</q> ityevamādibhiḥ
sūtraiḥ tat pūrvapakṣe <q>hetuprapañcārthaṃ</q> pūrvapakṣahetūn prapañcayitum । <q>hetuprapañcasya prayojanaṃ</q>
śabdādhikaraṇa <q>uktam</q>&mdash;sarve pūrvapakṣahetavaḥ upanyasya nirākāryāḥ । anupanyaste hi kasya
cinmandadhiyaḥ punarutkopo bhavediti । <q>asmiṃstvayamaparo viśeṣaḥ parihārāntarapariharaṇīya-
tvam</q> &mdash; yathā yāvantaḥ śabdāḥ nityatvahetavaḥ ekenaiva pratijñopanyāsena parihriyante tathaite
ānarthakyahetavo na bhavanti nānāparihārapariharaṇīyatvātḥ tasmāt pṛthamupanyastāḥ pṛthak
pṛthak parihāradānāyeti ।</p>
<p><q>tasmādanityamucyata</q> iti sūtram; tadanupapannamiva pratibhāti । yadi tāvadvākyasyā-
nityatvamucyate tatsiddhāntino'pi sammatameva । anityaṃ hi kāraṇavattvamucyate; yaddhi kāraṇavat
tadanityam । vākyañcānu<note n="2">C <dn>ānupūrpīviśeṣa ।</dn></note>pūrvyaviśeṣaparigṛhītavarṇātmakapadasaṅghātātmakaṃ ānupūrvyasya kāraṇattvena
kāraṇavat । na ca tādṛśe'nityatvamucyate, tadaśakyaṃ varṇānāṃ nityatvāt । padārthānāñca yadyapi
keṣāñcidanityatā tathāpi keṣāñcidgotvādīnāṃ nityatvādityāśaṅkyāha&mdash;<q>tasmādanityamucyata iti ।
siddhārthāpekṣitayā pramāṇāntarasavyapekṣārthatvaṃ anityatvaṃ, śabdārthayornityatvālloke vedepi</q> ।</p>
﻿<pb n="16"/>
ataeva bhāṣyakāreṇāpyayamartho vivṛtaḥ । <quote>yadyapi nityāni na nityakāryaṃ
kurvanti</quote> iti । kiṃ punarnityasya kāryaṃ ? pramāṇāntarānapekṣaṃ svārthaprati-
pādanam । ataḥ pramāṇāntarānapekṣataiva nityatocyate । tenāsyā
evāyamākṣepaḥ—tasmādanityamucyata iti ।</p>﻿<pb n="17"/>
<p><q>vidhinā ।। vidhyuddeśenaikavākyatvāt iti ।</q> kasyedaṃ vyākhyānam ?﻿<pb n="18"/>
vidhinetyasya ? nanu ca nopapadyate vidhirvidhyuddeśaḥ । satyaṃ,
lakṣaṇayocyate । kimiti lakṣaṇā ? ekavākyatvāditi vacanāt ।
ekavākyatvaṃ vidhinā nopapadyate । vidhinaiva hi sarvasyaikavākyatā ।
satyaṃ kartavyatānvayaḥ yasya । na ca stuteḥ kartavyatā'vasīyate ।
kiṃ tarhi ? stutyena saṃbandhaḥ । kiṃ vidhyartho na stutyaḥ ? na
brūmo na stutya iti । kṣepiṣṭhatvādayastu guṇāḥ vidheye stutimutpādayanti;
ta evātadarthānāmityākṣiptāḥ; ākṣepasamādhānārthaṃ caitat sūtram; tasmāt﻿<pb n="19"/>
yuktā lakṣaṇā । ata eva ca <quote>kathamekavākyatvaṃ</quote> iti praśnaḥ ।
kimidaṃ ? idamidam vidhyuddeśenaikavākyatvam । vidhyuddeśasya ca
tadanekavākyatvācca na kartavyatāvagamaḥ akartavyatāvagame ca nāsti
prāmāṇyam । ato'yaṃ praśnaḥ kathamekavākyatvamiti ।</p>
<p>itara āha—<q>uktaṃ vidhyuddeśeneti । nanu caivaṃ siddhārthatā prāpnoti,
na kāryārthatā । kimidaṃ siddhārthatā na kāryārthateti ?
uktam—na kāryārthatayā pratīyata iti । kutastarhi kāryārthatāvagatiḥ﻿<pb n="20"/>
vidhyuddeśāditi brūmaḥ । maivaṃ vocaḥ, nāyamabhisaṃbandho vivakṣitaḥ
ālabheta bhūtikāma iti । ālabheta yatastato bhūtiḥ—iti ।
kimanenoktam ? na vidhyuddeśāt kāryāvagatiḥ । kiṃ tarhi ?
sastutipadāditi vadāmaḥ । taduktaṃ<q>—bhinnāvimāvarthāviti ।</q>
ko'bhiprāyaḥ ? ayamabhiprāyaḥ—syādvidhyuddeśādeva kāryāvagatiḥ yadye-
karūpāvagatiḥ syāt sastutipadāt kevalapadācca । iha tvanyarūpai-
vāvasīyate । ālabheta bhūtikāma ityeko'vagatyupāyaḥ । ālabheta
yataḥ tato bhūtirityayamanyaḥ । ayamapi codvidyāt kathamānartha-
kyamatadarthānām ।</p>﻿<pb n="21"/>
<p><q>kimarthā stutiriti cet ?</q> iti tulye kāryāvagame kimupāyāntarā-
śrayaṇena । kathaṃ copāyāntaratvaṃ ? kasyātropālambhaḥ, kena vedamāśritaṃ﻿<pb n="22"/>
kena cotpāditam kintu śabdādevāvagamyate । anekapadābhidhāne hi
na padāntaranirapekṣādarthāvagatirdṛṣṭā । tathā darśitam-<quote>paṭo bhavati raktaḥ paṭo
bhavati</quote> iti । na raktapadanirapekṣāt padadvayādavagatiḥ dṛśyate । saiṣā
autpattikī śaktiriti ।।</p>﻿<pb n="23"/>
<p>nanu ca vināpi tena sidhyediti punarānarthakyameva coditam ।
satyaṃ vakturayamupālaṃbhaḥ na pratipattuḥ; na ca tairvinā pratipattirityuktam;
pratipattāraśca vayam na vaktāraḥ, vede vaktā nāstītyuktam ।</p>﻿<pb n="24"/>
<p>nanu ca satsvapi stutipadeṣu pūrvasya vidhisarūpattvāt vidhirabhipretaḥ
syāt; na vivakṣyeta stutipadasaṃbandha iti kimatra coditam ? । idamatra
coditam । kimavāntaravākyānvayo nāsti padārthānvayavādino hi
naivedamarthāntaram ।</p>
<p>anarthāntaratve ca siddhaiva । avāntarānvayāt kāryāvagati-
rnasiddhyati । sakalapadārthāvagatau satyāṃ kathamavāntarānvayasya nimittatā
śakyate kalpayitum । tasmāt sakalapadapadārthānvayanimittaiva kāryāvagatiḥ﻿<pb n="25"/>
na avāntarānvayanimittā bhavitumarhati ।</p>
<p>1<q>nanu nirapekṣādvidhimavagamiṣyāma iti ।</q> kimidamanuktamuktam ।
<q>idamanuktamuktam ।</q> nanvavāntarānvayasyāpi nimittatvamabhyupagataṃ
bhavatā । bāḍhamabhyupagatam । ko doṣaḥ ? nanvayaṃ doṣaḥ । atrāpi
tadapahnotuṃ na śakyate । satyaṃ, pratīyamānaṃ hyapanhotuṃ na śakyate na
punarapratīyamānamapi । na cātrāvagatidvayamasti vākyabhedaprasaṅgādi-
tyuktam । <q>atha yaduktam na ca kriyā'vagamyate, kriyāsaṃbaddhaṃ vā
kiṃciditi ।</q> nanu kartavyatā stutipadānna gamyate । kartavyatāṃ ca
vedaḥ pratipādayatītyavaidikatvam ।</p>﻿<pb n="26"/>
kena coktaṃ vaidikatvaṃ ? veda evāyaṃ, yato hi kartavyatā'vagamyate sa
vedaḥ asmācca kartavyatāvagamyata ityuktam । prāmāṇyasya cāyamākṣepaḥ
kṛtaḥ । sa cāyaṃ pratisamāhitaḥ । kimatra vaidikatvena ।</p>
<p>nanvevaṃ sati vidhyuddeśasyāpyavaidikatvaṃ, tadapi hi pratipattau
nimittam, asāvapi veda eva । bāḍhaṃ nimittatayā, na tu naimittikatayā,
stutipadārthastu nimittameveti viśeṣaḥ ।।</p>﻿<pb n="27"/>
<p>tulyaṃ ca sāṃpradāyikam ।।</q> kadācidiyamāśaṅkā syāt vidhyuddeśa-
stutyarthaṃ bālānāṃ pravṛttaye prakṣiptānyarthavādapadānīti । tadayuktam ।
tulyaṃ ca sāṃpradāyikam । naiva kaścit prakṣepamarthavādapadānāṃ smarati ।﻿<pb n="28"/>
vidhyuddeśānāmivāvagatyantaraṃ nāstītyuktam । evaṃ cedrodanānupapattiḥ parihṛtā ।
pratyuta kāryāvagatāvayaṃ doṣaḥ na punaḥ siddhārthāvagatau ।।</p>
<p>nanu caivaṃ sati pramāṇamātraparyavasāyiṣu arthavādapadeṣu mṛgyaṃ pramā-
ṇāntaraṃ stutyavagatau, na ca tadasti yathā avakā vidhīyante āpaśca stūyante ।﻿<pb n="29"/>
evaṃ cārudati roditīti śabdaḥ । evaṃ sarvatra stenādiṣu ।
tasmāt punarapyanupapattireva ।। neyamanupapattiḥ । vidhyarthenaikavākyatve
sati yathā pramāṇāntareṇa saṃbandho'vagamyate tathā vyākhyeyam । taduktam
—guṇavādastviti । hetupracayaparihārastu hetuvadevāvagantavyaḥ ।।</p>﻿<pb n="30"/>﻿<pb n="31"/>﻿<pb n="32"/>﻿<pb n="33"/>﻿<pb n="34"/>
<p><q>vidhirvā syādapūrvatvādvādamātraṃ hyanarthakam ।</q> uktaṃ bhūtārthānāṃ
kāryārthapratipādakatayā prāmāṇyam । yatra punaḥ kāryataivāvagamyate
kāryāntareṇa caikavākyatvaṃ tatra kathaṃ ? yathā 'auduṃbaro yūpo bhavati'
iti । <quote>ūrgvā uduṃbara urk paśavaḥ ūrjaivāsmā ūrjaṃ paśūnāpnoti
ūrjo'varudhyai</quote> iti yūpoduṃbarayoḥ sādhyasādhanatā'vagamyate, paśūduṃbarayorapi ।
gamyate ca ekavākyatvaṃ yasmādudumbareṇa paśavaḥ sādhyante tasmādaudumbaro
yūpaḥ kartavya iti ।</p>﻿<pb n="35"/>
<p>kimatra yuktam । sādhyāvagame saṃbhavati siddhāvagatirna yuktā ।
kasmāt ? vidhyarthatvādvākyasya vidheśca sādhyākāṃkṣitvāt । na caṃ
mukhye'rthe saṃbhavati lakṣaṇā yuktā ।।</p>
<p>nanu ca sādhyadvayamekasmin vākye na saṃbhavati । vayamapyetadeva
brūmaḥ । tasmānnibījamevedamarthadvayaṃ pratīyate ।</p>﻿<pb n="36"/>﻿<pb n="37"/>
<p>nanu cānekasminnapi pratipādye'rthe saṃbhavati ekavākyatā dṛṣṭā
yathā devadatta gauḥ krayyetyevamādiṣu laukikeṣu vākyeṣu । viṣama
upanyāsaḥ tatra hi arthavaśādvākyanirṇayaḥ । iha tu śabdādevāvagantavyaḥ ।
ataḥ saṃbhavadvidheyānāṃ stutyarthena prāmāṇyaṃ durghaṭam ।।</p>
<p>atrocyate-<q>uktaṃ tu vākyaśeṣatvam ।।</q> satyamuktaṃ, tattu nopapadyate;
dvayoḥ sādhyatvenāvagamādityapyuktam । kimidaṃ viruddhaṃ pralapyate ।﻿<pb n="38"/>
na hi dvayoḥ sādhyayoḥ guṇayoriva samatvāt saṃbandhaḥ । kathaṃ
tarhyekārthāvagatiḥ ? yadyavagatirasti tadanurūpaṃ nimittaṃ kalpanī-
yam ।। nanu ca sādhyadvayaṃ pratīyate । na tarhyekārthāvagatiḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="39"/>
<p>asti ceyam । yasmādanenedaṃ bhavati tasmādanenedaṃ kuryāditi । siddhaṃ
tarhi bhavatītyasyārthasya siddhārthatvam । kathaṃ siddhasya bhavatīti vyapadeśaḥ ?
pramāṇāntarataḥ siddhiratropayujyate nārthataḥ siddhiḥ । siddhamasiddhaṃ
vā pramāṇāntarapramitamarthāntarāvagatau nimittatāṃ pratipadyate । tasmādekārtha-
tvāt siddhaṃ prāmāṇyamatrāpi ।।</p>﻿<pb n="40"/>
<head>vidhiścānarthakaḥ kvacit ।।</head>
<p>nanu ca vidhyasambhavādevādhastye'dhikaraṇe pramāṇamātraparyavasāyitvaṃ-
muktamarthavādānām; iha tu prameyatāstītyāśaṅkitaṃ, nirastaṃ ca । kimidamucyate
<q>vidhiścānarthakaḥ kvaciditi ?</q> kvavā vidherarthavattve sambhavati kevalaṃ pramāṇa-
toktā yenedamucyate 'vidhiścānarthakaḥ kvacit iti । tatsāmānyāditi ।
kimidaṃ tatsāmānyam ? vidhisambhavaḥ evātra pradarśitaḥ nāsambhavaḥ ।
ayathārthagrāhiṇa idaṃ codyam ।</p>﻿<pb n="41"/>
<p>atrāpi sādhyadvayamupanyasyatā vidheyasya stutyarthatā nāvagamyata
ityuktam । yatra vidheyāsambaddhā stutiravagamyate na tatra stutyartheneti
śakyate vaktum । tadidamucyate—<q>vidhiścānarthakaḥ kvaciditi ।</q> na hi
vetase vidheye āpaḥ śāntā iti stutirupapadyate । na cāpsu jāyanta iti
vidhiḥ sambhavati, tathāpyekārthāvagateḥ nimittatvaṃ parikalpyate evamatrāpi
bhavitumarhatīti । idaṃ tatsāmānyam । <q>prakaraṇe ca sambhavanniti ।﻿<pb n="42"/>
<p>kimanenopanyastam ? idamanenoparanyastam—ekavidhyarthatve sambha-
vati nānekavidhyarthatā yuktā kalpayitum; viniyojakavirodhāt ।﻿<pb n="43"/>
viniyogamātrāpekṣī viniyojakaḥ sa na śakyate viniyogabhedāt anyathā-
kartum, tadanyathātve pauruṣeyī kalpanā prāpnoti । kiñca vidhyantaratopi vākya-
bhedaḥ prāpnoti । kiṃ jātam ? ekārthāvagaterbādhaḥ । bādhyatām, na niyogo
viniyogaṃ bādhitumarhati । kāryato hi bādhaṃ bādhavido manyante ।﻿<pb n="44"/>
tasmādvastutaḥ sādhyadvayāvagamepi pramāṇataḥ siddhasādhyatayaiva hi ekārthā-
vagatiriti sthitamevaṃvidheṣvapi pramāṇatvam ।</p>
<p><q>heturvā syādarthavattvopapattibhyām ।</q> kā punaratrāprāmāṇyaśaṅkā ?
yadi hetvarthaḥ karaṇaṃ yadi vā śūrpārthaḥ ubhayathāpi anvitapadārthako vākyārthaḥ ।﻿<pb n="45"/>
ananvayini hi padārthe nimittatayā naimittikatayā vā pratibhā-
mātram । ataścāprāmāṇyaṃ na tvanvayini । tasmāt pramāṇalakṣaṇāntaḥ
pātitā kathamasyādhikaraṇasya ? । na cārthāntaraṃ yuktamatrārpayitum,
prasaṅgābhāvāt anaupodghātikatvācca ।</p>
<p>nanu cāyamastyeva prasaṅgaḥ kimarthavādo neti । satyamasti
niṣprayojanastu saḥ । nanu cedamasti prayojanaṃ arthavādatve śūrpeṇaiva homaḥ﻿<pb n="46"/>
itarathā hyaniyama iti । satyamastīdaṃ prayojanaṃ tārtīyaṃ tvetat ।
na ca lakṣaṇāntaraprayuktaṃ prāsaṅgikaṃ bhavitumarhati । cintitaṃ
caitannivītaṃ manuṣyāṇāmityevamādiṣu । tasmāt pramāṇalakṣaṇāntaḥ
pātitaivāsya vaktavyā ।</p>
<p>seyamucyate—hetupakṣe hi tannimittaṃ karaṇatvaṃ jñāyate । yadi
vedātsiddhaṃ tarhi vaidikatvam । satyaṃ siddham; sāpekṣantu । sāpekṣatve
ca pramāṇāntaraṃ mṛgyam । na ca tadastīti pratibhāmātram । tasmā-
ddhetutvamidānīṃ pratipadyate । heturayam kāryatvenānvayasambhavāt । na
pramāṇamātraparyavasāyitā śakyate vaktuṃm, kāryārthatvādanvayasya ।</p>﻿<pb n="47"/>
<p>nanu ca śūrpasyānnakaraṇatā na sambhavati । asādhakatamatvāt
vyāpṛtasya cānyatrākaraṇatvāt । upapadyate hi karaṇatvamāpekṣikatayā । āpe-
kṣikī hi vivakṣā, vivakṣātaśca kārakāṇi bhavantīti kārakajñāḥ । vartamānakāla-
tāpyasya āpekṣikyevetyuktaṃ kālajñaiḥ । tasmādupapanno'yam-arthavattvopapatti-
bhyamiti । avaśyaṃ cāyamāpekṣikakaraṇabhāvo grahītavyaḥ; stutāvapi tulyatvāt ।</p>
<p><q>stutistu śabdapūrvatvādacodanā ca tasya ।</q> atrocyate—nāyaṃ
hetuḥ । kasmāt ? śūrpahome hi hetuḥ pratīyate । siddhaśca﻿<pb n="48"/>
hetuḥ na sādhyatayā'vagantuṃ śakyate । homasya ca sādhyāvagatirvedāt ।
na ca sādhyatvenāvagamyamāno vedāt sāpekṣo bhavati । tasmāt hetuvadevāyaṃ
na hetuḥ । evaṃ ca kṛtvā avartamāno'pi vartamānatayā pratipattuṃ śakyate ।</p>﻿<pb n="49"/>
<p>nanu ca vartamāna eva nāstītyuktam ? kena coktaṃ nāstīti । phala-
paryanta ārambho vartamānavyapadeśaṃ bhajatīti sthitam । na punarvidhipakṣa
etadupapadyate । na hyarthāntare prayogaḥ śakyate nirūpayitum ।
āpekṣikatvaṃ ca karaṇasya madīya eva pakṣe śakyate nirūpayitum ।
vidhipakṣe hi kriyāntaratā kena vāryate ।</p>﻿<pb n="50"/>
<p>śūrpaśabdāditi cet nivṛttāstarhi darvīpiṭharādayaḥ vyāhataśca
hetvartho bhavati । ata evamuktam—yadi ca heturavatiṣṭheta
nirdeśācchūrpa eveti । hetvavyāghāta iti cet—avyavasthā
tarhi । avyavasthāyā api sa eva heturvyāghātaḥ nivartyābhāvāt ।﻿<pb n="b051"/>
kārakasya hetoḥ nivartyābhāvepyātmalābho jñāpakasyeva । tasmāddhetuvanni-
gadānāmapi pramāṇatayaivāvasthānam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b052"/>
<p><q>tadarthaśāstrāt ।</q> yaduktaṃ <quote>‘dṛṣṭo hi tasyārthaḥ karmāvabodhanaṃ
nāma’</quote> iti tadayuktam । avivakṣitārthatvaṃ svādhyāyasya mantreṣu
dṛśyate kathamavivakṣitārthatvam ? tadarthaśāstravirodhādibhiḥ navabhiḥ
pradarśyate । nanu cāvivakṣitārthatve tadarthaśāstrādayopyavivakṣitārthā eva ।</p>﻿<pb n="b053"/>
omityucyate । kathaṃ tarhi tairavivakṣitārthatvam ? parasparavyāghātāda&mdash;
sambaddhārthataiva avivakṣāhetuḥ । yadi mantrā avivakṣitārthāḥ tadā tadartha-
śāstrāṇāmavivakṣitārthatvamiti parasparavyāghātaḥ । raśanābhidhānavivakṣāyāṃ﻿<pb n="b054"/>
<p><quote>‘aśvābhidhānīmādatta’</quote> ityasya tadarthaśāstrasya vyāghātaḥ । na ca
parisaṅkhayādibhiḥ śakyate vyāghātaḥ parihartumiti pradarśitam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b055"/>﻿<pb n="b056"/>﻿<pb n="b057"/>
<p><q>aviśiṣṭastu vākyārthaḥ ।</q> atrābhidhīyate&mdash;nāvivakṣitārthaḥ
svādhyāyaḥ । niyogasambandhitayā svādhyāyasyārthavattā uk‍tā kārye
prāmāṇyābhidhānāt kāryārthābhidhānatayā paraprayogepi ।</p>﻿<pb n="b058"/>
<p>kimidaṃ prayoga iti ? anuṣṭhānamityarthaḥ । anuṣṭhīyamānārthaupayi-
katayā vivakṣitārthatvamavagamyamānaṃ na śakyate tadarthaśāstradibhirvihantum ।
prāptārthānuvādakānyapi vākyāni dṛśyante <quote>‘ya evaṃ vidvān paurṇaṃmāsīṃ yajata’</quote>﻿<pb n="b059"/>﻿<pb n="b060"/>﻿<pb n="b061"/>﻿<pb n="b062"/>
ityevamādīni । na caitānyatadarthakāni iti pradarśitaṃ devatāvidhānādibhiḥ
viśeṣaiḥ । evaṃ pratisūtraṃ draṣṭavyam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b063"/>
asya cārthasya nyāyyatvaṃ vaidikānyapi liṅgadarśanāni upo-
dvalayanti <quote>‘āgneyyā āgnīdhramupatiṣṭhate’</quote> ityevamādīni ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ prathamādhyāyasya
dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b064"/>
<head>atha tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><q>dharmasya śabdamūlatvādaśabdamanapekṣaṃ syāt</q>&mdash;kimidamaprastutaṃ
cintyate ? kimaprastutam ? acodanārthavicāraḥ bravīti ca
dharmasya śabdamūlatvādaśabdamanapekṣaṃ syāt iti । aśabdaścenna
pratijñātaṃ; apratijñātacintā ca pratijñāṃ vihanti । pūrvāparavirodhāccā-
﻿<pb n="b065"/>
buddhipūrvakatā prāpnoti । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;idamapi vedavidbhiḥ
pramāṇatayā parigṛhītam । tasmādidamapi vicāraṇīyamiti । tada-
yuk‍tam । pratyakṣādyapi taiḥ pramāṇatayā parigṛhītaṃ tadapi vicāraṇīyaṃ
prāpnoti । <q>nanu ca</q> vicāritametat । kva vicāritam ? satsaṃprayoge
puruṣāṇāmityaṃtra pramāṇamiti । kiṃ pratyakṣaṃ pramāṇamapramāṇamityasya
saṃśayasya nirṇayāya tatsūtram ? dharmaṃ prati pramāṇaṃ na bhavatītyetatparaṃ
﻿<pb n="b066"/>
sūtraṃ, na tarhi pramāṇāntaraṃ pramāṇatayā cintitamasmin śās‍tre ।
tasmātpratijñātaṃ cintanīyaṃ nābhyupagataṃ apratijñātaṃ ca smṛtiśāstram ।
ato'saṃbadvaiveyaṃ cintā ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate-pratijñātārthasya cinteyam । nanu ca svatantraśabda-
viṣayā sā pratijñā na cātra svātantryamasti । satyaṃ, svātantryaṃ nāsti
svatantraśabdaviṣayaiveyaṃ cintā । kimaṣṭakā kartavyeti svatantraśabdaḥ ?
﻿<pb n="b067"/>
nāyaṃ svatantraśabdaḥ svatantraśabdasambandhastu । kena svatantreṇāsya
sambandhaḥ ? yāṃ janāḥ pratinandantīti । tataḥ kim ? sāpekṣapara-
tantratvāt asyāpi sādhakatā prāpnoti tatsāmānyāccetareṣāmapi । tadi-
damāha&mdash;<q>dharmasya śabdamūlatvādaśabdamanapekṣaṃ syāt iti ।</q> ape-
kṣitaṃ caitat yāṃ janāḥ pratinandantītyevamādibhiḥ । ata eṣāmaśabdataiveti
﻿<pb n="b068"/>
sa eva pratijñātārthaḥ punarākṣipyate । na sāpekṣānapekṣayoḥ
ekārthatvaṃ saṃbhavatītyuk‍taṃ viṣayabhedāditi ।</p>
<p>nanu cātra viṣayabheda eva na saṃbhavati dvayoḥ kāryārthatvāt
tadeva hi na saṃbhavatītyucyate । nanu ca kāryārthasyaiva anumānaṃ
bhaviṣyati । tatparityāge kāraṇaṃ vak‍tavyam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b069"/>
<p>nanu ca kāryāvagatirapi tyak‍taṃ na śakyate tadānupūrvyasiddhamanu-
mānaṃ kena vāryate; satyaṃ na vāryate yadyatra smaraṇābhimāno na syāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b070"/>
smaraṇābhimāne ko doṣaḥ ? smaraṇādanumānaṃ prāpnoti na kāryataḥ । kiṃ
tataḥ ? smaraṇaṃ hi pramāṇaviṣayaṃ nārthaviṣayaṃ; kimiti ? tatpurassaratvādartha-
saṃvidaḥ । siddhaṃ tarhi prāmāṇyaṃ; neti brūmaḥ ayathārthatvepi saṃbhavāt ।
﻿<pb n="b071"/>
tasmānna kāryato'numānasiddhiḥ&mdash;asmākaṃ cedamanumānam । na cāsmākaṃ
smaraṇavyavadhānādidamupapadyate na kāryaṃ smaraṇasambandhi kāraṇasambandhi
tata । na ca vyavahitasya nirapekṣaṃ tadastītyanapekṣam । tasmādvandhyā&mdash;
sutasmaraṇatulyamidaṃ kāryam । nanu cānidaṃprathamatāpi tathātve heturdṛṣṭā-yathā
śabdārthāvagatau vedo'yaṃ brāhmaṇo'yamiti । viṣama upanyāsaḥ
dṛṣṭe'rthe'nidaṃprathamatā yuktā । arthadarśanameva hi tatra mūlatāṃ
﻿<pb n="b072"/>
pratipadyata iti । iha tu tasyābhāvaḥ । tasmānmṛgyamatra pramāṇāntaraṃ
na ca tatpramāṇāntaramastītyuktam । tasmādacodanālakṣaṇo dharmaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>api vā kartṛsāmānyāt pramāṇamanumānaṃ syāt ।</q> nā-
pramāṇaṃ codanā, pramāṇasya hi tathātve'vagatireva kāraṇam । ayathārthatve
punaḥ duṣṭakāraṇatā viparyayaśca । seyaṃ tāvadavagatirasti na ca viparyayaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b073"/>
nanu ca kāraṇābhāvāt duṣṭakāraṇatānvayaḥ; kimabhāvaḥ kāraṇe śakyate
vak‍tuṃ; kimiti na śakyate ? vedasaṃyogasya saṃbhavāt; satyaṃ
kāraṇasyābhāvo na śakyate vak‍tum । bhāvo'pi naiva ।</p>
<p>nanu kāryata evāvagamyate kāraṇasya bhāvaḥ na, smaraṇavyavadhānādi&mdash;
tyuktam । kimidaṃ smaraṇavyavadhānāditi ? idaṃ tat, smaraṇaṃ hyatra pramāṇa-﻿<pb n="b074"/>
tayopalabhyate । tataḥ kiṃ ? tadgatameva prāmāṇyamanumātuṃ śakyate na
śabdagatam । upalabdhasya hi kāraṇasya śaktyanumānaṃ kāryataḥ nānupa-
labdhasya । nanu ca smaraṇameva nopapadyata iti kāraṇāntarānumānaṃ; kasya ?
kāryasya । maivaṃ vocaḥ, na smaraṇaṃ kāraṇamityuktam । smaraṇasya tarhi
kāraṇāntarānumānam । kimāyātaṃ kāryasya ? । na hyanyakāraṇamanyasya
﻿<pb n="b075"/>
bhavitumarhati । nanu ca praṇāḍyā bhaviṣyati । kāraṇatastarhi kāryaṃ vijñeyaṃ
na kāryataḥ kāraṇaṃ; kāryaṃ hi kāraṇamātraparyavasāyi na tatastatpraṇāḍīmapekṣate ।
kāraṇaniṣpattirhi kāryotpattau hetuḥ na tanniṣpādakamapi । asamba-
ndhasya cānumāne'vyavasthā prāpnoti । nanu ca niyatakāraṇakāraṇakaṃ hi
﻿<pb n="b076"/>
yatkāryaṃ tat kāraṇakāraṇamapyavagamayati; naivaṃ, tāvadeva hi tatra
kāraṇam । kimevaṃ smṛteḥ śabdakāraṇakāraṇataivāsmin kārye ?
omityucyate, siddhaṃ tarhi caityavandanādīnāmapi prāmāṇyam ।
﻿<pb n="b077"/>
na, anabhyupagamāditi cet, na tarhi kāryato viśiṣṭakāraṇānu-
mānaṃ, tasmāt pramāṇāntaraṃ mṛgyam । na ca tadastītyuktam ।
tadidaṃ vandhyāsutasmaraṇavadakāraṇaṃ na tatsmaraṇaṃ karaṇībhavitumarhati ।
﻿<pb n="b078"/>
tasmāt duṣṭakāraṇataivātra sthitā । tasmādaprāmāṇyaṃ codanāyāḥ ।</p>
<p>aho anavasitanayanītijño bhavān । kimiti ? kāryata&mdash;
stāvat smaraṇe śaktirasti । smaraṇamidānīmakāraṇamityakāraṇatā
smaraṇe'dhyavasīyate । na ca tadakāraṇatvaṃ smaraṇe'dhyavasātuṃ śakyate
saṃbhavādvedasaṃyogasya, kāraṇāntarasya cāsaṃbhavāt asmin kārye ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b079"/>
﻿<pb n="b080"/>
caityavandanādiṣvasaṃbhavāt na punarasmadīyaṃ kāryato'numānam । tasmāda-
tantramanupalabdhirgranthaviṣayā । vismaraṇopapatteśca pratipat‍tuḥ । tasmā-
davyāhatamanapekṣatvaṃ codanāyāḥ । yatpunaridamuk‍taṃ <quote>‘yāṃ janāḥ
pratinandanti’</quote> ityaṣṭakāliṅgā mantrā iti । tadanupapannaṃ; kutaḥ,
tadekavākyatayaivāprāmāṇyamuktam । kathaṃ tadeva prāmāṇyahetutayopanyasyate ।
﻿<pb n="b081"/>
naivedaṃ prāmāṇyahetutayopanyastam, vedasaṃyogasya tu saṃbhave liṅgam । kathaṃ
kṛtvā talliṅgaṃ ? talliṅgāpekṣaṃ devatābhidhānaṃ karmaṇi । tasmānmāntravarṇikīṃ
devatāṃ anuvadan vedasaṃyogamupodvalayati । yatpunaridamuk‍taṃ ye dṛṣṭārthāste
tata eveti, asadidamuktaṃ; kimatrāsaduktam ? bāḍhamatiśayenāsaduktam ।
adhyayanavidheḥ pramāṇāntarāpekṣitok‍tā bhavati । svarūpe vā kena vāritama-﻿<pb n="b082"/>
vaghātāderiva dṛṣṭārthatvam । kathaṃ tarhi uparitane'dhikaraṇe dṛṣṭārthatvāda-
prāmāṇyam ? tatraiva viśeṣaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>virodhe tvanapekṣaṃ syādasati hyanumānam ।</q> yadi saṃbhavati veda-
saṃprayoge'pratihataṃ kāryānumānaṃ smṛtāviti prāmāṇyaṃ vedasyāprāmāṇyamapi
﻿<pb n="b083"/>
anayaiva yuk‍tyā prasak‍tam । kathaṃ ? virodhāt । virodho'pi ca
smṛtyā saha veda upalabhyate । virodhe cāprāmāṇyaṃ parasparavyāghātāt ।
yathā audumbaryāḥ sarvaveṣṭanaṃ sparśanena । satyamevaṃ yadyanyataḥ kāryānumāna-
vighāto na syāt । kuto'nyataḥ ? viruddhādeva vaidikādvacasaḥ,
﻿<pb n="b084"/>
sākṣādvedapratipādite hyarthe na tadvirodhi sāpekṣaṃ puṃvacaḥ prabhāṇaṃ bhavitumarhati ।
pramāṇāntarānavacchinne pramāṇaṃ pramāṇaṃ bhavati na punaḥ tadavacchinnepi । siddha-
sādhyavyavasthāyā hi bādhaṃ naiyāyikā manyante । na siddhaṃ sādhyena bādhyate
siddhena hi sādhyaṃ bādhyate । siddhaścāyaṃ vaidiko'rthaḥ pratyakṣāvagamyakāraṇatvāt na
viruddhakāraṇaviṣayamanumānamātmānaṃ labhate agnāviva śaityānumānam ।
﻿<pb n="b085"/>
tasmānna virodhe prāmāṇyaṃ smṛteḥ । aprāmāṇyāccāvirodhaḥ । avirodhāccāvighātaḥ ।
avyāghātāccāvihataṃ prāmāṇyaṃ codanāyāḥ । nanu ca kāryārthatve śabdasya
ko virodhaḥ ? kāryadvayaṃ hi pratīyamānaṃ ekārthamapi vikalpenānuṣṭhīyamānaṃ
﻿<pb n="b086"/>
na parasparaṃ vyāhantumutsahate । satattvaṃ hi vastunaḥ siddhasya viruddhamavagamyamānaṃ
parasparavyāghātaṃ saṃvidaḥ upajanayati । kāryaṃ punarekatayā pratipat‍tuṃ na śakyate
anubandhādibhirbhedenaivāvagamāt । bhinnānubandhaṃ ca na svarūpe virodhamāvahati
ekakāryatvāc‍ca yugapadanuṣṭhānavirodhamātraṃ, nirjñātasvarūpasya hi karmaṇo'nu-
ṣṭhānaṃ, anuṣṭhānavirīdhaśca vikalpenaiva parihṛtaḥ prasaṅgāt kāryasiddheḥ । tasmā-
dvirodha evātra nāsti kāryārthatvācchabdasya । kimidamaprāmāṇyamāśaṅkayate
nirākriyate ca ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b087"/>
<p>satyaṃ bhavedetadevaṃ yadyanuṣṭhānavirodhe kāryavirodho na syāt । nanūk‍taṃ
vṛhadrathantarādiṣu anuṣṭhānavirodhe satyapi kāryavirodho na jāyata iti ।
anabhijño bhavān vaikalpikānāṃ padārthānāṃ; anuṣṭhānameva hi kāryamityucyate ।
tadvirodhe kāryavirodho nāstīti pralāpaḥ ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ tarhi punaḥ punaranuṣṭhānaṃ bahubhiśca । tathaivāvagamāt kāryasya ।
vyāghātastarhi vrīhibhiryajeta yavairyajeteti । bāḍham, kathaṃ tarhi prāmāṇyaṃ ?
uk‍tamanapekṣatvāditi । kimanapekṣatā vyāghāte [prāmāṇye] kariṣyati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b088"/>
vyāghāto hi parasparaviparyayamāpādayati viparyayaśca mūrdhābhiṣik‍tamaprāmāṇye ।
satyamevam । iha tu viparyaya evātmānaṃ na labhate ubhayoranapekṣatvāt । na
tarhi vyāghātaḥ । kathaṃ na vyāghātaḥ ? ekatvādanuṣṭhānasyaikaśabdāt । kimidaṃ
mahendrajālopamam ? idamidaṃ ekatvācchāstrasya ; tataśca virodhāvagatestathaiva ।
﻿<pb n="b089"/>
tatsmṛtistu na tathā । kutaḥ aprasiddherekatāyāḥ । ānumānikaṃ hi tatra
kāraṇaṃ anugate ca pratyarthini nānumānamātmānaṃ labhate ityuk‍tam ।
tasmāditaretarāśrayatātra vyāhatā siddhe neti vaiṣamyam । tasmāt smṛti-
﻿<pb n="b090"/>
mukhamaprāmoṇyaṃ niṣiddhaṃ codanāyāḥ pramāṇāntaropalabhyamānakāraṇatayā'numāna-
pratiṣedhaḥ । taduk‍tam&mdash;</p>
<p><q>hetudarśanācca</q> iti । adhikaraṇāntaraṃ veti ko'rthaḥ ?
ayamarthaḥ । pūrvayuk‍tinirapekṣaṃ yuk‍tyabhidhānam । yuktyantarāpekṣiṇī yuk‍tiḥ
pūrvamuk‍tā । iha punaḥ nirapekṣatayā'bhidhīyamānā'dhikaraṇāntaramityucyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b091"/>
kathaṃ punaḥ yuk‍tyantaranirapekṣaṃ kāryānumānavirodhe hetudarśanaṃ ? hetu&mdash;
darśanādeva । na hi dṛṣṭe hetau hetvantarānumānaṃ kramate । dṛṣṭo'tra
lobha eva hetuḥ । tasmāt dṛṣṭe hetau na vaidikānumānaṃ viruddhama-
viruddhaṃ vā bhavati । asati vedānumāne dṛṣṭakāraṇānāṃ vaidikaprayoga-
grāhyatvaṃ kimasti । astu; kka tarhi aprāmāṇ‍yābhidhānamupayujyate ।
﻿<pb n="b092"/>
adṛṣṭopakāriṇo na gṛhyante dṛṣṭārthāstu gṛhyanta iti viṣayabhedaḥ tasmāda-
dṛṣṭārtham । dṛṣṭakāraṇamapramāṇamiti yuk‍tamaprāmāṇyābhidhānam । taduk‍taṃ
vaisarjanahomīyasya vāsaso dṛṣṭārthaṃ dānam ।</p>
<p><q>śiṣṭākope'viruddhamiti cet ।</q> virodhāvirodhaparihāreṇa sthitaṃ
prāmāṇyaṃ codanāyāḥ । sa evāyaṃ virodhaḥ kvāsti kva nāstīti
﻿<pb n="b093"/>
cintyate hānopādānārtham । viṣayavyāptidarśanaṃ kimarthaṃ ? nyāyasvarūpābhidhā-
na paraṃ hyetacchāstraṃ na lakṣyaniṣṭham । satyam yathā bhavānāha । nyāyasvarūpā-
bhidhānamevedaṃ viṣayavyāptyā pradarśyate, svarūpe'bhihitepi nyāyasya kasmiṃ-
ścidviṣaye'sadiva pratibhāti kāryadhiyām । ataḥ tadapanuttaye kṛtadhībhirayaṃ
yat‍naḥ kṛtaḥ । yathā'sminnevodāharaṇe kramakālavirodhaṃ manvānasya﻿<pb n="b094"/>
viruddhamācamanādi pratibhāti । kathaṃ ? yathāśrutasyārthasya vidhivitāna-
vaśādanuṣṭhānamiti sthitaṃ kramalakṣaṇe । pratyakṣavidhivitānavirodhāt
virodhaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b095"/>
<p>atrocyate śāstrārthavirodhe virodhaḥ । śāstraṃ ca kāryārthaṃ na
vidhivitānārthāmit‍yuk‍taṃ dvitīye sūtre । kāryameva vitataṃ pratīyate nityaṃ
kāryaparatantratvāt vitānasya, na svātantryeṇa prameyatā kāryasya ca
kāryāntareṇa virodhaḥ, na padārthavaitatyena tad‍guṇatvāt । kāle kathaṃ ?
kālo'pi hi pracayaḥ kāryāṇām । atastadapekṣatvāt na viruddhayate
<quote>“api ca prāptānāṃ padārthānāmuttarakālaṃ krama āpatati yadā padārthāḥ
prāp‍nuvanti tadā krama eva nāsti”</quote>। kimanenānabhihitamabhihitam ? sa
eva hi guṇabhāvaḥ kamasya pratipāditaḥ। sa cok‍tatvānna pratipādanīyaḥ ।﻿<pb n="b096"/>
<p>astyatrābhiprāyaḥ&mdash;na ca vitānapracayāveva kramakālāviti
manyate । kathaṃ ? paurṇamāsyāṃ paurṇamāsyā yajeta kaḥ pracayo'tra karmaṇāṃ ?
dvitīyādiṣbapi tulyatvāt na tatpracayasya paurṇamāsītvaṃ yuk‍tam ।
kāryatayā ca kramāvagatirddaṣṭā&mdash;yathā'dhvaryurgṛhapatiṃ dīkṣayitveti ।
tasmānna guṇatayā parihāra upapadyate । kāryatvāt kāryatayā ca
virodha iti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b097"/>
<p>tadidaṃ parihriyate&mdash;kiṃ prāpte dīkṣākārye dīkṣāvitānamavagamyate
adhvaryurgṛhapatimityetasmin vāk‍ye uta tatprāptinirapekṣa evāyaṃ svatantraḥ
kāryatayā'vagamyate samidādivat । na hi kāryamantareṇa kāryavita-
tiravagamyate kāryasya cedvitatiḥ na kāryāntaratayā śakyate'vagantum ।
tasmādanavagate kārye vitānasyānavagamāt kena virodhaḥ ? kastarhi
adhvaryurgṛhapatimityasya viṣayaḥ ? svāvasare vakṣyāmaḥ । kālepi cāyameva
parihāraḥ । katha ? paurṇamāsīśabdavācyaṃ kimabhipretamāyuṣ‍mataḥ tatrāpi kriyā-
pracitireva saṃyogavibhāgajā grahāṇām । iyāṃstu viśeṣaḥ coditakāryapraciti-
﻿<pb n="b098"/>
rekatrāṅgam । kiyāntarapracitiranyatra । tatra kriyāntarapracityā
tāvadavirodhaḥ । coditakāryapracitistu kāryoṃttarakālabhāvinī । tasmāt
kramavadavirodhaḥ ।</p>
<p><q><quote>“na cācamanādayo</q> vyavadhānaṃ kurvanti”</quote> iti pratipadārthāṅgābhi-
prāyam । sāṅgasyaiva hi padārthasya padārthāntareṇa kramāvagatiḥ । tasmādācama-
nādyanvitā eva vaidikāḥ prayogāḥ pratipattavyā iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b099"/>
<p><q>teṣ‍vadarśanādvirodhasya samā vipratipattiḥ syāt ।</q> śabdārtha-
vipratipattau satyāṃ kimaprāmāṇyaṃ vedasya syāt । saṃśayādapratipatteḥ ।
nanu ca sandigdheṣu vāk‍yaśeṣādityud‍dhṛtamidamaprāmāṇ‍yam । satyamud‍dhṛtam ।
yatrānekārthatayaiva sarvatra nimittabhāvaḥ prasiddhaḥ yathā'kṣādiṣu । yatra
punaḥ vipratipattyaiva kvacit kasyacinnimittatvaṃ na tatra prayogātsaṃśayo
﻿<pb n="b100"/>
bhavati । prayogasya ca saṃśayaṃ vāk‍yaśeṣo vyāvartayati । nābhidhāne
saṃśayam । abhidhāne cāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ । abhidhānasaṃśayaśca vyavahāra&mdash;
vipratipattyā । śabdārthavyavahāramūlaṃ ca vedārthajñānamityuk‍tam । tena
vyavahāravadvedārthepi prāptā vipratipattiḥ । na cātra vedārthasya virodhāt śak‍yate
nirākartum asau vipratipattiḥ । ubhayathopapattervāk‍yārthasya । tasmāt
nimittavipratipattyā'nadhyavasāyaḥ । anadhyavasāyāccāprāmāṇyam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b101"/>
<p><q>śāstrasthā vā tannimittatvāt ।</q> satyaṃ yadyavirodhaḥ syāt ।
api tu kāryata eva virodho'vagamyata eva । śrūyate hi varāhaṃ gāvo'
nudhāvantītyevamodiṣu vākyaśeṣeṣu । tataḥ kiṃ ? viśiṣṭanimittakānva-
yo'vagamyate । nanu tadevedamāpatitaṃ vākyaśeṣānnirṇaya iti । naivedamā-
patitam sandigdhe hi nimitte tatra nirṇayaḥ । atra punarviparyaya eva
nirākriyate varāhādyevautpattikaṃ na kṛṣṇaśakunādīti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b102"/>
<p>nanu ca vedādeva nimittāvagamo'bhyupagato bhavati । na
laukikādvayavahārāta yūpādīnāmiva । evaṃ sati ko doṣaḥ ? na khalu
kaścidanyo doṣaḥ । tadeva hi vaidikanimittatvaṃ na siddhayati ।
kutaḥ ? apratipanne laukikanimittabhāve na vedāt pratipat‍tuṃ
śakyate । ata eva vaidikatvaṃ na brūmaḥ kiṃ tarhi śiṣṭaprayoga
eva valavānityucyate vākyaśeṣānuguṇyāt । siddhe cāsyautpatti-
katve prayāgasyānyato naiva tadvirodhinī pratipattirātmānaṃ labhate । autpattika-
﻿<pb n="b103"/>
tayā gauṇenāpi vyavahāropapatteḥ । yadi hi vyavahārādeva dvayorautpattikatva-
kalpanā syāt tatretaretarāśrayāt kalpanāvyāghātaḥ । atra tvanyataḥ śāstrīyasya
prayogasya siddhamautpattikatvamityuk‍tam । siddhe ca tasmin pratipakṣa-
vyāghāto'vagamyate । anumānavirodhāt । tasmādgauṇo nārthavyavahāraḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b104"/>
<p><q>coditantu pratīyetāvirodhāt pramāṇena ।</q> yadyevamanāryavyavahāraḥ
gauṇaḥ । evaṃ tarhi ye śabdāḥ āryavyavahāre nimittatayā na prasiddho
teṣāmanimittataiva vaidike vyavahāre yathā pikanemasatatāmarasādīnām ।
mābhūditi cet tadevedamaprāmāṇyaṃ prāpnoti । nigamaniruk‍tavyākaraṇādi-
vaśādbhavatvarthāvagatiriti cet, na; tayoḥ prayogamūlatvāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b105"/>
kathaṃ tarhi prakṛtipratyayārthohanaṃ ? viniyogavaśāt । viniyuk‍tasya
mantrasya vākyaśeṣībhūtasya cārthavādasya vṛddhavyavahāraprasiddhanimittānuvarti
prakṛtipratyayohanaṃ na punarūhyapadanimittaṃ vidhyuddeśavākyaṃ bhavitumarhati ।
tasmādaprāmāṇyaṃ codanāyāḥ ।</p>
<p>satyaṃ yadi sāmānyato dṛṣṭaṃ kāryānumānavirodhi syāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b106"/>
atha tu yatraiva pratyarthī vidyate tatraiva kāryānumonavirodhaḥ tadā vihatapratipakṣaṃ
kena vāryate । kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ sāmānyato dṛṣṭaṃ na bhavatīti sāmānyameva
tanna syāt apratipakṣasiddhau । tasmādapratipakṣamlecchavyavahārasiddhamapi
nimittameva vedārthāvagatau । ato virodhāvirodhanirastapratipakṣaṃ sthitamana&mdash;
pekṣatvaṃ codanāyāḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b107"/>
<p><q>prayogaśāstramiti cet ।</q> kiṃ punaḥ karaṇaṃ siddhasya pauruṣe-
yatayā'napekṣatvamāśaṅkayate । kāryataḥ pramāṇataścāśaṅkayate kāryaṃ
paṭhitasya pāṭhaḥ śākhāntaravat, pramāṇaṃ punaḥ ācāryavacaḥ pramāṇamiti ।
nanu vipratiṣiddhamidaṃ pauruṣeyatvamanapekṣatvaṃ ceti । kimatra vipratiṣiddham ?
yathā'vagamyante'rthāstathā bhavanti । dvayaṃ cātrāvagamyate pauruṣeyatvamanapekṣatvaṃ;
smaraṇāt pauruṣeyatvaṃ, kāryavacanābhyāmanapekṣatvam । tasmād‍dvayamastu ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b108"/>
<p><q>na, asanniyamāt ।</q> naitadupapadyate pauruṣeyatvamanapekṣatvaṃ ceti ।
siddhaṃ cāsya pauruṣeyatvam । na kāṭhakādivat pravacanaparihāryam ।
kṛtiśca pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭārthābhidhānamevocyate na varṇādikāryatā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b109"/>
tasmātsāpekṣatvam । yatpunaḥ kāryamupanyastaṃ paṭhitasya pāṭhaḥ śākhāntaravaditi,
naitacchākhāntaratulyaṃ; prayogābhyāsaḥ kāryagamyasyāvagamyate svaravidhyarthavīda-
parityāgāt । tadānantaryapratipattau padārthānāmavyavadhānamāvahati ।
﻿<pb n="b110"/>
avyavahitāśca pratīyamānāḥ sukhamanuṣṭhīyanta iti paṭhitasya pāṭhaprayojana-
mācāryāṇām । ata eva prayogaśāstramiti vyapadiśyate, kalpaśabdā-
bhidheyatā; kalpanā hyatra padārthānāṃ na vidheyatvam । avagatasya klṛpti-
rbhavati maṇeriva । yaduk‍tamācāryavacaḥ pramāṇamiti pramāṇādavagamyata
iti tanna । apramāṇatvādasya vacanasya । na hi svarūpe śabda-
﻿<pb n="b111"/>
syānapekṣatvamastītyuk‍taṃ kintu kārye । tasmādanyaśeṣatvādasya vākyasya
dṛṣṭānusārivyākhyānaṃ yuk‍tam । vedo vā''cāryo'bhipretaḥ ।</p>
<p>yadvā ācāryavacaḥ pramāṇam tadvadapekṣya । kiṃ punaḥ prayojanaṃ
cintaṣyāḥ ? vihitakalpanāparatvādasya śāstrasya na virodhamavagacchāmaḥ ।
astyatra vihitavirodhinī kalpanā sarvāsu tithiṣu darśapūrṇamāsādīnāṃ
kalpanā । sā ca kālaviśeṣaśravaṇādvirudhyate viruddhaṃ cānapekṣyam ।
anyathā hyādare tena vyāghātādaprāmāṇyaṃ codanāyāḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b112"/>
<p><b>anumānavyavasthānāttatsaṃyuk‍taṃ pramāṇaṃ syāt ।</b> iha vyavasthita-
viṣayamavyavasthitaṃ codāharaṇam । kimidaṃ vyavasthitaviṣayamavyavasthitaṃ
ceti ? idamidaṃ prācyodīcyadākṣiṇātyābhimāninaḥ kurvate । holākādīnā-
meveyaṃ vyavasthā । na cābhimānasya niyāmakaṃ kiñcidastītyavyavasthā ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b113"/>
<p><q>kathaṃ punarniyāmakaṃ nāsti ?</q> vidhistāvanna niyāmakaḥ niyoga-
mātraparyavasāyī hi saḥ । karmaśabdo'pi holākādirna niyāmakaḥ karma-
viśeṣābhidhānāta । na cānyatkiñcit guṇo jātiḥ saṃsthānaṃ deśo vā tada-
bhāvāt । samākhyapi naiva । nanu yo yatra jātaḥ sa tena deśena samākhyāyate
prācyedīcyadākṣiṇātyā iti । na janmamātrātsamākhyeyaṃ āgatādiṣvapi
﻿<pb n="b114"/>
tulyatvāt na niyāmikā samākhyā । lohitākṣādayastu niyāma&mdash;
katvavyabhicaritāḥ । kiṃ punarasyāścintāyāḥ pramāṇalakṣaṇaupayi-
katvamasti ? kathaṃ vā nāsti; na, yadi niyāmakamasti yadi vā nāsti
kiṃ jātamanapekṣatvasya । idameva jātam । abhimāno vidyate । na ca
tasya mūlamupalabhyata ityaprāmāṇyaṃ pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b115"/>
<p>rāddhānte tu nābhimānaprabhavaṃ vacanamiti parihṛtam । yadyabhimāna-
prabhavaṃ vaidikaṃ vacanaṃ tadā bhavedaprāmāṇyaṃ codanāyāḥ abhimānasya ca
mūlaṃ nāstīti bhavatvasāvayathārthobhimānaḥ na punarayathārthatvaṃ codanāyāḥ śakyate
vak‍tum ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b116"/>
﻿<pb n="b117"/>
<p><q>prayogotpattyaśāstratvāt śabdeṣu na vyavasthā syāt ।</q> kathaṃ puna-
rvyākaraṇāsmṛternirmūlatve sati <q>vedasyāprāmāṇyamāśaṅkayate ? yadi</q> gāvyādī-
nāmapyanādisattā syāt kiṃ jātaṃ <q>codanāyāḥ; ucyate; aśvagoṇyādīnāṃ</q>
niyatārthatvaṃ smaranti vedavidaḥ niyatārthatayā <q>ca vidavyākhyānamapi</q> kurvate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b118"/>
yadi ca vyākaraṇaṃ pramāṇaṃ tadidamupapannaṃ syāt । nirmūlatve hi niyatārthatā
niṣpramāṇikā syāt । bhavatu kā no bādhā । aniyatanimittako vedārthaḥ
prāpnoti । tataścānadhyavasāyādaprāmāṇyam । na ca śāstrasthanyāyo'tra śakyate
﻿<pb n="b119"/>
vak‍tum । tasmādvayākaraṇanibandhana evātrādhyavasāya iti । atastadupapatti-
rvicāraṇīyā । tadidaṃ vicāryate । kiṃ gaurityevamādīnāmanāditvaṃ sās‍nādi-
mati gāvyādīnāṃ cādimatteti । kimiyaṃ smṛtiḥ sambhavanmūlā neti
vicāryate । kiṃ tāvatprāptaṃ ? āstāṃ tāvanmūlacintā śabdānuśāsanaṃ
tāvadaniyatārtham ।</p>
<p>keyamaniyatārthatā ? iyamaniyatārthatā prayoganiyamārthaṃ hīdaṃ
śāstram । na cāsau prayogo niyantuṃ śakyate । atha prayogādeva niyamaḥ
siddhaṃ tarhi gāvyādīnāmapi sās‍nādimatyanāditvam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b120"/>
<p>kathaṃ punaḥ prayogo niyantuṃ na śakyate ? itthaṃ na śakyate
prathamaṃ tāvadidamanuśāsanaṃ, dhātoḥ pare pratyayā bhavantīti । tathā ca keci-
tkartari, kecitkarmaṇi, kecit kartṛvarjiteṣu sarvakārakeṣu ; taccedaṃ
sarvamanupapannam । kathamanupapannaṃ ? evamanupapannaṃ&mdash;dhātorityucyate; ko
nāmāyaṃ dhātuḥ ?</p>
﻿<pb n="b121"/>
<p>nanu bhūvādayo dhātava iti kāṃścicchabdān kayā citparipāṭayā
paṭhitvā <quote>‘dhātava’</quote> iti saṃjñā kṛtā । atastayā saṃjñayā ye saṃjñino
lakṣyante tebhyaḥ pare pratyayā bhavantīti kiṃ nopapadyate ? gaṇḍatītyādīnāmapi
sādhutvaṃ prāpnoti; ghaṭaṃ bhūyata iti ca । sattādīnāmapi tārtīyapratyayaprasaṅgaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b122"/>
anārṣaḥ pāṭha iti cet । bhavatvapyayaṃ parihāraḥ gaṇḍatyādīnāṃ
punaraprayoga eva ।</p>
<p>atha kriyāvacano dhāturityucyate, na, bhavati tiṣṭhatītyādīnā-
maprayogaḥ gaṇḍateścānarthakaḥ pāṭhaḥ । akriyāpi k‍vacit pratīyata iti cet
﻿<pb n="b123"/>
prayogatastarhi niyamaḥ na kriyātaḥ prayogaḥ । kriyāvagatibhātraṃ niyāmakamiti
cet nādhyāropānadhyāropayostulyatāvagatiḥ saṃbhavatītyuk‍tam । tasmādida-
mapi na niyāmakam । pāṭhakriyāvacanābhyāṃ niyama iti cet
﻿<pb n="b124"/>
tatrāpi samuditaṃ vyastamiti vak‍tavyam । samuditapakṣe gaṇḍatibhavatyādīnāṃ
tathaiva vyudāsaḥ । pratyekamiti cet pacatyādīnāṃ pāṭhānarthakyam ।
āgamayatyādīnāṃ nivṛttyarthamiti cet । ubhayaṃ tarhyāśritam । evaṃ
sati bhavatyādiṣu sa eva doṣaḥ । tasmāt punarapi prayoga eva śaraṇam ।
﻿<pb n="b125"/>
tathā kārakaniyamāsiddhiḥ । dhruvamapāye'pādānamiti dhruvatayā'podānamuk‍tam ।
dhruvasya kārakatvameva nopapadyate, meṣānmeṣo'pasarpati iti kārakam ।
meṣāditi kasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ kārakametat । yasya hi yasyāṃ kriyāyāṃ
vyāpāro vidyate sa tasyāṃ kārakam । na ca dhruvasya vyāpāra upalabhyate ।</p>
<p>athāyamabhiprāyaḥ sārthāddhīnaḥ rathāt patitaḥ iti sārtharathayoḥ
kriyopalabhyata iti; nāsti kriyā sārthasya rathasya ca । api tu gamanarūpo
na ca kiyāntare vyāpṛtaṃ kriyāntare kārakaṃ bhavati । na ca gameḥ
﻿<pb n="b126"/>
kartā pacatītyasyāvasīyate । tasmānniṣkriyaṃ kārakamiti vadato vyāpṛtodanyat
sarvaṃ sarvatra kārakaṃ syāt । pacatītyatra paṭhati dhāvati bhuṅkate ityeva
mādyapādānaṃ syāt । evaṃ pacatyādiṣu kartā paṭhatyādyapādānaṃ syāt ।</p>
<p>ayamaparaḥ kārakaniyamaḥ । karmaṇā yamamipraiti sa saṃpradānamiti
karmaṇā cedabhipreyate na kārakam । kartrā hi karmaṇā yo'bhipreyate
sa sampradānamityudāharaṇādvidmaḥ upādhyāyāya gāṃ dadāti iti । kartṛvyā-
pārānunippādi vyāpāraṃ ca kārakam । yaḥ punarabhipreyate na tasyābhiprayaṇe
vyāpāraḥ tena tam iti karmakaraṇanirdeśāt phalaṃ karma bhavati na kārakaṃ
yajeriva svargaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b127"/>
<p>nanu ca <quote>‘karmaṇā yamabhipraiti’</quote> iti kārakaṃ karma parigṛhyate;
sutarāmakārakatvam; na hi kārakasaṃbandhitayā kārakavyapadeśo bhavati,
karotīti kārakaśabdavyutpādanāt । tasmānna śakyate śāstrataḥ kārakaniyamme
'vagantum । kriyāsaṃbandhitayā ca [kārakatve] viśeṣānuśāsanaṃ na siddhayati ।
ṣaṣṭhī ca sarvakārakāṇāṃ prāpnoti svargasya ca yāgakārakatvaprasaṅgaḥ prayā-
jādīnāṃ ca darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ । prayogapratipattibhyāṃ niyama iti cenna tarhi
śāstrataḥ । yadapi sādhakatamaṃ karaṇamityucyate kiṃ tat sādhakatamamiti ?</p>
﻿<pb n="b128"/>
yasya vyāpārānantaraṃ kriyāniṣpattiriti, prāptaṃ tarhi taṇḍulairodana&mdash;
miti । athānyena hetunā sādhakatamatvaṃ; tadvak‍tavyam; prācuryāditi cet,
yasya hi āphalaniṣpatteḥ punaḥ punaḥ vyāpāraḥ । kasya vā nāstīti । āste
pak‍tā sthālyādisabhārasaṃbhṛtaḥ sajjaḥ । prasak‍taṃ tarhi kāṣṭhaiḥ pacatīti
sthālyāmudakeneti । bhavatvevamiti cet, na tarhi kāṣṭhaiḥ sthālyāmodanaṃ
pacatīti prayoganiyamaḥ । prayogāditi cet namaḥ śāstrāya ।</p>
<p>ādhāro'dhikaraṇamiti cānuśāsanam । kasyādhāratvaṃ ? yatrādhīyate
sa ādhāra iti । yadi tāvat kriyā sarvakārakāṇāmadhikaraṇatvaprasaṅgaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b129"/>
atha yatra karma tadadhikaraṇāmiti cet, same pacatīti na prāpnoti apsu
pacatīti prāpnotīti । kaṭe bhuṅkate iti cāpabhraṃśaḥ । karturhi tadadhikaraṇaṃ
na kriyāyāḥ, nāpi karmaṇaḥ । sarvakārakavyavasthānaṃ yatreti cet sthālyā-
modanaṃ pacatīti na prāpnoti । adhikaraṇasya vā kārakatvaprasaṅgaḥ । na
hyadhikaraṇaṃ adhikaraṇavyavasthitamiti śakyate vak‍tum । saṃbandhitayā
sarvakārakādhikaraṇatā vā'dhikaraṇatve heturuk‍taḥ nirvyāpāratvaṃ ca kālādi-
ṣūk‍tam । yadapyucyate karturīpsitatamaṃ karmeti, ko'yamātiśāyanikaḥ sarvaṃ
﻿<pb n="b130"/>
kriyārthamīpsitatamam । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;yadarthā kriyā tat tamapā'bhi-
dhīyate । prāptamakārakatvam । uk‍taṃ hi saṃpradānasūtre । tathā yuk‍taṃ cānī-
psitam iti । kathaṃ yuk‍taṃ ? tamabartheneti cet, na tarhyanīpsitamiti
śakyate vak‍tuṃ anyasyātiśayino'nupādānāt । tasmādandhapadamevedam ।</p>
<p>akacitaṃ ca kathitameva । tasmāt prayogādeva sarvamupapādanīyaṃ
na śāstrādityavagacchāmaḥ । tathā svatatraḥ karteti kimidaṃ svātantryam ?
yadīcchātaḥ pravṛttiḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b131"/>
<p>jāyate mriyate kūlaṃ patatītyakartṛtā prāpnoti । tataścāsādhutā-
prasaṅgaḥ śabdasya ।</p>
<p>atha tadvayāpārādhīnaṃ kārakāntaraṃ manyase keyaṃ tadadhīnatā yasmin
sati yo niṣpadyate tat tadadhīnaṃ; prāptaṃ tarhi sarvakārakāṇaṃ kartṛtvamitareta-
rādhīnatvāt । na kenacidvinā kasyacit niṣpattimupalabhāmahe । yasya
hi yena vinā vyāpāraniṣpattiḥ na tena tadapekṣate; parasparāpekṣaśca kārakagrāmaḥ
tasmānna niyamaḥ ।</p>
<p>dhātūpāttavyāpāraḥ karteti cet । na vidmaḥ kasya dhātūpātta
iti sarveṣāṃ saṃbandhitayā'vagamāt । tathā ca prayogadarśanaṃ kāṣṭhāni
﻿<pb n="b132"/>
pacantīti । yasya vivakṣita iti ceta; vivakṣāyāḥ kāraṇaṃ vak‍tavyam । prayoga
iti cet ; pramāṇaṃ tarhi śāstraṃ ; tasmānnirmūleyaṃ śāstraniyamātkarturava-
cchittiḥ । tatprayojako hetuśceti prayojyenaiva vyākhyātam । ye cāpyarthopapado-
pādhayaḥ te'pi kriyāviśeṣeṇa vā'rthaviśeṣeṇa vā niyāmakāḥ । tadyathā
rucyarthānāṃ prīyamāṇa iti saṃpradāne । bhītrārthānāṃ bhayaheturityapādāne । atrāpi
na vidmaḥ kimarthamapekṣate saṃpradānaniyamāya uta rucyarthoccāraṇamiti । kiñcātaḥ
﻿<pb n="b133"/>
yadi rucyarthoccāraṇaṃ devadattāya modakā dīyantāmiti na prāpnoti । kimiti
rucyarthā hi te rucinimittatvāt । nanu ca rucyartho dhātvarthaḥ parigṛhyate
kimasau nirviṣaya eva ? na nirviṣayaḥ yadyasmai rocate tadviṣayo rucyarthaḥ ।
avagatastarhi, modakābhidhānāt dhātūccāraṇaṃ nibandhanamiti cet devadattāya
modakāḥ kiṃ rocanta iti praśnottarānupapattiḥ । tadapekṣayaiva prayuk‍tiriti cet
na, praśnottarānupapatteḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b134"/>
<p>praśnanirākaraṇārthametaduccāraṇaṃ na caturthīprayogasya sādhutvāya । tathā
apādāne'pi bhayahetutvaṃ bhīteḥ kārakamātrasyāpādānatāmāpādayati, sarvakāra-
kavyāpārādhīnatvādbhīteḥ । upapadādiṣu tu kārakataiva nāsti । anayaiva
diśā vibhak‍tividhānamapi pratyuk‍tam । viṣayanirūpaṇapūrvakatvāt vibhak‍ti-
vidhānasya । evaṃ vākyārthāvagamapūrvakasya niyamasya na vākyārthau-
payikatvaṃ tatsiddhestadavagamāt । evaṃ kṛtpratyayā api vyākhyā-
tāḥ । tiṅpratyayā api kālād‍yupādhayo na tadvacanāḥ ।
apratītaiśca niyamanirūpaṇamaśakyam । kena cok‍taṃ kālādayo
﻿<pb n="b135"/>
nocyanta iti ? uk‍taṃ bhagavatā bhāṣyakāreṇa bhūte dhātvartha iti ।
na ca dhātvarthenaiva dhātvarthanirūpaṇaṃ śakyam । tathā liṅādayo'pi
vidhyādyarthānirūpaṇāt ।</p>
<p>kathaṃ punarvidhyāderanirūpaṇaṃ ? upapadārthavaśatvādbhedasya । na
svato bhedaḥ śakyate'vagantum । abhinnasvārthānāṃ ca niyamo durvacaḥ
aśvagoṇyādīnāmiva; tathā taddhitasamāsau samarthavacanā[ta] durnirūpau ।
kimidaṃ samarthavacanāditi ? samarthānāṃ prathamādvā samarthaḥ padavidhiḥ iti
cānuśāsanam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b136"/>
<p>ekārthānvayitā ca sāmarthyam । tallakṣaṇatvārthaṃ ca
samāsaviśeṣābhidhānaṃ taddhitaviśeṣābhidhānaṃ ca । tena ca tau lakṣyete iti
itaretarāśrayaṃ taddhitaviśeṣavidhānam । tathā asamarthasamāsopasaṅkhayānaṃ samarthācca
taddhitānutpattiḥ na prayogāt ṛte śakyate'vagantum । tataścet kṛtaṃ śās‍treṇa ।
asamarthānāṃ tāvatsamāso aśrāddhabhojī dadhighaṭo goratha iti । samarthāccānu-
tpattistaddhitasya aṅgulyā khanati vṛkṣamūlādāgata iti । tasmāt prayoga-
śaraṇaṃ śīs‍traṃ na prayoganiyamāyālam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b137"/>
<p>tathā <quote>‘arthavadadhāturapratyayaḥ prātipadikam’</quote> ityatrāpi kiṃ kāryamartha&mdash;
vattvaṃ utautpattikamiti vak‍tavyam । ko vā viśeṣaḥ ? yadi kāryamarthavattvaṃ
<quote>‘siddhe śabdārthasaṃbandhe’</quote> iti na ghaṭate । athautpattikaṃ tatkathanopāyatvācchāstrasya
na śās‍traupayikatvaṃ setsyati । upāyatvenedaṃ śās‍traṃ upeyamūlaṃ cetītareta-
rāśrayam । evaṃ ca tannibandhanaṃ svarakāryapratyayavidhānaṃ ca na siddhayati ।
adhāturapratyaya iti cāvayavātirekaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b138"/>
<p>kimanena nivartyate ? dhātorarthavattvepi pratyayasya ca prātipadikasaṃjñā
mā bhūt ityevamarthamuk‍tam । yadi prātisvikamarthavattvamāśritya
adhāturapratyaya ityuk‍tam vākyasya tarhi prātipadikasaṃjñā prāpnoti ।
samāsagrahaṇaṃ tannivṛttyarthamiti cet; adhāturapratyaya ityanarthakam ।
tasyāpi samāsagrahaṇānnivṛttiḥ । ekārthatve sati nivartakaṃ nārthāntare
﻿<pb n="b139"/>
iti cet; tadayuk‍tam, samāsasyāpyarthāntarābhyupagamāt vāvacanānarthakyena ।
atha arthavatsamudāyanirākaraṇatayā samāsagrahaṇam; kṛttaddhitagrahaṇaṃ tarhi na
kartavyam । tatrāpi kṛdantāstaddhitāntāśceti samudāya eveṣyate । tasmāt
prayogasya tāvadabhyupāyatā durghaṭā । dughaṭena copāyena dūrāpetamupeyajñānam ।
﻿<pb n="b140"/>
uk‍tānuk‍taduruktanirūpaṇaṃ ca vyākhyātdṛṇāṃ lakṣaṇe prayogata eva
pratipattavyam । chandasi viśeṣābhidhānaṃ ca tadarthājñānānnopapadyate ।
tat jñānapūrvakamiti cet, anarthakaṃ tarhi; vedārthajñānāya hi aṅgāni
prayujyante । nāṅgajñānāya vedārthaḥ tasya kāryārthatvāt । ataḥ śabdasya
śāsaṃna anuśāsanameva । tathā ca prātiśākhyādīnāṃ praṇetṛbhiḥ paraspara-
viruddhārthapradarśanena prakaṭīkṛta eva śāstrādaniyamaḥ । yadapīdamaparaṃ
﻿<pb n="b141"/>
aprayogānna bhavati iti vyākhyātṛvacanaṃ, taddarśayati mūlāparijñānaṃ sūtra-
praṇetdṛṇām । aparijñātamūlasya tasya vacanānmūlaniyamo niyama
eva । ākṛtigaṇābhidhānaṃ ca śāstrato niyamasya mātṛkā । bahulagrahaṇaṃ ca
śāstrato'niyamasya ḍiṇḍimaḥ । evamasyāḥ smṛteranāditvamabhyupagacchadbhiḥ
abhyupagatamajñatvam । tasmādanirṇītanimittādvedārthajñānamiti vadadbhiḥ
sanmārgānusārī loko vyāmohitaḥ । yadvā śraddhāvijṛbhitamārjavāt । tadida-
muk‍taṃ <quote>‘prayogotpattyaśāstratvāt śabdeṣu na vyavasthā syāt’</quote> iti ।
nanu ceyamanupapattiḥ pāṇinīyasyoktā । anyasmānniyamaṃ vidmaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b142"/>
na । anyasyāpyayamevopadeśopāyaḥ । śabde prayatnaniṣpatteraparādhasya bhāgitvaṃ
āstāṃ tāvadupadeśopāyaḥ idameva tāvadvicāryate kimādimattayāpi śabdasya
vyavahāraḥ siddhayati neti । kimiti na siddhayati ? evaṃ na siddhayati ।
vṛddhavyavahāraparaṃparayā śabdārthavyavahārasiddhiḥ avicchinnā ca setyuk‍tam ।
avicchede ca kaḥ khalvavasaro'pabhraṃśasya । yaji paraṃ svavyavahārasiddhayarthaṃ kasya

﻿<pb n="b143"/>
cit saṃjñā paribhāṣā vā kṛtā, tatra ca kartṛsmaraṇaṃ yathā'sminneva
vyākaraṇe । na ca gāvyādīnāṃ ghaṭādīnāmiva saṃbandhasya kartā smaryate ।
tasmāta ādimattāyā avasara eva nāsti । satyaṃ yadyavasaro na;
asti tvasau, dṛśyate hi bālānāmanyaśabdoccāraṇecchāyāmapi śabdāntaro-
ccāraṇam । yathā kartecchāyāṃ katteti viṣṇurviṇṇuriti । satyam ।
bālānāṃ anyathoccāraṇamupalabhyate । tat‍tu tadvayavahārāvadhikameva । yatpunaḥ
﻿<pb n="b144"/>
smaryamāṇaprabhavaṃ tadapyaśak‍tijamityaśak‍tijamevābhidhānam । atrocyate
&mdash;satyaṃ yadyasak‍tijadarśanādaśak‍tijatvaṃ gāvyāderbrūmaḥ । vayaṃ tu
punaḥ smṛtita upalabhya smṛtermūlosaṃbhabamaśak‍tijadarśanenok‍tavantaḥ । nanu ca
tadevedamuk‍taṃ; na, tathocyamānamanumānaṃ bhavati । tatra ca viruddhādera-﻿<pb n="b145"/>
vasaraḥ । atra punaḥ smṛtermūlābhāvo na śakyate vak‍tuṃ ityetāvatā aśak‍ti-
jadarśanam । saṃbhavamātranirasanaścābhāvo nāśak‍tijadarśanamapekṣate । ato'bhi-
yuk‍tasmaraṇamanyatheti na śakyate vak‍tum । evaṃ tarhi smaraṇamevedaṃ na
niyamāyālaṃ bhavatītyuk‍tam; niyamāyālaṃ bhavati । kathaṃ punarna bhavatīti
jñātam ? tata eva pūrvok‍tavyāpakāvyāpakavyākhyānāt tadvayākhyānaṃ
kathaṃcitsamāhitaṃ vyākhyātṛbhiḥ । yathā samāhitaṃ kathaṃcit tathaiva
parigṛhyatām । tadapi hi smaraṇameva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b146"/>
<p>evaṃ kṛtvā sadṛśānāṃ śabdānāmekasminnarthe śak‍tibhedo na
kalpitaḥ । dṛśyate hi adyatvepyetacchabdasya śabdāntarasmaraṇa-
vyavahitamarthāvagamahetutvam yathā adritunna[ṅga]miti । ata eva
vibhak‍tivyatyayaṃ śabdavido'bhyupagacchanti । aśmakairāyāta ityuk‍te
aśmakebhya iti pratipadyate । tasmādanenāpi prakāreṇākṣep‍tuṃ na śakyate
prāmāṇyaṃ codanāyāḥ ।</p>
<p><q>prayogacodanābhāvādarthaikatvam ।</q> kiṃ ya eva
﻿<pb n="b147"/>
laukikāḥ śabdāḥ ta eva vaidikāḥ, kiṃ ta eva caiṣāmarthāḥ ityasyāḥ
cintāyāḥ prayojanam । nanu cākṛtyadhikaraṇasyāyamupod‍ghātaḥ । katha-
mupod‍ghātaḥ ? yadi ta eva śabdāḥ ta evārthāḥ tadā vyak‍tyābhidhāna-
mukhena śakyate prāmāṇyākṣepaḥ kartuṃ; yadi tvanya eva śabdā arthāścānya&mdash;
tvādevāprāmāṇyaṃ kiṃ vyaktyabhidhānamukhenāprāmāṇyopanyāsena ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b148"/>
<p>ata idamuk‍taṃ&mdash;<q>idaṃ tāvatparīkṣyamiti ।</q> kathamanyatvāśaṅkā;
vyapadeśabhedāt ; laukikānāṃ vaidikānāṃ cetyabhiyuk‍tā vyapadiśanti ।
kṛtaṇatvamagniśabdaṃ paṭhanti । tathā devāsaḥ tmametyevamādeśca darśanāt । tathā
arthānyatvamapi vedādeva pratibhāti । uttānā vai devagavā vahanti, hiraṇya-
parṇoḥ vanaspatiḥ । ghṛtaṃ madhviti ca । nanu caivaṃ vedārthāvagamo nopapadyate
laukikaśabdārthapūrvakatvādvedārthasya । sa eva mābhūdityākṣiptam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b149"/>
<p>apratipādakastarhi vedaḥ ? omityucyate na prayojanānuvarti
pramāṇaṃ bhavitumarhati । evaṃ tarhi pramāṇādeva prayojanamavagacchāmaḥ ।
kiṃ tatpramāṇaṃ ? śabdārthayorananyatvāvagatiḥ । bhedo hi svarūpataḥ kāryato
vā syāt svarūpaṃ tāvat tadeva varṇātmakaṃ gavādīnāṃ ; kāryamapi tadeva
sāsnādimatpratipattihetutvam । kenānyatvamavagacchāmaḥ ? nanu ca ṇatvādibhiḥ,
﻿<pb n="b150"/>
varṇānyatvaṃ hi tat na padānyatvaṃ, arthapratipattihetutvaṃ, tasya
caikatvam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b151"/>
<p>nanu cārthānyatvāt padānyatvaṃ; arthānyatvameva hyasiddham ।
uttānā vahantītyasyārthasyāsiddheḥ । na cāyamartho'rthānyatve
uttānaśabdāt pratipat‍tuṃ śakyate । tasmāt dvayābhāvāt siddha-
mekatvam । kathaṃ tarhi uttānā vai devagavā vahantīti ? । uk‍taṃ﻿<pb n="b152"/>
stutyarthatvena prāmāṇyaṃ guṇavādena vyakhyātam । kathaṃ tarhi
vyapadeśaḥ ? anuśāsanaviṣayānyatvāsiddhayarthaḥ । sāpekṣānapekṣatvena
viṣayabhedaḥ siddhayati ।</p>
<p><q>prayogacodanā ।</q> uktaṃ tad‍bhūtānāṃ kriyārthatvena samāmnāya iti
tadidānīṃ vicāryate । kimidaṃ bhūtānāmiti na vidmaḥ kimākṛtau bhūtānāṃ
uta vyak‍tāviti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b153"/>
<p>nanu yadyasmāt pratīyate sa tad‍bhūtaḥ । ubhayaṃ cāsmāt
pratīyate । kathaṃ tarhi sāmānyena pratyayāt vyak‍tau ca
kriyāsaṃbhavāditi । kiṃ cātra nopapadyate ? idaṃ cātra nopapadyate vyak‍tau
ca kriyāsaṃbhavāditi । kriyāsaṃbhavo hi vyak‍tau tad‍bhūtatve heturuk‍taḥ ।
vyak‍tau kimanenāvagamo nirastaḥ ? omityucyate; ākṛtāvavagamā-
bhidhānāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b154"/>
<p>agranthajño hi devānāṃ priyaḥ । kā'trāgranthajñatā ?
iyamatrāgranthajñatā । kriyārthena samāmnāya ityuk‍tam । kiyārthatayā ca
tad‍bhūtatvaṃ nirūpitam । nāpratītaṃ kiyārthaṃ bhavatīti vyak‍tāveva
tad‍bhūtatvam । sāmānyāvagatistarhi kathaṃ, astītyetāvacchakyate vak‍tum ।
na punaḥ kriyārthatayā tad‍bhūtatvam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b155"/>
<p>nanu ca sāmānyāvagatau satyāṃ vyaktyavagamo na prāpnoti । aho
batānubhavepyanavamarśaḥ ! kasya sāmānyasyāvagamaḥ ? sambandhitayā hyana-
vagamyamānaṃ sāmānyaṃ sāmānyamiti nāvagamyate । sambandhyantarasāpekṣā hi
sambandhini buddhirbhavati । viśeṣataścātra rūparūpitayā nāvagamyate । na
hi rūpiśūnyā rūpabuddhirasti । yadi syāt rūpataiva na syāt । kimiti
﻿<pb n="b156"/>
tarhi bhedenopanyāsaḥ ? kriyārthena rūpasyānanvayapradarśanārtham । na
cānanvitasya śabdārthatvaṃ yuk‍tam pañjarasyeva siṃhamānayeti pañjarasthā-
vagatau । kimiti tarhyupanyāsaḥ ? amumevārthaṃ pradarśayituma ।
kimartham ? ananvitanimittatayā aprāmāṇyābhidhānaṃ ākṛti-
vādinaḥ । vyak‍teścānvayamicchanti vrīhin prokṣatītyevamādiṣu ।
﻿<pb n="b157"/>
vyak‍titad‍bhūtapakṣe vā kimanapekṣatvaṃ siddhayati ? । śiddhayatu mā vā
apanyāyāśrayaṇaṃ tāvajjātivādinaḥ । vyaktipakṣe tu kāryānurūpā karaṇakalpanā
nyāyyā । nanu ca kathamayaṃ nyāyyaḥ pakṣaḥ yasmāt vṛddhavyavahāraparaṃparā
na vyutpattau kāraṇatāṃ pratipattuṃ śak‍noti । kathaṃ na śak‍noti ?
anvayavyatirekāśrayo hi vṛddhavyavahāraḥ । anvayavyatirekau ca sāmānya-
nibandhanau । na ca vṛddhavyavahārādanyadvayutpattau kāraṇamupalabhomahe ।
karturasmaraṇādityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b158"/>
<p>nanu cākṛtāvapi tad‍bhūtatvaṃ nirastam । āmnāyasya kriyārtha-
tvāditi । kiṃ punaranayorbalīyaḥ ? kāryamiti brūmaḥ । taddhi kalpanābījaṃ
kāraṇacakrasya, vṛddhavyavahārādi saha tad‍bhūtatayā kāraṇaṃ kāryataścā-
sannataraṃ tadbhūtatvamavagamyate tadanurūpā ca vyutpattiḥ kalpanīyā । sā
cenna vṛddhavyavahārapūrvikā saṃbhavati kalpyatāṃ vā samayaḥ kṛtakatvaṃ vā vyā-
moho vā । nanu ca vṛddhavyavahārādevāvagatirdṛṣṭā bālānāṃ; na hi dṛṣṭe'nupapannaṃ
nāmeti । upapannā tarhi ! satyaṃ jarśanata upapannā, nimittatastu nopapadyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b159"/>
na ca samayaḥ kṛtakatvaṃ vopalabhyate । tasmānnimittakalpanā nayānnirasteva
lakṣyate ।</p>
<p>yadi punaḥ sāmānyopalakṣitaṃ vyaktidravyameva nimittatāmāpadyate vākyārtha-
pratipattau tataḥ ko doṣaḥ ? naiva kāścit na khalu kaściddoṣaḥ, upalakṣaṇatve
tu pramāṇaṃ vak‍tavyam । kāryapratipattiraivātra pramāṇam । na hi vyak‍tāva-
pratipannāyāṃ kāryapratipattirghaṭate । na hi sāmānyenānupalakṣito vyaktiviśeṣaḥ
śakyate pratipādayitumiti sarvamupapannam । ato vyaktyabhidhānaṃ manyate
vyāḍiriti pradarśitam । ata eva saṅkhayādīnāṃ viniyojyopādeyatvamupapannaṃ
﻿<pb n="b160"/>
bhavati । na hyanāśrito guṇānvayabhāgbhavati । anyatvavyapadeśaśca
na jātipakṣe upapadyate । ato vyaktinimittataiva ca tad‍bhūtateti
draṣṭavyam ।</p>
<p><q>ākṛtistu kriyārthatvāt ।</q> atrocyate । siddhayatyapi
kadācidarya pakṣaḥ kāryāvagatireva hyanaikāntikī, śyenacitaṃ
﻿<pb n="b161"/>
cinvīteti nātra vyaktivacanatā[tad‍bhūtatā]śakyate vak‍tum । na hyatra
vyaktigataṃ kāryaṃ pratīyate । kimiti na pratīyate ? nāyaṃ vākyārthaḥ
śyenaiścitaṃ śyenacitamiti । karmaṇyagnyākhyāyāmiti smaraṇāt ।
abhidhānasmaraṇaṃ ca yathārthamityuktam । ataḥ śyenaśabdo'yaṃ citau vartate ।
tasmāt dravyāntarasādhyāyāṃ citau śyenaśabdaḥ upamārthe vṛttaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b162"/>
na hi vyaktisādṛśyamupapādayituṃ śakyate । tasmāt sāmānyānvayo
dṛśyate na vyak‍teḥ । anghayinaśca padārthā ityuktam । tasmānnopalakṣaṇa-
tayaiva sāmānyasyānvayo'vagamyate । kintu kāryataḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b163"/>
kiñcopamānopasarjanārthānāmapyanvayitvamasti । bāḍhamasti pratipattau,
na kārye । kiṃ kāryānanvayino'pi anvayitā bhavati ? uk‍tamarthavādānāṃ
mantrapadānāṃ ca । ākṛteḥ tarhi kimiti neṣyate ? vrīhīn prokṣatīti
kāryapratipattāvanaṅgatvāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b164"/>
<p>nanu copalakṣaṇatve nāṅgaṃ bhavati; nopalakṣaṇamaṅgaṃ vāsova&mdash;
dviśeṣāvagatau । tasmātkvacidvayak‍tiranvayinī kvacitsāmānyamiti na
vidmaḥ ka tad‍bhūtatvaṃ nyāyyamiti । tasmādanavadhṛta[ti]nimittaṃ punara-
prāmāṇyaṃ prasaktam । atrocyate&mdash;na tad‍bhūtatayā vyak‍teranvayo'vasī-
yate । yadi hyanvayinī vyaktistadā vyaktimātrānvayaḥ ekasyā vā vyak‍teḥ
﻿<pb n="b165"/>
na cobhayaṃ pratīyate । anutsṛṣṭasāmānyapratyayo hi sarvatrānvaya upalabhyate ।
nanu copalakṣaṇatayā sāmānyapratyayo'stītyuktam । tadeva tu nāvagamyate ।
upalakṣaṇaṃ hi nāma nātmākāratayopalakṣyamupalakṣayati yathā yatrāyaṃ kākaḥ
ado devadattasya gṛgamiti, na kākākāraṃ gṛhamavasīyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b166"/>
<p>yadapi cok‍tam yena pañjarasthaḥ siṃho dṛṣṭaḥ tasya siṃhāvagamādeva
pañjarāvagamaḥ, tadbalādākṛteḥ vyaktyavagamādevāvagama iti । tadapyayuktam ।
kutaḥ ? siṃhākārādākārāntaratayā pañjaramavagacchanti, naivaṃ gāmānayetyākārāntara-
mavagamyate । tasmādapratīyamānākārāntaratayā vyaktiranveti iti duśśakaṃ-
vak‍tum । nanu ca kāryārthatvādanvayasya ākāramātrasya ca tadanupapatteḥ
vyaktipurassaraiva sāmānyāvagatiḥ nimittānusāreṇa; satyaṃ yathāha
﻿<pb n="b167"/>
pitṛmān । tathāpyākārāvagatiparyantaivānvayāvagatiḥ । athākāraḥ pañjarasthānīyaḥ
kalpyaḥ, tato vyaktimātrānvayaḥ ekavyaktyanvayo vā syāt । bhavatu kā
no bādhā । anadhyavasāyī śabdaḥ syāt । kena cok‍taṃ neti ? anadhya-
vasāye hi kathamākṛterananvayaḥ śakyate vak‍tum । yathā gāmānayetyaśvasya,
﻿<pb n="b168"/>
na punaranadhyavasitānvaye, yathā aktāḥ śarkarā iti ghṛtasya ।
tasmādupalakṣaṇapakṣastāvadasambaddhaḥ । athedamucyeta svābhāvikī śabdaśaktiḥ ।
kāryataścānvayaḥ । vyaktisthaṃ ca kāryam । na ca vyaktimātraṃ viśeṣo
vā'vasīyate । gotvasambaddha meva dravyaṃ pratīyate । pratipannaṃ tarhi gotva-
sambaddhā vyaktayaḥ pratīyanta iti । maivaṃ vocaḥ । kāryāvasāyī hyanvayaḥ na
punaḥ pratipattimātraparyavasāyī । yathā daṇḍinamānayeti na daṇḍasyānayanama-
﻿<pb n="b169"/>
vasīyate vidyate ca pratītiḥ evaṃ gavāderapi । avivekajño bhavān uk‍taṃ
vivekaṃ na gṛhītavānasi । kimuk‍tam ? idamuk‍tam । yatrākārāntara-
vivekaḥ tatrākārāntaramupalakṣaṇam । yathā daṇḍītyeva daṇḍiviśeṣāvagatau
nānayane daṇḍasyānvayaḥ । yatra punaḥ daṇḍitayaivāvagagyate na viśeṣataḥ
﻿<pb n="b170"/>
tatra tathābhūtasyaivānvayaḥ śakyate vak‍tum । viśeṣāvagatau tu daṇḍiśabdo
na daṇḍe vartate । aviśeṣāvagatau vā kiṃ daṇḍiśabdo daṇḍe
vartate ? satyam । na nimittato vartate । arthāntarasahitasyaiva
nimittatvasiddhervyavahārāt । na punaḥ kāryato vivekāvagatiḥ । gavādīnāṃ
punaḥ nimittabhedānavagamāt sambandhiṣu nimittatayā bhedo na ghaṭate kiṃ
punaḥ kāryataḥ । kathaṃ tarhi vrīhīn prokṣatīti viśeṣāvagatiḥ
na cennimittato bhedaḥ ? kāryato viśeṣāvagatiḥ kāryaṃ hi
﻿<pb n="b171"/>
prayojane paryavasyati tadvati vā tadvatsu vrīhiṣu । kathaṃ punaḥ tadvanto
vrīhayaḥ pratīyante ? prakaraṇāt । tasmānna samo'yamupanyāso daṇḍivaditi ।
ato'nanvite sāmānye kāryasyaivāparyavasānaṃ; na ca sambhavati paryavasāne'-
paryavasānaṃ śakyate vak‍tum । nanu ca kāryaviṣayatvādaparyavasānamuktam ।
satyamuk‍tam yadyasambhavaḥ kāryasya । yathāsambhavaṃ hi kāryaviṣayatvaṃ na vikāra-
vattayaiva karaṇādīnāmiva । nanu ca teṣāmapi svavyāpāre vikāro vidyata
﻿<pb n="b172"/>
eva । gotvāderapi tulyam । tadapi hi vyāpārasiddhau vyāpṛtameva ।
nanu ca na kiñcit prāgvyāpāraṃ nirvṛttyuttarakālaṃ ca karaṇādīnāmiva
vikāramupalabhāmahe sāmānye । na vikāritā vyāpārasiddhau hetuḥ । kintu
sati tasmin bhāvaḥ । na ca sāmānyāvagamaśūnyā niyogārthanirvṛttiri-
tyuk‍tam । yathāpratīyamānasyaivārthasya nirvṛttiḥ pratīyamānajñānā&mdash;
dupapadyate । tasmādupapannaḥ sāmānyasya kāryānvayaḥ । anyatvābhidheyatvaṃ tu
﻿<pb n="b173"/>
upādānataḥ siddhayati । tasmāṃt sāmānyapurassaraivānvayāvagatiḥ । uddeśye tu
kāryata upalakṣaṇatvaṃ nātad‍bhūtatayā । ataḥ siddhaṃ yathāvagamyamānārthabhūtaiḥ
tad‍bhūtairiti । etaccok‍tameva sāmānyākāreṇa śabdāt pratītiriti ।
atrākṛtigrahaṇamupalakṣaṇatayopanyastam । anākṛtāvapi nāgṛhītaviśeṣaṇā
viśiṣṭe buddhiriti । <quote>“atha vyaktyantarepi prayujyate na tarhi vyaktiḥ padārtha”</quote><note n="(1)"> p. 162.</note>
﻿<pb n="b174"/>
iti ko'bhiprāyaḥ । ayamabhiprāyaḥ । na hyekaṃ dharmamanāśritya vastvantare
jñātasambandhasya vastvantarasaṃbandhitā śakyate'vagantum । na cāsaṃbandhinaḥ
prayogaḥ । prayujyate cedāśritaṃ tarhi vyatiriktaṃ kiñcit । vyak‍terasā-
dhāraṇataiva rūpaṃ sarvasāmānyaviśeṣaviyuktā hi vyaktiriti darśitam ।
﻿<pb n="b175"/>
<note n="(1)"> p. 162.</note><quote>“naiṣa doṣaḥ”</quote> iti sarvasāmānyā tviyaṃ viyuktiriti । evaṃ tarhi
viyuktirvācyatayok‍tā na vyak‍tiḥ tadidaṃ sāmānyamevāpatitam । <quote>“netyu-
cyate yo'rthaḥ sāmānyaviśeṣāṇāṃ cāśrayaḥ sā vyaktiriti”</quote>। kasyedamuttaraṃ
dīyate ? । viyuktimātraṃ sāmānyamāpādayataḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ tasyedamuttaraṃ ? na
kiñcidupalakṣaṇatvena sāmānyaṃviśeṣaṃ vā gṛhṇāti āśrayamātrābhidhānaṃ śabdasya ।
﻿<pb n="b176"/>
nanu cāśrayamātratāpi sāmānyaṃ; netyucyate; sāmānyaṃ hi ākā&mdash;
rāntaravatāmekarūpatā । āśrayo nāma na cāśrayibhyaḥ ākārāntaram ।
tasmādananyatvāvagateḥ prayogaḥ siddhayatītyabhiprāyaḥ । yadyevaṃ prayoge
tarhi virodhaḥ । nahyaśvavyak‍tau gośabdaprayogo dṛśyate, prāpnoti ca
yuṣmatkalpanāyām । nanu cādarśanaṃ bhavataivoktam । evaṃ tarhi prayogadarśanaṃ
﻿<pb n="b177"/>
māśritam । omityucyate । kathaṃ tarhyadyajātāyāṃ gavi prathama&mdash;
prayogaḥ sidhyati ? dṛśyate ca । kiñca vyak‍tāveva prayogaḥ iti pratijñāna-
mātrāmidaṃ, yadi vyaktāveva prayogaḥ syāt vyaktyantaranirapekṣādvayavahārā-
d‏vyutpattiḥ syāt tato vyaktyantare vyutpattyantaraṃ prāpnoti । tadbhede ca iyaṃ
vā gauḥ iyaṃ vā gauḥityuk‍taṃ syāt । yathā ayaṃ vā akṣo' iti ।
na punaḥ ekavyutpattinibandhanaṃ <quote>‘iyaṃ gauḥ iyamapi gauḥ iyamapi’</quote> iti syāt ।
tasmānna vyaktyabhidhānapakṣaḥ sambhavati vyutpattyantarānavagamāt ।
﻿<pb n="b178"/>
ubhayaṃ tarhi bhavatu guṇapradhānabhāvastu kāryato nirṇeyaḥ । tathā ca pradhānapakṣe
laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ veti sandihyate । upādānapakṣe punaḥ sāmānyameva ।
tadidamuktaṃ ubhayaṃ bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ iti । nāyamapi pakṣaḥ saṃbhavati ।
kāryato hyupādānalakṣaṇatvaṃ na punaḥ pratipattitaḥ । pratipattiśca sāmānya-
nibandhanā । kutaḥ ? anvayavyātirekābhyāṃ, vrīhīn prokṣati
iti vyak‍tiniṣṭhe'pi prayoge sāmānyākāratayaiva hyabhidhānamabhidhatte ।
﻿<pb n="b179"/>
vyak‍tito'vasīyata iti cenna । vyaktyantaragatatvenānavagateḥ । sāmānya-
niṣṭhe punaḥ prayoge ekākāratayaiva dravyamavasīyata ityuk‍tam । tadi-
damāha&mdash;<q>mānasādapacārāditi ।</q> tasmānnānadhyavasāyaḥ sāmānyapratyayā-
dadhyavasāyyeva śābdam ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ prathamādhyāyasya
tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b180"/>
<head>bṛhatī</head>
<head>prathamādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><q>uktaṃ samāmnāyaidamarthya tasmātyarvaṃ tadarthaṃ syāt ।</q> nanu cedaṃ
pramāṇalakṣaṇaṃ; vakṣyati ca dvitīyādau&mdash;uk‍taṃ pramāṇalakṣaṇamiti;
kimidamupanyastaṃ kimudbhidādayo guṇavidhayaḥ āhosvit karmanāma-
dheyānīti । kiṃ vā pramāṇalakṣaṇe'yamupanyāso na ghaṭate ? bāḍham, sthite
prāmāṇye'rthaviśeṣāvadhāraṇacintopapadyate । aprāmāṇye panaḥ arthābhāvāt
﻿<pb n="b181"/> 
keyaṃ viśeṣacintā । uk‍taṃ samāmnāyaidamarthyamiti ca yat
guṇavidhānopapattitayā vyākhyātaṃ tadapi nopapadyate । na hi mantrārtha&mdash;
vādatvāsaṃbhavo guṇavidhitve hetuḥ । kiṃ tarhi ? kriyāprāptirguṇa-
vidhānatve hetuḥ । tathā ca svayamuditam&mdash;avihite karmaṇi guṇa-
vidhānamanarthakamiti । yadi ca mantrārthavādatvāsambhavo guṇavidhitve hetuḥ
svargakāmo yajetetyapi guṇavidhiḥ syāt ।</p>﻿<pb n="b182"/> 
<p>yadap‍yuktam&mdash;prakṛtau jyotiṣṭome guṇavidhānamarthavadbhavip‍yati
iti । tadap‍yayuk‍taṃ, tatrāpi guṇapadaṃ śrūyata eva jyotiṣṭomeneti । atha
tatra viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ bhaviṣ‍yatītyabhiprāyaḥ iha kasmānna bhavatīti । athai-
kasmin siddhe karmaṇi itarattatraiva guṇavidhānamiti, iha siddhe tada‍guṇavidhānaṃ﻿<pb n="b183"/> 
kimiti na bhavati । na ca niyame hetuṃ paś‍yāmaḥ । viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ ca
viśiṣṭakarmotpattau pratīyate । na hi viśiṣṭa utpanne karmaṇi guṇāntara&mdash;
vidhānaṃ yuktam; <quote>“guṇaścāpūrvasaṃyoge vāk‍yayoḥ samatvāt”</quote> iti nyāyā-
bhidhānāt । tasmānna lakṣaṇāntargatatvaṃ nāpi nyāyābhidhānam । atrocyate
&mdash;pramāṇalakṣaṇamevedam । nanu pramāṇalakṣaṇe'rthaviśeṣāvadhāraṇacintā
nopapadyata ityuktam । naivedamarthaviśeṣāvadhāraṇamupanyastam । kiṃ tarhi,
karmavidhānamatra sambhavati uta guṇavidhānamātrameveti । guṇavidhai ca
saṃbhavati na karmavidhānaṃ nyāy‍yam guṇaparatvādvāk‍yasya rak‍tapaṭavat ।﻿<pb n="b184"/> 
tasmāt karmavidhānāsambhavāt aprāmāṇ‍yam । guṇavidhipakṣe kathaṃ ? laukika-
karmāśrayaṇāt । avaś‍yaṃ hi guṇavidhipare vāk‍ye laukikaṃ karmāśrayaṇīyam ।
vaidike vā ko doṣaḥ ? na khalu kaścit । kintu asambhavaḥ vaidikasya ।
kathamasambhavaḥ ? sarvatropapadaśruteḥ । evamapi kimityaprāmāṇyaṃ, dhātvarthe'nyataḥ
pravṛttirmṛg‍yā । anyataścet sāpekṣatvaprasaṅgaḥ sāpekṣatvāccāprāmāṇ‍yaṃ prasak‍tam ।
yadi punaḥ stryupagamādiṣ‍viva niyamavidhānānnirapekṣatvaṃ tadā kathamaprāmāṇyaṃ
syāt ? syādetadevaṃ yadi sarvatra puruṣārthā eva vidhayaḥ syuḥ । karmārthā api﻿<pb n="b185"/>
vaidike vā[ko] doṣaḥ ? na khalu kaścit । kintu asaṃbhavaḥ vaidikasya ।
kathamasambhavaḥ ? sarvatropapadaśruteḥ । evamapi kimityaprāmāṇ‍yaṃ ? dhātvarthā-
nyataḥ pravṛttirmṛg‍yā, anyataścet sāpekṣatvaprasaṅgaḥ । sāpekṣatvāccāprāmāṇ‍yaṃ
prasaktam । yadi punarabhyupagamādiṣviva niyamavidhānānnirapekṣatvaṃ kathama&mdash;
prāmāṇ‍yaṃ syāt । syādetadevaṃ yadi sarvatra puruṣārthā eva vidhayaḥ syuḥ
karmārthā api tu kecit vidhayaḥ pratīyante । na tatra niyamaḥ sambhavati ।
kiṃ ca svargakāmo yajeta iti kiṃ niyamyate ? nanu ca kartā, yathaitatkartṛ-
viśeṣaṇaṃ na ghaṭate tathā pradarśitamekādaśe । phalasya tvavidheyatvādeva
niyamāsambhavaḥ । phale karma niyamyata iti cet; uk‍tama-
vidheyatvaṃ karmaṇāṃ padārthāntaraparatvādvāk‍yānā, tasmātpramāṇāntaraṃ mṛg‍yaṃ
andhapratibhā veti pratipattavyam । guṇavat‍karmavidhānaṃ kimiti
na daṇ‍ḍinamānayeti । anavagamāt । na hyatra tṛtīyādi-
bhirmat‍varthaḥ bhavati yathā pratipādyate । mat‍vantānāmeva hi so'rthaḥ ।﻿<pb n="b186"/>
 lakṣaṇayā parigṛhyata iti cet । prāptaṃ tarhi sāpekṣatvan । na śrutito hi
lakṣaṇā śak‍yā'vagantum । tasmāt pramāṇāntarameyatā ।</p>
<p>yaduk‍taṃ&mdash;uk‍taṃ samāmnāyaidamarthyaṃ tasmāt sarvaṃ tadarthaṃ syāt
iti na guṇavidhau heturiti । bhavati hi nāmanirākaraṇatayā hetuḥ । kathaṃ
punaranena nāma nirākiyate । aidamarthyāsambhavāta । kathamaidamarthyaṃ
na saṃbhavati ? niyogārthatayā vidh‍yuddeśamantrārthavādānāmarthattoktā ।
taccaitat avidheyatvānnāmno na saṃbhavatīti । nanu avidheyānāṃ
hi śrut‍yā vā'rthavattoktā । tacca dvayamasya na saṃbhavati । tasmāt﻿<pb n="b187"/> 
vidheyat‍vam । vidheyaśced‍guṇaḥ । tasmād‍guṇavidhiḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ <quote>‘somena
yajeta’</quote> iti vidh‍yuddeśa udāharaṇaṃ ?। kathaṃ vā na saṃbhavati ? tatrāpi 
yāgasyāvidhānāt । mābhūdyāgasya vidhānaṃ guṇastāvadvidhīyate ।</p>
<p>nanu ca guvidhirapi naiva saṃbhavati nāmatayā prasiddheḥ । vṛddhavyavahāre
hi prasiddhiḥ prasiddhirit‍yucyate । nanu yājñikavyavahāro'pi vṛddhavyavahāra eva ।
na, laukikavyavahārapūrvakatvāt yājñikavyavahārasya na ca loke nāmatayā
prasiddhirudbhidaḥ arthāntarābhidhānatayā prasiddheḥ । tasmād‍guṇavidhiḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b188"/> 
<p><q>evamapi prakṛtau j‍yotiṣṭome guṇavidhānamarthavadbhaviṣ‍yatīti ।</q>
ayuk‍tamevedaṃ bhāṣ‍yaṃ pratibhāti । kimiti ? j‍yotiṣṭomepi j‍yotiṣṭomapadaṃ
vidhāyakameva । tatrāpi yaj‍yartho mṛg‍yaḥ । kena vok‍taṃ neti ?
yadyevaṃ tatra vidhānaṃ nopapadyate guṇavidhiprakṛtitā tatra lakṣitā ।
etaduk‍taṃ bhavati&mdash;somena yajeteti guṇaṃ vidadhatā pratipannā'&mdash;
nyato yāgasiddhiḥ । pratipannā cet tatraivedamap‍yupapannaṃ bhaviṣyati ।﻿<pb n="b189"/>
tasmājjyotiṣṭomaśabdo'bhyupagataprakṛt‍yupalakṣaṇārthaḥ viśiṣṭavidhānāsaṃbhava-
ścoktaḥ । nāmadheyapakṣe punaḥ niyogārthatā na saṃbhavati yajinopāttatvādvidheyasya
samarpitavidheyā nāmatā ca na vidherupakaroti vidh‍yarthaupayikatayā ca
prāmāṇ‍yam । atastvadīyepi pakṣe prāmāṇ‍yaṃ pramāṇāntaramṛg‍yameva ।
as‍madīye punaḥ pakṣe padārtho'pi tāvad‍vṛddhavyavahāraprasiddhaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>api vā nāmadheyam ।</q> atrābhidhīyate&mdash;guṇaparametadvāk‍yamiti
yaduk‍taṃ sat‍yametat viniyoge tu tat । na ca viniyogāpekṣā kartavyā ।﻿<pb n="b190"/>
kiṃ tarhi ? bhāvāpekṣā bhāvaścāyaṃ yajeteti । tasmāttadviṣayo niyogaḥ । na caivaṃ
viśeṣaviṣayo niyogaḥ pramāṇāntarasiddho'sti । <quote>“j‍yotiṣṭomāt‍karmāntaraṃ”</quote>
iti । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati&mdash;siddhaṃ laukikādvaudikaṃ karmāntaramiti । darśayiṣyati
ca <quote>‘tebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyeta’</quote> iti । kathaṃ tarhi guṇārthena punaḥ śrutiriti ?
kartavyatāprāp‍tyabhiprāyaṃ ca tat na viniyogābhiprāyam । kiṃ vā na
yathāviniyogaṃ niyogaḥ । eṣā tāvatprakriyā sūtrakārasya bhāvārthāḥ karma-﻿<pb n="b191"/>
śabdāḥ tebh‍yaḥ kriyā pratīyeteti paṭhataḥ । kimidaṃ yathā
viniyogaṃ niyogapratyarthībhūtaṃ sūtraṃ, ? bāḍham । anyathā hi rak‍paṭanyāyena
ś‍yenādividhānaṃ prāpnoti । nirākṛtaṃ caitat abhāvārthatayā । kiṃ punarasyāḥ
prakriyāyā mūlam ? avagatiriti brūmaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu viniyoge'p‍yavagatireva। kena cok‍taṃ neti ? kin‍tu kartav‍yatā
bhāvaviṣayā avagamyata ityuk‍tamasmābhiḥ kāryasvabhāvatvādbhāvasya । viniyo-
gāvagamaḥ idānīṃ kimarthaḥ ? bhāvārtha iti brūmaḥ । kathaṃ tarhi guṇaparatocyate ?﻿<pb n="b192"/>
prāptau sat‍yāṃ bhāvasya । nanu copapadaśravaṇe sati kevalasya bhāvasya
viṣayataiva nāvagamyate yathā raktaḥ paṭo bhavatīti । na kevalaṃ
paṭabhavanamevāvasīyata iti pradarśitam । kena cok‍taṃ kevalo bhāvo
viṣayatāmāpadyata iti । sa tu viṣayoniyogasyetyuktam । na cāsau
padāntarasaṃbandhaṃ niruṇaddhi rak‍tapaṭavadviśiṣṭa evāvasīyate । kathaṃ puna-﻿<pb n="b193"/>
rudbhidādayo guṇāḥ santo viśeṣaṇatāṃ pratipadyante । kiṃ guṇatayaiva viśeṣaṇa-
viśeṣ‍yabhāvaḥ ? nāmnopi hi dṛśyate ḍit‍tho'yaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ ḍabit‍tho'yaṃ kṣatriya
iti । kathaṃ punaratra nāmatvam ? sāmānādhikaraṇ‍yāvagateḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ
sāmānādhikaraṇ‍yamavasīyate ? tṛtīyānirdeśāt । asti hi yāge
tṛtīyārthaḥ sa tasyānena siddhayatīti kathitaḥ । tṛtīyā codbhidādiṣu
śrūyate । tasmādudbhidā yāgenet‍yavagamyate ।</p>
<p>tadidamayuktam&mdash;na hyekavibhak‍tinibandhanaṃ sāmānādhikaraṇ‍yaṃ;
kiṃ tarhi ? ekārthāvagatinibandhanam yadyekavibhak‍tinibandhanaṃ
﻿<pb n="b194"/>
syāt aruṇayaikahāyanyeti dravyaguṇayoḥ kriyāsaṃbandho na syāt parasparasaṃba-
ndhaniṣṭhataiva syāt nīlotpalavat । ata eva gauraśvaḥ puruṣo hastīti
na sāmānādhikaraṇ‍yamekavibhaktitvepi pratīyate । ekārthatayā cāyaṃ devadatta
iti pratīyate । tasmānna vibhak‍tiḥ kāraṇaṃ sāmānādhikaraṇ‍yasya ।</p>
<p>atrocyate&mdash;uktaṃ bhāvārthatvāt yajyarthe kartavyatā na punarnāmārthe ।
avagamyate ca saṃbandhaḥ । yadi guṇanimittakaḥ parigṛhyate tadā
luptamatup‏pratyayanirdeśaḥ kal‍panīyaḥ । atha tu nāmadheyaṃ tadā﻿<pb n="b195"/>
akal‍pitaśabdāntaranimittakaḥ saṃbandho bhavati । upapadyate cāsau samāna-
vibhaktiyogāt । yattvaruṇayeti pradarśitaṃ tatra bhāvasaṃbandhitā dvayoḥ ।
iha tvarthāntarāśravaṇāt kasya sambandhināṃ tṛtīyā kathayati anyadato bhāvava-
canāt । tasmānnirdeśamātraphalaiveyaṃ tṛtīyā । nanu ca nirdeśamātre
prathamayā bhavitavyam । prātipadikārthāvyatirekānuśāsanaṃ tat; na
padārthāvyatirekasya । tathā ca ḍit‍thena brāhmaṇena bhuk‍tamiti nidarśitam ।</p>
<p>nanu caikārthāvagaterabhāvāt kiṃ vibhaktiḥ kariṣyati ।﻿<pb n="b196"/>
matub‍lopa evātra varam । dvayorvā niyogārthatā । dvayostāvat niyogārthatvaṃ
nāsti kāryaviṣayatvānniyogasyetyuktam । na ca kāryābhidhāyi nāmetyuktam ।
bhavatvavayavayogāt kāryābhidhāyitā nāmnaḥ, satyaṃ, bhavatyarvyatirik‍tapakṣe ।
padārthāntaratayā tu saṃbandhāt kaḥ siddhārthatāmapaharati । siddhārthaścāniyoga-
viṣaya ityuk‍tam । tasmādavayavayogānugateḥ siddhamavyatiriktārthatvaṃ
nāmnaḥ । avyatiriktatvācca parihṛto vidhyasaṃsparśaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b197"/>
<p>nanu ca yāvadevok‍taṃ yajeteti tāvadudbhidā yajeteti syāt ।
syādayaṃ doṣaḥ yadi prayojanānuvarti pramāṇaṃ; pramāṇānuvarti tu
prayojanam । dṛśyate ca vāk‍yāntarārthopayikatvaṃ nāmnām । tasmā&mdash;
tsiddhamanapekṣatvaṃ codanāyāḥ ।</p>
<p><q>yasmin guṇopadeśaḥ pradhānato'bhisaṃbandhaḥ ।</q> uk‍taṃ nāmadheya-
mapi guṇaphalasaṃbandhenārthavadbhaviṣ‍yatīti । tadayuk‍taṃ manvānasya viṣaya&mdash;
viśeṣe kvacida‍‏yuk‍tatā pratipādyate ।</p>﻿<pb n="b198"/>
<p>yathā tāvadayuk‍taṃ tathocyate&mdash;guṇopabandhārthaṃ tāvat pañca-
daśānyājyānīti । phalopabandhārthaṃ citrayā yajeta paśukāma iti ।</p>
<p>tatra pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ&mdash;yuk‍taṃ tāvat udbhidā yejetetyeva&mdash;
mādīnāṃ nāmadheyatvaṃ yajyarthasāmānādhikaraṇyāt । tathā āj‍yādīnāma-
pyājyaiḥ stuvata iti stutyarthasāmānādhikaraṇyāt । yatra punaḥ bhāvārtha-
sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ na pratīyate pañcadaśānyājyānīti tatra nāmāvagatirnāsti﻿<pb n="b199"/>
anugatārthatvepi sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ na pratīyate pañcadaśānyājyānīti tatra
nāmāvagatirnāsti । anugatārthatvepi sāmānādhikaraṇyānnāmatā uk‍tā । na
tadihāsti । tasmānna guṇopabandhena nāmnaḥ śak‍yate'rthavattā vak‍tum ।
yuk‍taṃ tāvat guṇopabandhe । phalopabandhe punaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyasaṃbhavāt
kimiti nārthavattā citrayā yajeta paśukāma iti ।</p>
<p>ucyate&mdash;nārthavattā yajeta paśukāma ityeva siddheḥ । tatra hi
sannidhānādeva yāgaviśeṣo labhyate na nāmataḥ । mā bhūdviśeṣaḥ nāmatā tāvannā﻿<pb n="b200"/>
nirākartaṃ śak‍yate । kena cok‍taṃ nāmatvaṃ nirākriyata iti । prayojanaṃ nāstī-
tyetāvatā''kṣepaḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ guṇavidhānaṃ citrayā yajeta paśukāma iti ।
evaṃ guṇavidhānaṃ-atra nirjñāto yāgaviśeṣaḥ phalāya codyate nirjñāte hi
viśeṣe padāntarāvagatiḥ na viśeṣāyopapadyate । kutaḥ । nirjñātatvādeva । yatra
hi vidheyo'rthaḥ svavāk‍yānvitapadāvagamya eva bhavati tatra tata eva viśeṣā-﻿<pb n="201"/>
vagamaḥ vākyāntaranirjñātastu nātmaparijñānāya svavākye padānvayamapekṣate ।
anapekṣitasya sāmānādhikaraṇyamaśābdam । tasmāccitrāpadaṃ vidheyatayā'va-
gantavyam । yatra tarhi upapadādeva viśeṣāvagatiḥ vihitasyāprakṛtatvāt
bhavatu tatra prayojanam । iha tāvadekāntato nāstītyudāhṛtam । aprakṛtepi
ca naiva nāmadheyatayopakaroti । aprakṛte hi karmāntara(meva ।)taiva ।
tatra ca padadvayārthavidhānaṃ pradarśitam । agnihotraṃ juhoti iti
kuṇḍapāyināmayane । tasmānnotpannasyotpadyamānasya vā phalopabandhe-
nā'rthavattā । tasmāccitrayeti yatropapadyate tatra vidhiḥ kalpanīyaḥ﻿<pb n="202"/>
yajeta paśukāma ityenānākāṅkitatvāt । tasmāt guṇaphalopabandhenārtha-
vadityayuktam ।</p>
<p>atrocyate । naitadayuktam—yatrāparo guṇaścodyate tatra pūrvaprati-
pannakarmanāmadheyataiva pratīyate । na hyakarmaṇi guṇo vidhātuṃ śakyate āśri-
tatvātprayogasyeti nyāyābhidhānāt । sāmānādhikaraṇyācca sthite nāmadheyatve
śaknotyeva nāminaṃ pratipādayitum । tasmādupapannaṃ guṇopabandhenārthavāditi ।
yuktamājyādiṣu; citrayeti tu kathaṃ ? tatra hi prakṛtatvādeva viśeṣāvaga-﻿<pb n="203"/>
mānnārthavattā śakyate vaktum । bāḍhaṃ, śakyate tatrāpi yadi na nāma
syāt notpannasya phale vidhānamupapadyate guṇaśruteḥ vyāghātāt; phalārthamidaṃ
na guṇārthamiti viśeṣānavagamāt । anavagame cānadhyavasāyaḥ । anadhya-
vasāyāccāprāmāṇyam । tannāmatayā parihṛtamiti phalopabandhenārthavaditi
yuktam । <quote>na cāmī yaugikā</quote> iti yaugikatvanirākaraṇaṃ kvopa—
yujyate ? । ayamabhiprāyaḥ—yaugikatve hi prakṛtayāgābhidhānasiddhiḥ
syāt; yathā pācakāya vetanaṃ dehīti sāmānādhikaraṇyābhāvepi
prakṛtapācakābhidhānasiddhiḥ । tasmānna cāmī yaugikā ityuktam ।
jātyabhidhāne tvatra vidheyataiva । vyaktyābhidhānaṃ hi viśeṣā﻿<pb n="204"/>
pekṣaṃ bhavati । na cāyaugiko vyaktyabhidhāyī bhavati । evaṃ citrayeti guṇa-
mātrābhidhānāt jātyabhidhāyibhistulyatā । <quote>citrayā yajeteti ca yāgānuvādo
nirjñātatvānna yāgavidhiḥ</quote> ityanena kiṃ pradarśitam ? anākāṅkṣitatvaṃ citrā-
padasya anākāṅkṣitatve ca sāmānādhikaraṇyābhāvaḥ, tadabhāvānna nāmateti ।
tasmāt phalavidhau na nāmatayopakāritā'vagamyata iti । <quote>guṇaphalakalpanāyāṃ
yajateravivakṣā</quote> iti kimanenāśaṅkitam ? yato guṇaphalasambandhepi naiva
nāmno'rthavattāsti । pratyuta rāddhāntinaitannirākaraṇīyaṃ nāmno'rthavattāṃ vadatā ।
tasmādasambaddhamevedaṃ bhāṣyakhaṇḍalakaṃ manasi viparivartate । atrocyate ।﻿<pb n="205"/>
