<p>guṇaphalakalpanāyāṃ na nāma śakyate nivartayitum । kutaḥ ?
yasmādyajateravivakṣā । avivakṣāyāṃ cānāśrito guṇo na śakyate phalāya
vidhātuṃ ca । anyataḥ pravṛttirhi karmaṇo guṇaphalasambandhasya nimittam ।
na ca ṣaśukāmavidhānādṛte yajyarthasya pravartakamasti । tasmāt
paśukāmasambandhāparityāge citrāpadasya nāmataivāvaśiṣyate । tasmā-
dubhayenānākāṅkṣitatvāt kvacidguṇānurūpo guṇavidhiḥ pratipattavyaḥ ।﻿<pb n="206"/>
guṇavidhikalpanāyapi na lakṣaṇeti<note n="(1)">P. <dn>199</dn></note> ।</q> lakṣaṇāśrayaṇe hi pramā-
ṇāntaraprameyā doṣa uktaḥ । asāvapyatra samānādhikaraṇasambandhā-
bhāvānnāstīti siddho guṇavidhiḥ । ataḥ siddhaṃ guṇaphalopabandhe-
nārthavannāmeti । ucyate । nātra guṇavidhiḥ sambhavati, nāmārthavidhāne
hi siddhasyārthasya kriyānupraveśitayā vidhānaṃ na punaḥ svārthasya kāryatayā
tataḥ kim ? idaṃ tato bhavati । yatrāyaṃ guṇaḥ siddhaḥ san 
karmaupayikatāṃ pratipadyate tatra vidhātavyam । ataḥ paśāvasya vidhānaṃ
tatra ca vidhīyamāne asyāparo guṇo vidhātavyaḥ strītvaṃ; yadi punaḥ﻿<pb n="207"/>
sārasvatyāṃ vidhānaṃ tatrāpi paśukāmasambandho'vagamyamānaḥ tyaktavyo
bhaviṣyati । agnīṣomīyaguṇaprāptiśca sārasvatyāṃ bādhanīyā bhavati ।
ataḥ sarvaprāṇidravyakāṇāṃ yāgānāṃ prakṛtibhūte'gnīṣomīye vidhānamasya
svavākyānvayanirastasya । tatra ca dvayamidamaprāptaṃ punarvidhātavyaṃ bhavati ।
tasmānna guṇavidhiḥ saṃbhavati । ataḥ pratīyamānānvayanimittatā'sya
kalpayituṃ nyāyyā । sā cātra nāmno na saṃbhavatītyuktam । tasmāt
siddhaṃ nāmadheyatvam । phalopabandhenārthavadityetadapi pradarśitam । tathā
pañcadaśānyājyānīti guṇavidhipakṣe guṇadvayavidhānaṃ; tacca na saṃbhavati ।
ata ekamatra lakṣaṇatayā grahītavyam । tacca karmaṇaḥ tasmādvākyāntare﻿<pb n="208"/>
nirjñātasya karmaṇo vācakasyājyaśabdasyaiva lakṣaṇatvamupapadyate । evaṃ paraṃparā-
saṃbandhāvagatirna parityaktā bhavati । pañcadaśānyājyānīti । yadapyuktaṃ
guṇavidhipakṣe nātra lakṣaṇeti । tadapyayuktam । kasmāt ? ājyāni
bhavanti iti yatra ājyāni vidhīyante sa bhavatinā vaktavyaḥ । ato'trā
pyājyavanti bhavantīti saiva lakṣaṇā ।</p>
<p>yattvaprasiddhaṃ karmaṇo nāmadheyatvamukta tata karmaṇo lakṣaṇatvāt siddha-
miti, pravṛttinimittasya ca sarvatra vidyamānatvāt <quote>yadājimīyu</quote> ityeva—
mādeḥ । atha kasmāt na pañcadaśasaṅkhyāviśiṣṭānyājyāni stotreṣu vidhīyanta﻿<pb n="209"/>
iti kimanenānirākṛtamupanyastam ? padadvayārtho'nyatra vidhīyate । kimevaṃ
bhaviṣyati ? anāvṛttirvākyasyetyabhiprāyaḥ । siddhyatyevaṃ yadi
prāgvidhānādanayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ siddhaḥ syāt agnaye pāvakāyetivat ।﻿<pb n="210"/>
na tvasāvasti । tasmādvidhyuddeśanimitta evānayoḥ saṃbandha iti na
padadvayārthasya vidheyatā saṃbhavati ।</p>
<p>atha kasmādagniprajāpatyorivāsaṃbandhayorapi vidhānaṃ na
saṃbhavati ? parasparasambandhāvagamāt । sa ca pramāṇāntarasiddho nāstīti
vidhyuddeśanimittaka eva grahītavyaḥ । tasmāt siddhamidamapi
nāmadheyami[damapīti]ti ।</p>﻿<pb n="211"/>
<p><q>tatprakhyaṃ cānyaśāstram ।</q> kena punarviśeṣeṇātra guṇavidhyā-
śaṅkā matvarthalakṣaṇābhāvāt guṇavidhānenāpi sāmānādhikaraṇyopapaptiḥ । tathā
ca darśitaṃ agnaye hotramasminniti samāso'yaṃ homavacanaḥ । upasarjanārtha-
vidhānenāpi guṇavidhirbhavatyeva yathā hiraṇyastraja ṛtvijo bhavanti' iti ।
yuktaṃ tāvat agnihotraṃ juhotīti । āghāramāghārayatīti tu﻿<pb n="212"/>
kathaṃ ? naivātra sāmānādhikaraṇyena prayojanaṃ, karmavacanataivātra na pratīyata
iti guṇavidhiḥ yatrāghāryaṃ dravyaṃ tatraivedamāghāraṇaṃ vidhīyate ।</p>
<p>nanu cāghāryadravyako yāgaḥ āhavanīyasādhyatvāt prāptāghāraka eva
kimāghāravidhānena; homāghārādāghārāntaramidaṃ dravyasaṃskārārthamityabhiprāyaḥ
karmasādhanamāghāre śabdaṃ manvānasya । ata evopāṃśuyāja iti
pradarśitam । tasmādakarmavacanatayaivāsmin udāharaṇe pūrvapakṣaḥ ।
agnihotre tu karmavacanatvepi guṇavidhiraviruddha ityuktam ।</p>﻿<pb n="213"/>
<p>atrocyate—nātra guṇavidhiḥ saṃbhavati । kutaḥ ? prāptatvāt
guṇānāṃ, ye guṇā vidheyatvenopanyastāḥ te anyata eva prāptāḥ । agnistāvat
yadagnaye ca prajāpataye cetyasmāt । āghāraṇamapi <quote>santatamāghārayati</quote>
<quote>ṛjumāghārayati</quote> ityevamādibhyaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="214"/>
kimidamasambaddhamucyate ? kimidamasaṃbaddhaṃ ? darvihome guṇavidhiruktaḥ ।
na ca darvihoma evaitadvidhānaṃ yadagnaye ca prajāpataye ceti । tatho—
pāṃśuyāje āghāraṇamityuktam । na ca santatādayaḥ upāṃ-﻿<pb n="215"/>
śuyāje guṇavidhayaḥ tadidaṃ viyatpadamiva pratibhāti ।</p>
<p>atra vadāmaḥ । guṇavidhipakṣe darvihoma evaitadvidhānaṃ upāṃśuyāje
ca gatam । na tarhi tatprakhyatā rāddhāntahetuḥ । bāḍhaṃ rāddhāntahetuḥ
kathaṃ ? tatprakhyatāpi hi darvihoma eva viṣayāntarāpekṣitvāt ।﻿<pb n="216"/>
'agnihotra juhoti' itivat । evaṃ santatamāghārayatītyupāṃśuyāja eva
prayojanavaddravyāpekṣitvāt āghāramāghārayatītivat । nāmatāpi hi tarhi
teṣāmevopāṃśuyājasya ca । aprāptijño devānāṃ priyaḥ । anyato guṇavidhāna-
siddheḥ । nāmnaścāvidheyatvāt agnihotraṃ juhotītyākhyātārthavidhānāt ।
kimanyadasmādvākyāt pratīyate vihite cākhyātārthe yadagnaye ca
prajāpatayecetyetadviṣayameva prakaraṇāt । ataḥ siddhamasyaivedaṃ nāmeti । eva-
māghārayatītyāpi niṣiddhe guṇavidhāne kimanyadākhyātārthādvidhātum । sa ca﻿<pb n="217"/>
dravyadevatopasaṃbandhāddharativadyajatiḥ । ataḥ santatādayo'pi tannaiva ।
tasmādidamapi tasyaiva nāmeti sthitaṃ santatamāghāraṃ nirvartayatītyarthaḥ । kathaṃ
punaratra na vākyabhedaḥ, yadagnaye ca prajāpataye cetyanekaguṇavidhānāt ।
naikakārakaviśeṣaṇavidhāne anekaguṇavidhānākhyo vākyabhedaḥ । saṃbandhya-
ntaravidhānaṃ hi anekaguṇatocyate na dravyāntaravidhānam ।</p>﻿<pb n="218"/>
<p><q>tadvyapadeśaṃ ca ।</q> iha rūḍhiśabdā udāharaṇaṃ śyenājyapṛṣṭhādayaḥ ।
kaḥ punaratrodbhidadhikaraṇena viśeṣaḥ ? ayamasau; pravṛtti-
nimittānurodhī yogaḥ, rūḍhiḥ punaḥ na yogamanuvartate । nanu ca﻿<pb n="219"/>
nāmadheyatvapakṣepi śyeneneti naiva yogānuvartitvaṃ kalpayitavyam । kiṃ tarhi ?
gauṇamabhidhānam । na rūḍhiḥ gauṇatāṃ vihanti । rūḍhimūlatvādgauṇā-
bhidhānasya । tasmāta matublopo niṣpramāṇaka iti varaṃ gauṇataivāśritā ।
idamevājñānamapanetuṃ bhagavatā bhāṣyakāreṇedamudāhṛtam । yuktaṃ matu-
blopabhayāt yogāśrayaṇānnāmadheyamiti vaktumudbhidādiṣu । na puna—﻿<pb n="220"/>
rlopabhayāllopāntarāśrayaṇaṃ śyene । luptavatikā hi gauṇānāṃ vṛttiḥ ।
tasmādvaraṃ matublopa evāśritaḥ śrautārthānvayabhāvitvāditi punaḥ pūrva-
pakṣitam । ucyate; rūḍhāvapi nāmadheyataiva nyāyyā । nanu na
rūḍhiryogamanuvartata ityuktam । yogo'pi hi naiva rūḍhimanuvartate ।
nanu cātra pūrvapratītā rūḍhiḥ yogamapaharati । satyam । yadi nimittā-
vagamapūrvako vākyārthaḥ । atha tu kāryāvagamapūrvakaṃ nimittatvaṃ tadā﻿<pb n="221"/>
naiva, bhāvārthagatā ca pratipattiḥ । atastadānuguṇyādyoga eva prathama-
taramavasīyata ityaparigṛhītā rūḍhiriti pradarśitaṃ vākyaśeṣe yadājimī-
yurityevamādau । yuktamājyādiṣu; śyene tu kathaṃ ? sāmānādhikaraṇyāt
sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ hi gauṇābhidhānepyabādhitaṃ, vatyarthasya vidheyatvāt ।﻿<pb n="222"/>
matublope punaḥ bhinnādhikaraṇatā'parihāryaiva vidheyatvānmatvarthasya । tasmā-
dvaterlopo na matupa iti siddhaṃ nāmadheyatvam ।</p>
<p><q>nāmadheye guṇaśruteḥ ।</q> kimarthamidamadhikaraṇaṃ ? yogika-
prāptārtharūḍhīnāṃ nāmadheyatvaṃ pratipāditam । śakyate ca vājapeye
tatprakhyatā vaktum । surāgrahavidhānāt । sarvanāmākṣepakabhidamadhikaraṇaṃ﻿<pb n="223"/>
yajeḥ tantrābhidhānopanyāsāt । tantrābhidhānapakṣe guṇavidhānepyanapekṣataiva
śabdasyeti na śakyaṃ nāmābhidhānam । tasmāt tantrābhidhānanirāsāyeda-
madhikaraṇamārabhyate ।</p>
<p>evaṃ tarhi udbhidādayopyatrodāharaṇam; bāḍham । kimiti tarhi
vājapeyena svārājyakāmo yajetetyudāhṛtam ? śiṃśipācodyametat
udbhidādāvapyudāhṛte kimityudbhidudāhriyeteti śakyate vaktum ।﻿<pb n="224"/>
tasmādacodyametaccodyāmahe । śakyate cātra viśeṣā'pi kaścidvaktum ।
'tulyatvātkriyayorna' iti । vājapeyagatametaddarśanam tadapi sarvārthameva । ata
idamucyate guṇavidhipakṣaḥ śreyān iti । kutaḥ ? evaṃ hi kāryānvayyu-
dbhidādiḥ padārtho bhavati । nāmadheyapakṣe punaḥ pravṛttinimittamātraṃ padārthaḥ ।﻿<pb n="225"/>
yasmādvihitasyodbhittvaṃ nodbhidādividhānaṃ tasmādapravṛttyarthaṃ nimittopādānaṃ
pravṛttyarthaṃ vākyamiti kāryanimittayorasāmañcasyaṃ syāt ।</p>
<p>nanu ca matvarthalakṣaṇā aśabdārthabhūtā''śrayaṇīyetyuktam । saiva
nāstītyucyate । kathaṃ nāsti ? ākhyātārtho hi kāryakāraṇasaṃbandhepye-
karūpo'vagamyate । sādhyamāna eva hi sādhanam । ubhayoravagatau kimiti
matvarthalakṣaṇā । tasmādupapanno'yamarthaḥ vājapeyena yāgaṃ yāgena svārājyamiti ।﻿<pb n="226"/>
darśanato'nyathābhidhānaṃ; na punaḥ śabdārthāvagatau ।</p>
<p>nanu vastudharmo'yaṃ na śabdadharmaḥ śabdo hi anyathā vidheyatayā'vaga-
mayati । anyathā coddeśyatayā । satyam । sa tūbhayarūpatvāt tathā'bhidheyatā
ca, ubhayābhidhānepi yajeteti śabdaḥ saṃbandhinoḥ samarpayituṃ kṣamaḥ । kṣamaścet
siddho guṇavidhiḥ prāmāṇyaṃ ca । maivam; tau tvakṣamau tayoścet sāmarthyaṃ nāsti﻿<pb n="227"/>
kimabhidhānasāmarthyaṃ kariṣyati । tasmāt dvayorarthayorvidhānāt kārya-
dvayamidaṃ prāpnoti-yajeta svārājyakāmaḥ vājapeyena yajeta iti ca
parasparāsambaddham । kiṃ jātaṃ ? parasparaṃ sambandhāvagatiratyaktā bhavati ।
anavagamyamānārthaḥ kalpito bhavati । tadevedaṃ sāpekṣatvam ।
viruddhā ca matvarthalakṣaṇā । tasmāt uktābhiryuktibhiḥ nāmadheyapakṣa eva
samañcasaḥ । yatpunaḥ kāryanimittayorasāmañcasyamuktaṃ; na, avighātāt ।
vighāte cāsāmañjasyaṃ nānaupayikatve । tasmādadoṣaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="228"/>
tadguṇāstu vidhīyeran ।</q> kimarthamidamadhikaraṇamārabhyate ? ko'yaṃ praśnaḥ ?
nanu cāgneyādayo guṇavidhayaḥ na nāmadheyānīti jñātuṃ; yuktam yaugika-﻿<pb n="229"/>
prāptārtharūḍhīnāṃ nāmatvam । na ca 'āgneyo'ṣṭākapāla' ityatra
nāmadheyatvaṃ saṃbhavati । ākhyātārthasāmānādhikaraṇyāddhi nāmatoktā
na cātra bhavatītyākhyātamavidheyārthatvāt bhāvārthaṃm na cāsau vidheyaḥ
na coktāddhetoḥ hetvantaraṃ nāmadheye'stīti praśnaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="230"/>
<p>atrocyate—punarapi sāpekṣataivātra śaṅkyate, kathaṃ ? yathaivātra
nāmadheyatvaṃ na saṃbhavati bhāvārthasāmānādhikaraṇyābhāvāt tathā guṇavidhānamapi
vidheyabhāvārthāśravaṇāt ।</p>
<p>nanvāgneya iti dravyadevatāsaṃyogaśravaṇāt yajyartho bhāvārthaḥ, satyaṃ yadi
dravyadevatāsaṃyogaḥ śrūyate । nanu cāgneya iti śrūyate; satyam, yadyaṣṭā-﻿<pb n="231"/>
kapālaviṣayo na syāt । yadyaṣṭākapālaviṣayaḥ tataḥ kim ? idaṃ tato
bhavati । avihitaivāṣṭākapālatā pratipattavyā । na cāvihito'ṣṭāka-
pālo'sti ।</p>
<p>nanu aṣṭasu kapāleṣu śrṛto yaḥ so'ṣṭākapālo laukikaḥ;
vācaniko vā, kapāleṣu śrayayatīti vacanādvā । vācanikastāvanna
sambhavati aṣṭasaṅkhyāśravaṇāt । saṅkhyā vidhīyata iti cainna;
itaretarāśrayaprasaṅgāt āgneye saṅkhyā saṅkhyāyāmāgneya iti ।﻿<pb n="232"/>
tasmānna guṇavidhiḥ sambhavati । na ca nāmetyuktam । kathaṃ tarhi
nāmadheyamityuktaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa ? kva voktam ? upanyāse kiṃ nāmadheyaṃ
uta guṇavidhiriti । guṇavidhipratiṣedhaṃ ca kurvatā nāmadheyamityuktaṃ bhavati
satyamuktaṃ na tu vidheyasya । ato nāmagrahaṇāt prasiddhārthatā darśitā ।
prasiddhiśca pramāṇāntarādṛte na bhavatīti sāpekṣatvaṃ prayogasya darśitam ।
atrocyate । syādetadevaṃ yadi saṅkhyāsambandhe devatāsambandhe cetaretarā-
śrayaḥ syāt । na tvasāvasti । aṣṭākapālasya devatāvidhiḥ । nanu cāsāva-﻿<pb n="233"/>
prasiddha ityuktam । kimabhidheyatayāpi ? na, kāryatayā । iṣṭamevaitata,
ata eva vidhīyate । tasmādabhidhānāprasiddhiḥ vidhānaṃ vihanti ।
na punaḥ kāryatayāpyaprasiddhiḥ tasmādyajyarthasyeva siddhamaṣṭāka-
pālārthasya vidhānam । prasiddhābhidhānaṃ caitat pradarśitaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa
'nānyena śrapitaṃ gṛhṇāti' iti । tasmādyajyarthavat taddhitārtho'yamapi
prasiddhaḥ । ato na sāpekṣatvaprasaṅgaḥ । na ca prāptārthatā'gnihotravatsambhavati ।﻿<pb n="234"/>
<p><q>barhirājyayorasaṃskāre ।</q> prāsaṅgikamidamadhikaraṇam । kaḥ punaḥ
prasaṅgaḥ ? vidheyenāpyarthena nāmārthānvayo dṛṣṭaḥ । ayamapi cājyaśabdaḥ
karmanimitta eva loke dṛṣṭaḥ । tasmādayamapi kāryānvayī saṃskāreṇājyaṃ kuryā-
diti । nanu cākarmanimittako'pi kvacit dṛṣṭaḥ <quote> ājyaṃ krayyaṃ</quote> 'barhirādāya
gāvo gatāḥ' iti । sārvabhaumo hi prayogaḥ śrauto bhavitumarhati naikadeśa﻿<pb n="235"/>
prabhavaḥ । kasmāt ? prasiddhasya śraute'rthe gauṇatā saṃbhavati ।
na cāyaṃ sarvatra ghṛtavacanatayā prasiddhaḥ । aprasiddhasya ghṛte gauṇatvaṃ
nopapadyate । karmaṇā sādhane yatra punarekadeśe prayujyate tatra karmanimitta-
kepi prayogātsiddho ghṛte gauṇaḥ । tasmātkāryārthataiva yuktā</p>﻿<pb n="236"/>
<p>atrocyate । na kāryārthatayānvayo ghaṭate itaretarāśrayatvaprasaṅgāt
barhiṣaḥ prokṣaṇaṃ prokṣaṇena ca barhiriti । kathaṃ tarhi aṣṭākapāle na ?
na, abhidhānataḥ prasiddherityuktam ? iha punaḥ kāryata evābhidhānamiti
vaiṣamyam । yūpe katham ? anyataḥ prasiddhyabhāvādagatikā gatiriyam ।
keyamagatikā gatiḥ ? kiṃ na śāstrādavagamyate ? satyāṃ prasiddhau
nāvagamyate ? aprasiddhe punaḥ padārthe apratihatatvādvidhyarthasya kalpyate ।﻿<pb n="237"/>
<p>yaduktaṃ sārvabhaumo gauṇo na saṃbhavati śrautasyāprasiddheḥ; eka-
deśasthastu saṃbhavatīti; nāvaśyaṃ prasiddhaścautārthameva gauṇaṃ prayuñjate
laukikāḥ rājaśabdamiva kṣatriyepi । tatrāpi tulyo doṣaḥ sādṛśyaprati-
pattyarthaṃ hi gauṇaṃ prayuñjate । atadbuddhyāpi gauṇaṃ prayuñjata iti
haṭho'yam । atrābhidhīyate । na prayokturvivakṣāmapekṣate śabdārthasambandhaḥ ।
saṃbandhāpekṣā hi vivakṣā ।</p>﻿<pb n="238"/>
<p>uktaṃ hi gopotalikādiṣu aśaktijatvāparijñānādanādimiva prayuñjata
iti sa evamatrāpi vivakṣāparijñānāt kasyacit prayokturvivakṣāśūnyamarthāntare
prayuñjate । kathaṃ punaridamavagamyate ? loke vede ca vyavahāradarśanāt । vede
tāvadājyaṃ vidhāya ghṛtaśabdena stauti । lokepi vā ājyaṃ krayyamiti kriyā-
sādhananirapekṣaḥ prayogaḥ । nanu ca tatrāpyajñātavivakṣā(rtha)tvaṃ śakyate vaktum ।</p>﻿<pb n="239"/>
<p>ukto vaitasādiṣu parihāraḥ । vaidikavyavahārasāmyāt vipratipattau
nirṇaya iti । kiṃ punaḥ prāsaṅgikasya prayojanam ? anavadhyavasāya eva ।
nanu ca bhāṣyakāreṇa karmaṇyeva viśeṣaḥ pradarśitaḥ ata evānadhyavasāyaḥ
prayojanam । nirṇaye tvadhyavasānāt sthitameva prayojanam ।</p>﻿<pb n="240"/>
<p><q>prokṣaṇīṣvarthasaṃyogāt ।</q> kimarthamidaṃ pṛthagadhikaraṇaṃ ? sārva-
bhaumaikadeśaprabhavayoḥ smṛtito'pavādaḥ kathyate । kathaṃ punaḥ prayogasya
smṛtito'pavādaḥ kathyate ? sambhavati smṛtyānuguṇyaṃ prayogasya । yasmāt
dvayoravayavayogaḥ saṃbhavati 'prokṣaṇīrāsādayati' 'prokṣaṇībhirudvejitāḥ smaḥ'
iti । tasmāt smṛtito nirṇaya iti । śeṣamuktam ।</p>﻿<pb n="241"/>
<p><q>tathā nirmanthye ।</q> kimatrātiricyate ? idamatrātiricyate । smṛti-
rapyativyāpikā aciranirmathite darśanāt । ataḥ smṛtito'pi na nirṇaya﻿<pb n="242"/>
iti manyate । aviśeṣavidhānāt smṛterna viśeṣaprayogo vihantuṃ
kṣamaḥ । vihantyaviśeṣajñānamiti cet, na vihanti viśeṣaparisamāpte—
raviśeṣasya । tasmāt pūrvavadidamapi । tena tathetyuktam ।</p>
<p><q>vaiśvadeve vikalpa iti cet ।</q> kathaṃ punaḥ guṇavidhi-
nāmadheyatayātra saṃśayaḥ ? guṇavidhipakṣa evātra sāmānādhikaraṇya-﻿<pb n="243"/>
mupapannataram । pratyayārthatvāt bhāvasya । kimiti tarhi nāmadheya-
tayopanyāsaḥ ? viṣayābhāvādvidhānasya । kimiti viṣayābhāvaḥ ?
agnyādibhiḥ śrutyāvaruddhatvāt prakṛtānāṃ karmaṇām । karmāntaraṃ
kimiti na bhavati ? tadapi nādhyavasīyate prakṛtatvādāmikṣāyāḥ ।﻿<pb n="244"/>
tasmānna nāmato nāpi guṇato'napekṣatvaṃ śakyate'vagantumiti । cenmanyase
anapekṣatvādhyavasānaṃ na śakyate kartumiti bhavatu guṇavidhānena
adhyavasānam tathā'vagamānnāmākhyātārthasambandhasya । nanu cokto viṣayā-
bhāvaḥ, durukto hi saḥ । kathaṃ duruktaḥ ? śrutāddhi kāryakalpanā, na kāryataḥ
śrutam । kimidaṃ ? idamidaṃ, utpattiśiṣṭaguṇāvarodho hyanavagame hetuḥ ।
na punaravagatasya vighāte । vaiśvadevaśabdaścāyaṃ ākhyātārtha eva vartate ।
nāgnyādayaḥ saṃbandhinamākhyātārthaṃ vaiśvadevaśabdābhidhetayā nivārayituṃ﻿<pb n="245"/>
kṣamāḥ । sambandhyantaraviṣayatāṃ nivārayanti nābhidheyatām । tataḥ
kim ? idaṃ tato bhavati abhidheyopapattyarthaṃ sambandhyantaraprāptiḥ notpatti-
saṃbandhino'gnyādayaḥ vighnanti । tathā saṃskāryatayā''kṣiptaṃ phalacamasasya
yāgasādhanabhāvaṃ somaḥ । tasmādvikalpenādhyavasānam । na prakaraṇāt
pratyakṣavidhānācca । na hi prakaraṇaṃ dravyasya ।</p>
<p>yadyevaṃ nāmadheyataivāstu; abhidhānopapattyarthaṃ hi guṇāntarasaṃbandhaḥ﻿<pb n="246"/>
kalpyate । atulyapramāṇaśiṣṭānāṃ tvavikalpaḥ tattu nāmadheyatayai-
vopapadyate ।</p>
<p>nanu cāvayavārtho'vagamyamānaḥ kāryānanvayī syāt । nānvita-
syānvayo nyāyyaḥ anvitaścāmikṣāyāmarthaḥ । tasmāt kāryānanvayo nābhidhānaṃ
vārayitumutsahate । tasmānna vikalpaḥ kalpayituṃ śakyate । nāpyāvṛttiḥ
karmaṇaḥ ataḥ nāmatayaivādhyavasānaṃ nyāyyam ।</p>﻿<pb n="247"/>
<p>kathaṃ punaravaiśvadeve vaiśvadevābhidhānam । guṇavidhau punarvidhānataḥ
siddhyati । satyamevaṃ yadyekāntato vidhānataḥ siddhyati । āmikṣāyāṃ
hi anabhidhānaprasaṅgāt । tulyaṃ ca prakṛtatvam । kataratpunaranayoḥ
balīyaḥ ? na vidheyasyāvidheyābhidhānaṃ siddhyati । bhavati ca tulyayogināṃ
lakṣaṇābhidhānaṃ nāmapakṣe daṇḍino gacchantīti ca । tasmājjyāyānayaṃ
pakṣaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="248"/>
<p><q>pūrvavanto'vavidhānārthāḥ । uktaṃ vidhyuddeśārthavādamantravidhibhiḥ
prāmāṇyam । iha punaḥ aṣṭākapāle mantratvaṃ nāsti । ataścodakatvāt
nāmadheyamapi na sambhavati sāmānādhikaraṇyābhāvāt aṣṭākapālādiṣu ।
arthavādaguṇavidhānatvaṃ tu sandihyate ।</p>﻿<pb n="249"/>
<p>tatra guṇavidhānaṃ tāvanna sandihyate, viṣayābhāvāt । kathamabhāvaḥ ?
guṇāntarotpattinirodhāt । puroḍāśakapāle tu abhāvārthatvādevāviṣayaḥ ।
tathā'rthavādo'pi dvādaśasaṅkhyā saṅkhyāntaranirodhāt na tatsambandhitayā
stutiḥ 'āpaḥ śāntā' itivat । tasmāt pratibhāmātratvāt punarapyana-
pekṣatvākṣepaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="250"/>
<p>evaṃ sthite kaścit guṇavidhānena prāmāṇyaṃ manyate ko'bhiprāyaḥ ?
kimutpattinirodhaṃ na paśyati ? na na paśyati sahavākyabhramāt
sarvasaṅkhyāyuktaṃ nirvapatiṃ manyate । ekavākyatvāt । ataścāvṛttiḥ
karmaṇo vikalpo vā guṇānāmityabhiprāyaḥ । vaiśvānaraṃ dvādaśakapālamiti
devatārthamupakramaṃ manyate ।</p>﻿<pb n="251"/>
<p>atrocyate । na guṇavidhānāt prāmāṇyaṃ śakyate
vaktuṃ viṣayābhāvāt । nanu vaiśvānaradevatākaṃ karma viṣaya
ityuktam । na tat, dvādaśakapālavirodhāt । <quote>'yadaṣṭākapāla'</quote>
ityevamādinā saṅkhyāvidhānamiti yaduktaṃ duruktaṃ tat । kathaṃ ?﻿<pb n="252"/>
vaiśvānaraśabdasya vyatiriktārthavibhaktivacanatvāt । dvādaśakapālaśabdasya
ca sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ śrautam । yadaṣṭākapāla ityevamādīnāṃ brahmavarcasapunāti
padasaṃbandhānna vaiśvānarapadārthādhikaraṇatā'vagamyate । punātistutyanyathānu-
papattyā tu kalpanīyaḥ sambandhaḥ । na ca kalpanā klṛptau upapadyata ityuktam ।﻿<pb n="253"/>
evaṃ tarhi pratibhaiva, na, stutyarthatayaivopapatteḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ stutyarthatopapadyate ?
nirastatvāt saṅkhyāyāḥ saṅkhyāntareṇetyuktam । abhidhānato hi nirāsaḥ,
nāsadbhāvataḥ sadbhāvanimittaśca saṃbandho, nābhidhānimittaḥ sadbhāve satya-
vayuttyābhidhānamupapadyate ।</p>﻿<pb n="254"/>
<p>nanvavayojitasya saṃbandhānavagamaḥ prāpnoti abhidhānārthamevā-
vayojanaṃ śakyate na punaḥ saṃbandhitāpyavayojayituṃ śakyate । vivakṣāhya-
bhidhānamanuvartate na vastu । tasmāta āpaḥ śāntā itivadupapannā
stutiḥ । tathā ca darśitaṃ śobhanamasya cakrasya nemitumbāramiti﻿<pb n="255"/>
guṇaphalasaṃbandhavidhānamapyetasmādeva na saṃbhavati । kasmāt etasmāt ?
stutyarthatvenaikavākyatāvagamāt । taddarśitamupakramopasaṃhārābhyām । ataḥ
stutyarthatayopapatteḥ siddhamanapekṣatvam ।</p>
<p>tatsiddhiḥ । uktamavayutyābhidhānataḥ saṃbandhena stutirupapadyata
iti । yatra punaḥ saṃbandhitaiva nāvagamyate । na ca guṇavidhānaṃ sambhavati
yathā 'yajamāna ekapālaḥ' 'yajamānaḥ prastara' iti tatra kathaṃ prāmāṇyam ?﻿<pb n="256"/>
<p>nanu ca gauṇamukhyādhikaraṇe sthitaṃ yathā gauṇaḥ saṃbandho'rthāntara-
vācināmapi bhavatīti । tadevedaṃ na mṛṣyate । kasmāt ? naiva gauṇatā
sambhavati arthāntarasaṃbandhitayā । kathaṃ punarna saṃbhavati ? gauṇe hyabhidhāne
guṇānāmeva vācyatvaṃ yuktam । anyathā śauryameva siṃhaśabdo devadatte prati-
pādayati, jvalanaśabdaśca māṇavake piṅgalatāmiti nopapadyate । siṃhajāti-﻿<pb n="257"/>
mukhena siṃhaśabdo guṇān pratipādayan yāvanto jātyabhisambandhā
guṇāstān pratipādayet, aviśeṣāt ।</p>
<p>atha manyase tāvanmātravivakṣāyāṃ sa eva pratīyata iti ।
vivakṣānuvartī tarhi śabdaḥ nābhidheyānuvartī । tataḥ kiṃ ?
adhyāropitatadbhāvo gauṇaḥ । adhyārope ca nārthāntarasambandhaḥ ।
kimiti ? adhyāropo hi adhigatārthaviṣaya eva nānadhigataṃ
vastu spṛśati । sa eveti gṛhyate na tatsadṛśa iti ।﻿<pb n="258"/>
tasmāt prastaraikakapālayoḥ yajamānaśabdo nālaṃ stutau । guṇavidhistarhi
bhavatu । asāvapyasaṃbhavānnaiva bhavati । guṇo vidhīyamānaḥ kāryārthe'tra
vidhīyate । sa cobhayathāpi nopapadyate । tadetaddarśitaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa ।
tasmātsaiveyaṃ pratibhāśaṅkā ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate । satyaṃ guṇavidhirna saṃbhavati arthavādastu na 
nivārayituṃ śakyate । nanu cārthāsambandhānnārthavāda ityuktam ।
ayuktamuktam । kathaṃ ? saṃbhavati svārthasaṃbandhitayaiva gauṇamabhidhānam ।</p>﻿<pb n="259"/>
<p>nanu svārthasaṃbandhiguṇamātrānavagamānnetyuktam । vivakṣāto
viśeṣa ityevadapyuktam । satyamuktam । vivakṣāyāṃ hi nābhi-
dheyasaṃbandho'stītyapyuktam । tataśca stutyanupapattiḥ । kiṃ kena saṃbadhyate ।
atrocyate—na, aniyamajñaḥ khalvasi । abhidheyāvivakṣāyāṃ siṃha-﻿<pb n="260"/>
śabdoccāraṇamanibandhanam । na ca śabdāntareṇādhyāropābhidhānaṃ nopa-
padyate । manda maivaṃ, adhyāropaviṣayatayā hi siṃhārtho vivakṣyate,
na guṇasaṃbandhitayā । na cāsau siṃhaśabdādṛte saṃbhavati
tasmānnanibandhanaṃ siṃhaśabdoccāraṇam । nanu cāsmābhiridamuktam ।﻿<pb n="261"/>
kimiti siṃhārtho devadette adhyāropyata iti । tadguṇadarśanāditi
cet; prāptaṃ tarhi mukhyārthasaṃbandhitayā pratipādanam । kathaṃ viśeṣā-
vagatiḥ iti cet । pramāṇāntaradarśanāt tatpūrvakatvācca gauṇasya ।﻿<pb n="262"/>
mukhyo'pi tāvadarthaḥ pramāṇāntaradarśanādviśeṣe vyavasthāsyāti gauṇo
neti kā yuktiḥ ? kathaṃ tarhi khapuṣpamiti ? yathaiva khapuṣpamiti ।
tasmātsiddho'rthavādaḥ । kiṃ prayojanaṃ kathaṃ ceti darśitaṃ bhāṣye ।</p>
<p>jātiḥ । jātyādiṣvapyevameva yojyam । pṛthagadhikaraṇāni tu parihārānyatva-﻿<pb n="263"/>
pradarśanārthāni । tasmāt gauṇārthānāmarthavādatayā sthitaṃ prāmāṇyam ।
lākṣaṇikārthānāṃ ca । kathaṃ punaḥ sṛṣṭyādiṣu lakṣaṇānāmapi
lakṣyatvam ? lakṣyaiḥ sahaikakriyāyogāt । tasmāllakṣaṇatve nimitta-
tvāt । ato lakṣyalakṣaṇateti na virodhaḥ । aśvādiṣu kathaṃ paśuśabdo﻿<pb n="264"/>
lakṣaṇayā । pratiṣedhapūrvakatvāt prayogasya । pratiṣiddho hi
tajjātīyeṣu jātiśabdaḥ prayujyamānaḥ tajjātīyāntareṣu gauṇatayaiva
prayogaṃ labhate । kasmāt ? jātiśabdo hi tajjātīye pratiṣidhyamānaḥ
samavetasya guṇasya pratiṣedhyatayaiva pratiṣedhaviṣayo bhavati । guṇapratiṣedhācca
tajjātīyeṣveva prayujyamāno gauṇārtha eva pratīyate । tasmājjātiśabdo
gauṇa ityavirodhaḥ । ataḥ siddhamanapekṣatvam ।</p>﻿<pb n="265"/>
﻿<pb n="266"/>﻿<pb n="267"/>
<p><q>sandigdheṣu vākyaśeṣāt ।</q> nanu ca yavavarāhādiṣu vākyaśeṣāt
sandehāpanayaḥ kṛtaḥ ? satyaṃ, padārthaviṣayastu saḥ, autpattikānautpattikatayā
sandihyamānaḥ padārtho nirṇītaḥ । asti vā padasyārthaḥ ? bāḍhamasti ।﻿<pb n="268"/>
kathaṃ tarhi vākyavākyārthayorautpattikatvaṃ vṛddhavyavahārāt । satyaṃ, sa
tvavayavaśa ityuktaṃ tadbhūtānāmityatra । tasmāt tadbhūte tatra sandehaḥ ।
iha tu kriyārthe । so'yaṃ padārthavākyārthayoḥ viśeṣaḥ । pratipāditaścāyaṃ
vistareṇa । ataḥ kriyārthasaṃśayādapyaprāmāṇyam । evaṃ sthite kaści-
dupakramavaśādupasaṃhāranirṇayo yukta iti manyate, avirodhāt । sāmānyaṃ hi
svātmani viśeṣe ca vartate । sṛṣṭyarthavat । atrocyate । syādetadevaṃ yadi﻿<pb n="269"/>
vākyāntaravihitaṃ sāmānyaṃ syāt । iha punaḥ viśeṣaparyantaivānvayāvagatiḥ
ekavākyatvāt । tasmādvākyaśeṣāpekṣaṃ kriyārthatvamiti siddham ।</p>
<p>arthādvā kalpanaikadeśatvāt । yatrāpyanuṣṭhāne saṃśayaḥ tatrāpi
śāstrameva sandigdhaṃ manyate ।</p>﻿<pb n="270"/>
<p>nanu caitadayuktam anuṣṭhānasandehātśāstrameva sandigdhamiti śāstra-
pūrvakatvodanumānasya । satyaṃ yathā bhavānāha siddhānuśāsane । kāryānu-
śāsane tvāskandatyanuṣṭhānasaṃśayo'pi śāstram । kimanuṣṭhānaṃ na śāstrapūrvakaṃ ?
satyamanubandhe śāstrapūrvakam । niyogārthaṃ tvanuṣṭhānam । tasmādupapannāṃ
niyogārthasaṃśayaḥ । sa punaḥ sāmarthyato nirṇetavyaḥ anuṣṭhānasyāsaṃbhāvyāt ।
sāmarthyasādhyatvāccānuṣṭhāsya । tasmānmāṃsādiṣu darśitā vyavasthā bhāṣyakāreṇa﻿<pb n="271"/>
ato vidhyarthavādamantrasmṛtināmadheyānuṣṭhānato'pekṣatākṣepaṃ kṛtvā sthāpitaṃ
prāmāṇyaṃ codanāyāḥ । iti pramāṇalakṣaṇam ।
iti śrīmatprabhākaramiśraviracitāyāṃ
śavarabhāṣyaṭīkāyāṃ bṛhatyāṃ
prathamādhyāyasya caturthaḥ
pādaḥ samāptaḥ﻿<pb n="272"/>
<head>atha dvitīyo'dhyāyaḥ</head>
<p><quote>prathame'dhyāye pramāṇalakṣaṇaṃ vṛtta</quote>iti । yathā pramāṇaṃ śabdaḥ
tathoktamityarthaḥ । kutaḥ <quote>yasmādvidhyarthavādamantrasmṛtayaḥ tattvato nirṇītāḥ ।﻿<pb n="273"/>
guṇavidhirnāmadheyaṃ ca parīkṣitam । sandigdhānāmarthānāṃ vākyaśeṣā-
darthāccādhyavasānamuktam</quote> । ete cākṣepahetravo'nyathāgṛhyamāṇāḥ । tattvatastu
parijñātā na prāmāṇyaṃ vighnanti । atastattvato nirṇītā yasmāt
tasmāt—'uktaṃ pramāṇalakṣaṇaṃ' ityuktam ।</p>
<p><quote>tanna prasmartavyaṃ</quote> ityanapekṣatvasavyapekṣaṃ bhedābhedakathanam ।
kasmāt ? kāryasya hi bhedābhedaḥ kathyate । sa cānapekṣatvanibandhanaḥ ।
anyasavyapekṣe hi śabde śabdādeva kāryavibhāgo na śakyate vaktum ।
tasmādanapekṣatvādityevaṃ na prasmartavyamityuktam ।</p>﻿<pb n="274"/>
<p>anantaramiti kasmāt ? anyadapi hi lakṣaṇaṃ śeṣādi ana-
pekṣatvasavyapekṣameva śabdānnirṇetuṃ śakyate । satyaṃ śakyaṃ na punarana-
ntaram । idameva tvanantaramityabhiprāyeṇokmam । kasmātpunaridamevā-
nantaraṃ na śeṣalakṣaṇādi ? kāryabhedapūrvakatvāta sarvasthoparitanasya,﻿<pb n="275"/>
<quote>pradhānāpradhānāni parākṣyante । bhinnānyabhinnāni ceti</quote> । kimidaṃ pradhānā-
pradhānānīti ? yadi tāvat parīkṣiṣyanta iti saṃbadhyate anyat pratijñātaṃ
anyatparīkṣitaṃ syāt । bhedābhedaparīkṣā hyanantaraṃ dṛśyate, na punaḥ
pradhānāpradhānaparīkṣā ।</p>
<p>nanu cetarattadarthaṃ—yaimtudravyaṃ cikīrṣyata iti pradhānā-
pradhānaparīkṣāpyanantaraṃ dṛśyata eva । naitadevam । tṛtīyasiddhaṃ hi
tat । saṃvyavahārārthamihānītaṃ kāryabhedaprasiddhye । tathā ca bhāṣyakāreṇa
svayamevoktam <quote>yaistudravyaṃ cikīrṣyate guṇastatra pratīyeteti ।
tatrāpūrvārthatā vyāvartitā dṛṣṭapraṃyojanānāmākhyātārthānām । iha
tu sarveṣāmeva śeṣāṇāṃ lakṣaṇamucyata</quote> iti । tasmātpradhānāpradhānā-﻿<pb n="276"/>
nītyasaṃbaddham । ucyate । pradhānāpradhānānīti sādhyānubandhā abhidhīyante ।
atastāni pradhānāpradhānānīti parīkṣiṣyante bhinnānyabhinnāni ceti ।
anubandhabhedastāvat—yajati dadāti juhotīti । anubandhābhedopi ya
evaṃ vidvān paurṇamāsīṃ yajata iti ।</p>﻿<pb n="277"/>
<p>āgneyo'ṣṭākapāla iti । tasmātsūktam—<quote>pradhānāpradhānāni parīkṣiṣyante
bhinnānyabhinnāni</quote> ceti । <quote>eṣa evārtho varṇanīyo nānya</quote> ityanantara-
śabdavyākhyānam । <quote>eṣa cādhyāyasaṃbandha</quote> ityānantaryasya hetvabhidhānaṃ
tathā pradarśitamasmābhiḥ ।</p>
<p><quote>tadiha ṣaṅvidhaḥ karmabhedo vakṣyate-śabdāntaramabhyāsaḥ saṅkhyā
guṇaḥ prakriyā nāmadheyamiti । kathaṃ karmabhedaḥ śabdāntaraṃ ?﻿<pb n="278"/>
bhidyate'ne neti bhedaḥ tacca karma tasmāt karmabheda ityuktam ।
vakṣyamāṇakramānapekṣaṃ śabdāntarādīnāṃ vyutkrameṇoccāraṇaṃ kramasyānaupayikatva-
pradarśanārtham । vakṣyamāṇamanusaṅkīrtyata iti kimarthaṃ ? hetvabhidhānakāla eva
pratijñābhidhānaṃ nyāyyaṃ naiyāyikā manyante ।</p>﻿<pb n="279"/>
<p>satyaṃ, sādhye sukhagrahaṇārthaṃ caitat, śrotṛbuddhisamādhānāt । <quote>tade
tannānākarmalakṣaṇaṃ</quote> iti pūrvācāryābhidhānaprasiddhiṃ darśayati anāditāṃ
nyāyasya kathayitum । <quote>atonyadupodghātāt prasaktānuprasaktaṃ ca</quote>
iti—apratijñātārthacintādoṣaparihārārtham । prathamaṃ tāvadidaṃ
cintyate prathame'dhyāye idamuktam codanālakṣaṇo'rtho dharma iti
codaneti kriyāyā abhidhāyakaṃ vākyam । vākye ca padānāmarthaḥ﻿<pb n="280"/>
tatra kiṃ padena padena dharmaḥ ucyate-uta sarvaireka iti sambandhaḥ ।
prathame'dhyāye idamuktamityasya kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ kena vā sambadhyate
ato na vidmaḥ kathamidaṃ vyākhyeyamiti ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate—kiṃ padena padeneti prakriyāvirodhaṃ manvānaḥ
vākyavākyārthayorautpattikatvābhidhānāt । tasyedamuttaram । satyaṃ
prathame'dhyāye idamuktam—codanālakṣaṇo'rtho dharma iti । codanā ca
vākyaṃ vākye ca padānāmartha ityuktam tadbhūtānāmiti ।﻿<pb n="281"/>
tato yuktamevedaṃ kiṃ padena padena dharma ucyate uta sarvaireka iti । etaduktaṃ
bhavati-kiṃ padena padenābhihitārthasya kāryayogitā, uta parasparasambandhasavya-
pekṣasyeti । kathaṃ punaḥ parasparasambandhitayā'vagamyamānasyārthasyāsambandhina
eva kāryayogitā । dṛṣṭā hi aruṇādiṣu dravyaguṇayoḥ । nanu tatrāvagatireva
nāstītyuktam । satyamevam । aidamarthyena nāstītyuktam, na guṇaguṇitayā;
anyathā niyama eva hi na syāt । evamatrāpi nāmākhyātayoḥ, kriyākāraka-
sambandhanirapekṣa eva niyogasambandhaḥ utājahatkriyākārakasaṃbandha evetyupapannaḥ﻿<pb n="282"/>
saṃśayaḥ । kiṃ tāvatprāptaṃ ? asmin saṃśaye kiṃ tāvadyuktamityarthaḥ ।
pratipadaṃ dharmā iti yuktam । kasmāt ? niyogārthatvāduccāraṇasya sarva-
padānām । nanu ca kriyākārakasaṃbandho'pyatrāvagamyate । satyamavagamyate,
na tu kriyārthatve kārakāṇāṃ pramāṇamasti । niyogārthasya sādhyatvenā-
vagamāt । kathaṃ punaḥ nirvyāpārameva kārakaṃ niyogārthamabhiniṣpādayati,
karma vā'kriyamāṇaṃ ? bhavatvarthādayaṃ dravyaguṇayoriva sambandhaḥ tādarthyaṃ tu
niyogāyaiva ।</p>﻿<pb n="283"/>
<p>tasmāt pratipadaṃ dharmaḥ । atrocyate—naitadupapadyate, yadi
hyajahatāṃ pratītamarthaṃ niyogārthatā na syāt syāt pratipadaṃ dharmaḥ ।
yatra punarapekṣitaiva saṃbandhāvagatirānuguṇyena tatra tattyāge śrutahāna-
meva syāt । na caitadyuktam । tasmādanyatarānugṛhīto'nyaparo vidhyartha
iti । <quote>evaṃ cādṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅkalpanā laghīyasī bhaviṣyati</quote> । kā﻿<pb n="284"/>
punaratrādṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā ? śabdādapi hi dṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭameva ।
satyaṃ yathā bhavānāha । pratipadaṃ kalpanāyāmāśrayāśrayi(bhāva)prasaṅge niya-
mānumānamadṛṣṭamapramāṇakaṃ prāpnotītyarthaḥ । tatra bahvadṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā
kathaṃ ? evaṃ tāvadāśrayatvaṃ kārakāṇāṃ, āśrayitvaṃ karmaṇāṃ, punaśca tatsiddhaye
sādhyasādhanatvaṃ viśeṣaniyamaśceti । anyatarānugṛhītapakṣe punaḥ
alpīyasyadṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā bhaviṣyatīti ।</p>
<p>kimidaṃ adṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅkalpaneti ? adṛṣṭamanumānaṃ yasyāsau
adṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgaḥ tasya kalpanā adṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā alpīyasī﻿<pb n="285"/>
bhaviṣyati । nanu ca naiva bhavati । kimalpīyasī bhavatītyucyate ।
anyatarānugṛhītapakṣepi vidhyarthasyaiva vidyate kalpanā । nanu ca
śābdamevedaṃ kimatra kalpyate ? kāryato'vagamaṃ navame vakṣyāmaḥ ।
śabdāvagatakāryamūlatvācca śābdam । tasmātsādhūktam—evamalpīyasya-
dṛṣṭānumānakalpaneti । <quote>tasmādekamapūrvamiti</quote> kimidamekama-
pūrvamiti ? nanvidameva । naivamekasmādapūrvamiti prakramāt ।
atrābhidhīyate । yadā pratipadaṃ dharmaḥ tadā pratipadaṃ niyogabhedena
bhavitavyam । pratipadamanubandhabhedāt । amumeva kāryabhedaṃ darśayituṃ﻿<pb n="286"/>
bhagavatā bhāṣyakāreṇa phalenopasaṃhṛtam। tasmādekamapūrvamiti ।।</p>
<p><quote>yadā ekamapūrvaṃ tadā sandehaḥ-kiṃ bhāvaśabdebhyaḥ uta dravyaguṇa-
śabdebhya iti</quote> ।। bhāvaśabdagrahaṇena kasya grahaṇaṃ ? ākhyātānāmeva ।
evaṃ tarhi nāmaśabdebhyaḥ utākhyātaśabdebhya iti vaktavyam । kimida-
mucyate । kiṃ bhāvaśabdebhyaḥ uta dravyaguṇaśabdebhya iti ।﻿<pb n="287"/>
kiṃ vātrātiricyate ? dviruccarito nāmaśabdaḥ । anabhiprāyajño bhavān ।
yadi hi kimākhyātaśabdebhyaḥ uta nāmaśabdebhya ityucyate tataśca nirṇīyate
ākhyātaśabdebhya iti tadā āgneyo'ṣṭākapāla ityakriyārthaḥ syāt;
nāmatvāt, bhavatīti ca kriyārthaḥ syāt ākhyātatvāt । aniṣṭaṃ caitat
bhavatyarthasyāvidheyatvāt । dravyadevatāsaṃbandhasya ca vidheyatvāt ।﻿<pb n="288"/>
tasmānnāmākhyātagrahaṇaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa na kṛtam । kiṃ tarhi,
yenaiva svabhāvenākhyātasya vidhyarthatā saṃbhavati yena ca nāmno na saṃbhavati
tenaiva svabhāvenopanyāsaḥ kṛtaḥ । kena punaḥ svabhāvenākhyātasya vidhyarthatā ?
kena ca nāmno na bhavati ? bhāvārthatayā''khyātasya vidhyarthatā ।
dravyaguṇābhadhānatayā ca na nāmnaḥ । <quote>kaḥ punarayamākhyātārthavyatirikto
bhāvo nāma</quote> ? kaścākhyātaśabdādanyo bhāvaśabdo nāma ? prativacanaṃ tu
<quote>yajati dadāti juhotīti</quote> ।</p>
<p>nanu sa evāyamākhyātārthaḥ ta evāmī ākhyātaśabdā ityākṣepaḥ । samā-
dhānaṃ tu, nākhyātārthamātraṃ yajati dadāti juhotīti, kintarhi anyotpāda-﻿<pb n="289"/>
katvamapi gamyate na kevalaṃ pūrvāparībhāvaḥ yathā bhavatīti ।
tadidamuktam <quote>yajyarthaścāto'vagamyate bhāvayediti ca</quote> । kimuktaṃ
bhavati ? pūrvāparībhāvaścāto'vagamyate, anyotpādakatvaṃ ceti । punaścā-
yamabhiprāyaḥ prakaṭīkṛtaḥ tathā yateta, yathā yatkiṃñcidbhavatīti । tenaite
ākhyātaśabdā api bhāvaśabdā ityucyante । ato dravyaguṇaśabdagrahaṇamapi﻿<pb n="290"/>
dravyaguṇapratyayotpādakatvāt akriyārthatvaṃ, na nāmatvāta । <quote>kiṃ tāvatprāptaṃ ?
aviśeṣeṇeti</quote> kā'bhiprāyaḥ ? dravyaṃ vā bhavatu kriyārthaṃ; kriyā vā
bhavatu dravyārthā । sarvathā tāvadaparityaktakriyākārakasaṃbandha eva kārya-
sambandha iti siddham । atrocyate । naivaṃ sidhyatīti । yadā hi dravyārthā
kriyā tadā kriyākārakasaṃbandhaḥ tyakta eva bhavati । kasmāt ? dravyaṃ
hi tadā karmabhūtaṃ kriyāyām । na ca karma kārakaṃ kārakasthā hyatpattiḥ
karmeti vakṣyāmaḥ । kathaṃ tarhi karmaṇi kārake dvitīyetyāgamaḥ । karturīpsita-﻿<pb n="291"/>
tamaṃ karmeti ca kārakādhikāre । yatra kiyāphalamabhinippadyate tatkarmeti
sūtrārthaḥ । anyathā hīpsitatamagrahaṇamanarthakaṃ syāt । tasmāt karmaṇi dvitī-
yetyapi siddham । tasmāt kriyārthaṃ yadā''khyātaṃ bhavati tadaiva dravyaguṇayoḥ
kārakatvasiddhiḥ । ata āha-<quote>ye ye bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdāstebhyaḥ kriyāpratīyeta
yajetetyevamādibhyaḥ</quote> । kutaḥ ? iti praśnaḥ kimanyathā bhāvārthatvaṃ hīyeta ?﻿<pb n="292"/>
bāḍhaṃ hīyate । pūrvāparībhāve hi bhāvārthatvaṃ bhavati । sa pūrvāparībhāvaḥ
dravyaguṇayostadarthatve sati । anyathā hi gādohanena paśukāmasya
praṇayeditivat āśrayamātrāvagatiḥ syāt । na ca godohanasādhyaṃ
praṇayanamavasīyate । nanu ca godohanena praṇayediti pūrvāparībhūtameva
praṇayanaṃ pratīyate godohanaṃ ca karaṇameva । satyaṃ pratīyate । na tu
godohanena paśukāmasya praṇayedityetadvākyārthatayā . tasmādaniyamapakṣe
na niyamena kiyākāraka(saṃbandha)bhāvamajahato vidhyarthatvaṃ vākyasya pratīyate ।
ata idamuktaṃ bhāvārthatvādeveti ।</p>﻿<pb n="293"/>
<p>etaduktaṃ bhavati । evameva saṃbandhāvagamāditi । tadidānīṃ pūrvāparī-
bhūtabhāvavyatirekiṇamarthaṃ bhāvaśabdavācyaṃ prapañcayati <quote>ya āhuḥ kimapi
bhāvayediti te svargakāmapadasaṃbandhāta svargaṃ bhāvayediti brūyuḥ</quote> iti ।
kimidaṃ svargakāmapadasaṃbandhāt svargaṃ bhāvayediti । svargakāmaṃ bhāvayediti
yuktaṃ vaktum । padārthasya hi padārthāntareṇa saṃbandhaḥ svargakāmaścātra
padārthaḥ na svargaḥ, ato'sadevedaṃ pratibhāti । atrocyate ।
satyaṃ svargakāmaḥ padārthaḥ । sa eva padārthāntareṇa saṃbadhyate ।﻿<pb n="294"/>
svargaparastvasau saṃbandhaḥ ityaidaṃparyamatra darśitaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa, dhātvarthasya karaṇa-
tvapradarśanārtham । vakṣyāti ca <quote>sthita etasminnadhikaraṇe guṇavidhirnāma-
dheyamiti vicāro bhaviṣyati</quote> iti । kathaṃ punaḥ svargaṃ bhāvayedityevaṃ paratā
vākyasya ? yathaivaṃparatā tathā'dhikāralakṣaṇe vakṣyāmaḥ । <quote>tasmāttebhyaḥ
kriyāpratīyata</quote> iti nigamitaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa । kā punaratra kiyā ?﻿<pb n="295"/>
vidhyarthaḥ nanu ca phalasya karaṇaṃ kriyetyuktam । phalasya ca yāgaḥkaraṇaṃ
na vidhyarthaḥ ucyate । yathā vidhyarthaḥ karaṇaṃ tatho'dhikāralakṣaṇe vakṣyāmaḥ ।
ihāpi ca bhāṣyakāreṇa <quote>te ca yāgadānasaṃbaddhāḥ svargasyotpattiṃ vadantī</quote>ti
vadatā vidhyarthasyaiva karaṇatoktā । tatsaṃbandhāddhi yāgādeḥ । <quote>kuta*</quote> iti praśno-
'yam । kathaṃ punarniyogārthasya karaṇatā'vagamyata ityabhiprāyaḥ । uttaravādī tu﻿<pb n="296"/>
<quote>eṣahyartho vidhīyate tathā yāgādinā svargakāma</quote> ityādhikāralakṣaṇasiddhamarthaṃ
darśayati । <quote>kena sādhayet svarga yāgādine</quote>ti । kimanena granthena pradarśitaṃ ?
saivādhikārikī yuktiḥ । svargaṃ sādhayato'dhikāra iti sthāsyati । <quote>yasya ca
śabdasyārthena phalaṃ sādhyate tenāpūrvaṃ kṛtvā nānyatheti tato'pūrvaṃ gamyata</quote> iti
pūrvāparavirodhaparihāro'yam । pūrvaṃ hi niyogāt phalamityuktam idānīṃ yāgā
tphalamiti । tenāpūrvaṃ kṛtvetyavirodhaḥ । tato'pūrvameva phalasādhanamiti gamyate ।﻿<pb n="297"/>
<quote>ato yastasya vācaka iti</quote> nigamanametat । yasmādapūrvaṃ sādhayan
bhāvārthaḥ phalaṃ niṣpādayati nānyathā, kṣaṇikatvāt tena tadviṣayo vidhyartho
liṅādibhiḥ pratyāyyate । tasya ca viṣayādhīnapratipattitvāt, bhāvārthānāṃ
ca viṣayabodhakatvāt tato'pūrvaṃ pratīyata ityucyate, na punastasyāmī vācakā
iti । <quote>na tu kaścit sākṣādapūrvasya vācako'sti</quote>iti bhāvārthābhiprāyametat ।﻿<pb n="298"/>
na punarliṅādiśabdo'pi niyogaṃ nācaṣṭe । kathaṃ punarbhāvārthe vācaka-
tvāśaṅkā ? kevalasyāprayogāt niyogaśabdasya, tiṅantasyaiva prayogāt;
tena yāvatprayogānuvartinyeva vācakateti bhrāntānāmarthāvagamaṃ muktvā prayoge-
yattā na sidhyatīti tannirākartumavācaka ityuktam ।</p>
<p>nanu ca na yuktam nirākartum kiṃ vā prayogeyattā
anyathā siddhyati ? arthāvagamo vā vibhāgādavagamyamānaḥ kimapahnotuṃ﻿<pb n="299"/>
śakyate ? kiṃ tarhi prayoganiyame kāraṇaṃ ? prayoga eva । vācaka-
tvasyeva prayogasyāpyanāditoktā । tasmātsūktaṃ na bhāvaśabdena niyogo'rtho-
'bhidhīyata iti । <quote>bhāvārthaiḥ kimapi bhāvayitavyaṃ</quote> ityavaibhaktika-
saṃbandhaṃ phalaniyogabhāvārthānāṃ darśayati ।</p>
<p>ato nāyaṃ vainiyogikaḥ saṃbandha iti siddham । anyathā﻿<pb n="300"/>
viniyogābhāvādasambandhaṃ bādaririva vibhaktividhānānusārī manyate ।
ataśca sthita etasminnadhikaraṇe guṇavidhirnāmadheyamiti vicāro bhaviṣyatīti
na śakyate vaktum । kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ na viniyogalakṣaṇasaṃbandho'yaṃ ?
viniyojakānāṃ śrutyādīnāmabhāvāt । kathamabhāvaḥ ? saṃbandhasyānavagamāt ।
nanu cāyamasti saṃbandhaḥ yajeta svargakāma iti । bāḍhamasti na puna-
radaimarthyalakṣaṇaḥ । kiṃ lakṣaṇastarhi ? adhikāralakṣaṇaḥ । aida-
marthyaṃ ca viniyogāvagamyamityuktaṃ śeṣaḥ parārthatvādityatra । tatra ca
śrutyādīni viniyoge kāraṇānīti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b301"/>
<p>kathaṃ tarhi <quote>“karmāṇyapi jaiminiḥ phalārthatvāt”</quote> iti ? na
dravyaguṇasaṃskāreṣveva pārārthyaṃ phalayāgapuruṣeṣvapīti bādaripakṣaṃ nirasyatā
pārārthyalakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandho'trāstītyabhyupagatam। satyamabhyupagataṃ na puna-
stacchabdedaṃparatayā। tathāca darśitaṃ naṣṭāśvadagdharathavaditi <quote>“nanu ca
bhāvārthaiḥ kimapi bhāvayitavyaṃ svargakāmasya ca kenāpi”</quote> iti guṇa-
pradhānabhāvaṃ darśayati। sa ca pārārthye satīti punaraidaṃparyameva prāpnoti।
netyucyate। bhāvasvabhāvo hyayamiti kathyate nedaṃparatāśabdasya। ata
eva ca dravyaśabdebhyaḥ tṛtīyāyuktebhyo'pi na vidhyarthatā'bhyupagatā।</p>
﻿e<pb n="b302"/>
tasmānna viniyogādyāgasvargayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ। kathaṃ tarhi, bhāvārthatvā-
devetyuktam। ata eva cākhyātaṃ na saṃbandhe smarati pāṇiniḥ।
nanu ca kartari karmaṇi bhāva iti smarati। satyaṃ smarati
na teṣāmanyasaṃbandhitām। yathā prātipadikādavagatasyārthasya
saṃbandhapratipādinyo vibhaktayaḥ na tathā'' khyātāttasyārthasya। nanu ca
tṛtīyādibhiḥ dviṣṭhatvātsaṃbandhasya dvayorapi sambandhitā uktā bhavatīti।
satyaṃ dviṣṭhaḥ saṃbandhaḥ। sambandhitā punarnāmārthasyaiva tṛtīyādibhiḥ।
yathā pumān sadvitīyo dvivacanasyaukārāntasya na punardvitīyopyarthaḥ।

﻿<pb n="b303"/>
ata eva cākhyātārthe kartṛkarmagatā saṅkhayaivocyate vacanaiḥ na
punaḥ kartrādayaḥ, pramāṇāntarāvagamyā hi te niyogataḥ pratyakṣādi-
bhirvā। ata eva tu niyogaḥ kāryepyarthe na bhaviṣyantamartha---
mavagamayati। kārakavyāpāro hi kālatrayāvacchedyo nādhikāraḥ। kathaṃ
tarhi prayājāderviniyojyatvaṃ ? nākhyātātpārārthyamavasīyata ityuktam।

﻿<pb n="b304"/>
<quote>“kimetāvantyeva pramāṇāni ityatra parihāraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ। <quote>“naivaṃ dravyaguṇa-
śabdā”</quote> iti। kiṃ naivaṃ ?”</quote> naivamadhikāralakṣaṇasambandhamarhantītyarthaḥ।
sarvathā hi viniyogapramāṇaviṣayā evaite। ataḥ siddhaṃ bhāvārthatvādeva
viniyogasaṃbandhitāṃ pratipadyata iti।
kathaṃ tarhi svargakāma iti। viṣayamaṅgīkṛtyaitaduktam na punarvi-
niyojyatām। yathā caitadevaṃ tathā svargakāmāghikaraṇe nipuṇatara---
﻿<pb n="b305"/>
mupapādayiṣyāmaḥ। <quote>“bhavanti kecitkarmaśabdā na bhāvārthāḥ yathā śyenaikātri-
kādayaḥ kecit bhāvārthā na karmaśabdāḥ yathā bhāvo bhavanaṃ bhūtiriti”</quote>
bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā iti padadvayābhidhāne bhāvārthasya kiṃ prayojanam ? yadi
karmaśabdebhyaḥ kriyetyucyate śyenaikatrikādibhyo'pyapūrvasyotpattirityuktaṃ
syāt। ete'pi hi karmaśabdāḥ। etebhyo'pi kimiti na bhavati ? dravya-
guṇaśabdanivṛttyarthaṃ bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā ityuktam। na karmaśabda-
nivṛttyartham। tasmādabhidhīyamāne viśeṣaṇe naiva śyenādīnāṃ
nivṛttiḥ। ete'pi bhāvārthasyaiva karmaṇo vācakā yāgādeḥ।
﻿<pb n="b306"/>
idamaparaṃ kharparaṃ <q><quote>“sthita etasminnadhikaraṇe nāmadheyaṃ”</quote></q> na punarasyāṃ
cintāyāṃ karmavacanatvaṃ śyenāderupapadyate। yadā''khyātārthena vidhiḥ sādhyata
iti sthitaṃ tadā lakṣaṇābhayannāmadheyatvābhityuktam। ataḥ śyenādini-
vṛttyarthamabhidhānadvayaṃ śakyam। atrābhidhīyate। nedaṃ śakyaṃ yadi karma-
śabdebhya ityucyate idamevādhikaraṇaṃ sthitiṃ na labhate। sthāpyamānaṃ hyetajjyo-
tiṣṭomādeḥ karmaśabdatāmāvahati। ataśca na nāmākhyātayoḥ viśeṣo labhyate।
﻿<pb n="b307"/>
bhāvaśabdābhidhāne punaḥ siddhavatkarmābhidhānāt jyotiṣṭomādernivṛttiḥ।
sakarmake pūrvāparībhūte bhāvaśabdo vartata iti।</p>
<p>evaṃ tarhi bhāvaśabdā ityevāstu karmaśabdnagrahaṇamatiricyate। ida-
meva hi na labhyate pūrvāparībhūte sakarmake bhāvaśabdo vartata iti।
anyatrāpi darśanāt bhāvo bhavanaṃ bhūtiriti bhāvaśabdasya। kiṃ punarudāharaṇaṃ ?
﻿<pb n="b308"/>
<p>yadi śyenaikātrikādayo'pi karmaśabdā naivaṃ dravyaguṇaśabdānāṃ nivṛttyartha-
midaṃ sūtramupapadyate। sarvatrādhikāracodanāsu nāmaivopapadamupalabhyate।
tasmānnirviṣayaṃ sūtraṃ manvānaḥ kiṃ punarihodāharaṇamiti pṛcchati।</p>
﻿<pb n="r309"/>
kā vārtā etasyaiva revatīṣvityevamādiṣu ?। yathākhyātādṛte nānyasya
vidhyarthatā saṃbhavati tathā tatraiva vakṣyāmaḥ । evaṃ tarhi nāmopapadānye-
vātrodāharaṇāni ? । anenaiva sūtraiṇa nāmākhyātayoḥ vidhyarthatve
vivekaḥ । aviveke hi nāmataiva na syāta dravyaguṇaśabdataiva
syāt । tasmātsiddhaṃ dravyaguṇanivṛttyarthamudāharaṇam । ākhyā-
tikyo vibhaktayaḥ pūrvāparībhāvaṃ pratipādayantītyupariṣṭādvakṣyati ।
visadṛśavibhaktiyogācca jyotiṣṭomādeḥ na pūrvāparībhūtapratipādana---﻿<pb n="b310"/>
<q>nasāmarthyamastīti</q> na nāmadheyānāṃ vidhyarthatā। kintu ākhyātānāmeveti
<q>siddho vivekaḥ</q>। <q>atra keciccodayanti</q>। <q>nanu karmaśabdamātrāt mābhūdapūrvotpattirityupa-
padyata evaitatsūtram</q>। <q>enañca kimihodāharaṇamityevamādegrenthasyābhiprāyavarṇanamanarthakama</q>।
asyārthaḥ। yadi tāvat dravyaguṇaśabdā adhikāracodanāsu bhavanti tadā labdhamudāharaṇa-
miti nodāharaṇābhāvābhiprāyeṇodāharaṇapraśnoṣapattiḥ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b311"/>
<p>kathaṃ tarhi śyenaikatrikādayo nirasyante ? anākhyātārthatvādeva।
bhāvārthagrahaṇaṃ kimartham ? karmaśabdatve'pi abhāvārthatvena anākhyātārtha-
taiveti। tasmātsūktametat kimihodāharaṇamityevamādergrantha-
syopanyāsaḥ।</p>
<p><q>sarveṣāṃ bhāvo'rtha iti cet</q>। kimanena pūrvoktamākṣiptam ?
yatpūrvoktaṃ tadevākṣiptam। bhāvārthebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyata iti। sarveṣāṃ bhāvo'rtha
﻿<pb n="b312"/>
iti vadatā kathamidamākṣiptaṃ bhavati ? yadi hyabhāvārthānāmapūrvārthatāṃ vadet
tadā''kṣepaḥ saṃbhavati। sarveṣāṃ bhāvo'rtha iti vadato naiva dravyaguṇa-
śabdāḥ santītyabhiprāyo gamyate। na punardravyaguṇaśabdāḥ api
bhāvārthā iti śakyate pratipat‍tum। karmaśabdasāmānādhikaraṇyācca
viśeṣataḥ। ayamabhiprāyaścodakasya। dravyaguṇaśabdā api bhāva-
rūpāpannā eva vidhyarthā bhavanti।</p>
﻿<pb n="b313"/>
taccedaṃ dadhnā juhātītyatra pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ। evañcet sarveṣāṃ bhāvo'rthaḥ dravya-
guṇāvagatistu nāntarīyakyeva। tasmādabhidhānavanna svarūpataḥ kriyānvayo
dravyaguṇānām। tasmādbhāvārthā iti sūtraṃ na viśeṣāvagatāvalam।</p>
<p><q>yeṣāmutpattau</q>। satyaṃ sarveṣāṃ bhāvārthatā, kintvekasya svataḥ
anyasya tadyogāt। kimidaṃ tadyogāditi ? tadarthānupraveśādityarthaḥ।</p>

﻿<pb n="b314"/>
kathaṃ punaridamavagamyate---ekasya svataḥ, anyasya tadyogādanupraveśāditi ?
tatsvabhāvāt, ekasya hi siddha eva svabhāvaḥ, anyasya sādhyaḥ tatra na
sādhyatāmanyato'pekṣate। siddhiḥ punaḥ na sādhyayogāddate sādhyatayā pratipat‍tuṃ
śakyate। kiṃ jahatsvabhāvā sādhyānvayitā siddhasya ? bhavatu, ko doṣaḥ ?
ayameva doṣaḥ siddhataiva nāvagamyate। ananvitānāñcāyaṃ vivekaḥ sūtrakāreṇa
pradarśitaḥ। tasmānnamaḥ śabdavidbhayo yairayaṃ viveko niścīyate।</p>
﻿<pb n="b315"/>
yathāhācāryavān। kintu nimittagataiṣā kathā। nimittataśca kāryama-
kāryaṃveti parīkṣakaiḥ vaktavyam। tathā ceyaṃ yeṣāmutpattāviti bhagavatā
sūtrakāreṇa nimittāvasthopavarṇitā utpattiśabdaṃ prayuñjānena। yeṣāmutpattau
nimittāvasthāyāmityarthaḥ। nimittato hyakāṅkṣā cākhyātārthasyaiveti darśitam।﻿<pb n="b316"/>
kārye punaḥ kiṃ siddhasādhyaviveko nāsti ? asti tāvat
<q>āśritatvātprayogasyeti</q>। kimidamāśritatvātprayogarayeti ? ucyate।
bhāvārthānāmeva prayogaḥ puruṣeṇāśrita iti।</p>
﻿<pb n="b317"/>
<p>kimidaṃ bhāvārthānāmeva prayogaḥ puruṣeṇāśrita iti ? yāvatā
dravyaguṇānāmapi kimiti nāśrita iti ? nimittāśritattvātkāryasya,
yathānimittamavabhāsate। tadidaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa <note n="1">p. 316</note>kiñcetyuk‍tvā kāryā-
dapyevaṃbhūtanimittataiveti pratipāditam, sākṣepanirapekṣatvātkāryāvagataḥ﻿<pb n="b318"/>
kva sāpekṣatvaṃ kva vā nirapekṣatvamuktam ? siddhasādhyayoḥ sādhyasyānapekṣatvaṃ
vidhyarthe sādhyaviṣayatvāt niyogasya। sādhyāpekṣitā ca siddharayeti
guṇavidhau darśayiṣyāma ityuktam। eṣa vinigamanāyāṃ hetuḥ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b319"/>
<q>codanā। kathaṃ punaridamavagamyate asti tadapūrvamiti</q> ?
nanu cāyaṃ praśno nopapadyate, apūrva hi vidhyarthaḥ। vidhitaśca prāmāṇya-
mityuktam। kathaṃ tadākṣepa upapadyate। atrocyate। ayamabhi-
prāyaścodakasya। niyogo hi karmaṇi puruṣaṃ niyuṅkte na svārthe।</p>
﻿<pb n="b320"/>
karma cānityam। na ca svargādyanantaramupalabhyate। tasmādyāgasya varaṃ
nityatvaṃ kalpayitavyam। ātmano vā saṃskāraḥ kaścita, devatāprasādo vā
na punastenāpūrvaṃ kṛtvetyetatsuktamiva pratibhāti।</p>
﻿<pb n="b321"/>
atrābhidhīyate---niyogaḥ karmāṇi puruṣaṃ niyuṅkta iti
na samyagavadhṛtaṃ bhavatā। ārambhe hi puruṣaṃ niyuṅkte na
karmaṇi। ārambhaviṣayaṃ hi karma। sa cārambho vidhyarthaḥ।
﻿<pb n="b322"/>
svargakāmasya cāsāvityārambhāt svarga iti। brūmaḥ। karmaṇāñcā---
rambhaḥ। karmādinityatvaparikalpanā punaḥ pramāṇāntaraviruddhaiva;
animittā ca ārambhe pratyārthini। kathaṃ punaḥ pramāṇāntaravirodhaḥ ?</p>
﻿<pb n="b323"/>
bhaṅgitvaṃ hi karmaṇāṃ prasiddhameva। kṣaṇāntarānupalambhācca। ātmanaśca
niṣkriyatvaṃ sarvagatatvādātmanaḥ। puroḍāśādeśca karmavadvināśadarśanāt।
saukṣmyādeśca viśeṣasya ārambhe pratyarthini nāsti kalpanetyuktam।
darśitaṃ tadbhāṣyakāreṇa sāmānyakalpanāyāṃ pramāṇaṃ na viśeṣakalpanā---
yāmiti।</p>
﻿<pb n="b324"/>
<p><q>tāni dvaidham। avagatametadbhāvaśabdāḥ pradhānakarmaṇo bācakā iti</q>।
kva punaridamavagatam ? bhāvaśabdāḥ pradhānakarmaṇo vācakā iti
bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā ityetatsamadhigatam। karmaṇaḥ pūrvāparībhūtasya
﻿<pb n="b325"/>
vācakā iti। na punaḥ prādhānyaṃ kacinnirdiṣṭam। athāyamabhiprāyaḥ
itarattadarthamiti vadatā nāmarthaṃ pratyākhyātārthasya prādhānyamuktamiti।
tadayuktam। svargakāmapadārthaṃ prati guṇabhāvadarśanāt। tathocoktam
---te svargakāmapadasaṃbandhāt svargaṃ bhāvayediti brūyuriti। tasmānna vidmaḥ
kimidaṃ <quote>‘avagatametadbhāvaśabdāḥ pradhānakarmaṇo vācakā’</quote> iti। atrā-
bhidhīyate---prādhānyaṃ hi niyogaviṣayatvamabhipretam। kutaḥ ? viṣayatvādeva।
﻿<pb n="b326"/>
viṣayatayā hi yāgādayaḥ pratīyante niyogārthasya। na kasyaci-
dutpattyādyarthatayā। taduktaṃ <quote>“adhikāralakṣaṇe vakṣyāmaḥ”</quote> iti।
tasmāda‍yuktamuktametadavagatamiti। cintā copapadyate---kiṃ sarvāṇyeva
niyogaviṣayatayā pratīyante ? utotpattyādyarthatayāpi keciditi।
﻿<pb n="b327"/>
yuktaṃ tāvata keṣāñcidutpattyādyarthatā kalpayitum yadyaivaṃbhūtānāmapi
niyogasaṃsparśitepapadyate; na tu tadadyāpi nirṇīyate। atha tu
nirṇayaheturasti tato na sarvasyāpūrvārthatā nyāyyā। <quote>“evamalpīyasya-
dṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanā nyāyyā”</quote> iti bhāṣyam। tatpunarasaṅgatārtha-
miti pratibhāti। niyogārthatvepi hi naivādṛṣṭakalpanā। ucyate।
﻿<pb n="b328"/>
parihṛtametat evamalpoyasyadṛṣṭānumānaprasaṅgakalpanetyatra। nanu yuktaṃ
tatra pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭakriyāniṣpattiparityāgena nāmārthānāṃ śabdato niyogasya
niṣpādakatvam। evamapyupapadyamāne na yuktamiti। atrāpi tulyaṃ kriyāntara-
sādhanotpādyarthatayā sambhavati śabde na niyogasādhanatā yuktā। nanu ca
niyogaśūnyānāṃ niyogaviṣayasādhanotpattyādyarthataiva nāvasīyate। na cāvihi-
tamaṅgaṃ bhavatīti vakṣyati। satyaṃ niyogādṛte nāṅgatā। astyevātra niyogaḥ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b329"/>
na ca niyogārthateti tṛtīye vakṣyāmaḥ। ke punaraste bhāvārthāḥ ?
ya eva loke cikīrṣitotpattyādyarthatayā prasiddhā darśitā bhāṣyakāreṇa।
prayojanamapyuktam।</p>
<p><q>dharmamātre tu karma syādanirvṛtteḥ prayājavat</q>। uktamajahātkriyā-
kārakasambandha eva niyogasambandhaḥ। kārakāṇāṃ bhāvārthānāñca
cikīrṣitārthānām। ihedānīṃ yatra dṛṣṭaḥ saṃskāro nopa-
labhyate cikīrṣitapratipādikā ca vibhaktirasti tatrāpi kimajahatkriyā-
﻿<pb n="b330"/>
kārakasambandhaiva niyogārthatā, uta yāgāderiva niyogaviṣayataiva dhātvartha-
syeti। kiṃ punaratra yuktam ? dṛṣṭasyābhāvānniyogasiddhirevāvaśiṣyate।
tasmāt prayājādivanniyogārthataiva sammārgādeḥ।</p>
<p>nanu ca cikīrṣitārthapratipādikā dvitīyāvibhaktiravivakṣitā bhavati।
na ceyamaikāntikī। balbajān śikhaṇḍakān kurvityevamādiṣu vyabhicārāt।
﻿<pb n="b331"/>
vede'pi sak‍tūn juhotīti। tasmāt karaṇārthepi asyāḥ prayogo
dṛṣṭaḥ। tulyaśrutitvāccetaraiḥ sarvadharmaḥ syāt। ucyate। yattāvalloke
vyabhicāradarśanamupanyastam---tadayuktam। loke hi vivakṣātaḥ kārakāṇi
bhavanti। vivakṣā ca puruṣavaśānuvartinīṃ। ataḥ cikīrṣitavibhaktidarśa-
nāt tathaiva vivakṣeti yuktaṃ prativak‍tum। vede tu katham ? uktamasmābhiḥ
﻿<pb n="b332">
kāryarthatayā prāmāṇyam। iha cikīrṣitārthāparityāgena niyoga-
saṃsparśitā na śakyate vak‍tum। kriyāntarasādhanatvenāśravaṇāt
sak‍tūnām। na ca saktavo niyogauk‍yenetikartavyatābhāvaṃ pratipat‍tuṃ
kṣamāḥ। kimiti niyogauk‍yaṃ na bhavati। abhāvārthatvāt sak‍tūnām।
﻿<pb n="b333">
kāryārthasya hi karaṇāṃśopanipātitā, kimityaṃśopanipātitā vā।
ato nānubandhabhāvaḥ। bhinnānubandhānāñca kimityaṃśabhāva evaik‍yam।
bhidyate cātra kimityaṃśabhāvaḥ। ato naik‍yaṃ vidheḥ। anekatvācca neti---
kartavyatā saktavaḥ। tasmādalaukiko'yaṃ cikīrṣitārthasaṃyogaḥ, cikīrṣita-
tvena sak‍tūnāmanavagamāt। na caitāvatā vyabhicāritā śak‍yate vak‍tuṃ
﻿<pb n="b334">
dvitīyāyāḥ। yāvaddarśanabhāvī hi chāndasaḥ prayogaḥ। tathā ca vyākhyā-
tāro dṛṣṭānuvidhiśchandasītyupadiśanti। ata eva ca bhagavatā sūtrakāreṇa
tṛtīyā ca hośchandasi iti tṛtīyārthe chandasi dvitīyā dṛṣṭetyuktam।
﻿<pb n="b335">
ata evopapadavibhaktitulyaiṣā। tasmādajahatsvārthavṛttitvānniyogārthasya
cikīrṣitārthaiveyaṃ <quote>“grahaṃ sammārṣṭi”</quote> <quote>“vrīhīn prokṣatī”</quote>ti dvitīyā।
nanu ca dṛṣṭo'rtho nāstītyuktam। niyogārthasya sādhyatvaṃ na cikīrṣi-
﻿<pb n="b336">
tārtheṣu sambhavatītyapyuktam। na cānyat pramāṇamasti yena kāryakalpanā
syāt। cikīrṣitārthābhidhānāt। niyogārthasaṃraparśitvācca siddhamadṛṣṭa-
kāryatvaṃ lokavat kāryāntarasaṃyogāt। loke'pi kāryāntarayogitvāt
ha/?/styādīnāṃ siddhaṃ nīrājanāderadṛṣṭārthatvaṃ prayojanam। varuṇapradhāseṣu śrūyate
---śamīmayyaḥ sruco bhavanti hiraṇmayyo veti। prakṛtau nānāvṛkṣīya-
﻿<pb n="b337"/>
sruk‍sammārgavyaḍagyamapūrvamiti nānāvṛkṣīyāḥ sruva utpādayitavyāḥ
sammārgārthena yathā pūrvapakṣaḥ। yathā tarhi siddhāntaḥ śamīmayya eva
hiraṇmayyo vā sammārjayitavyāḥ। tathā paridhyādiṣu।</p>
<p>nanu ca pūrvapakṣe'pyaṅgapradhānārthametadvidhānaṃ bhaviṣyati barhirvat।
naivam। yatra hyaṅgapradhānārtha evopadeśavidhiḥ kāryavidhirapi tathaiva tatra।
﻿<pb n="b338"/>
yatra punarupadeśe vidhibhedaḥ kāryavidhirapi tatra prakaraṇāt pradhānasyaiva
darśitam---<quote>‘ānarthakyāttadaṅgeṣu’</quote> iti। yatra hi pradhānasya tatkāryaṃ
na bhavati tatrānarthakyāttadaṅgānām। yatra punaḥ sambhavati tatra
﻿<pb n="b339"/>
pradhānārtha eva iti prakṛtatvādityuktam। yathā sahasradakṣiṇādayaḥ pradhānada-
kṣiṇāsu। nodāharaṇamādaraṇīyaṃ madhvaśanādiṣu darśanāt।</p>
﻿<pb n="b340"/>
<p><q>stutaśastrayoḥ</q>।। atrāpi sa eva saṃśayaḥ। kintu stuta-
śastrayoḥ cikīrṣitārthatvamuta vidhiviṣayataiveti। nanu cikīrṣitārthatve stutya-
rtho'pi hīyate stauti śaṃsatīti ca tadarthābhidhānam। tasmāt nātra saṃśayaṃ
﻿<pb n="b341"/>
paśyāmaḥ। ajahatsvārthe tṛṣṇayā hi cikīrṣitārthatvaṃ gṛhyate। viparī-
tañca tadatra। athāyamabhiprāyaḥ paśupuroḍāśavat; yāgasya sato
devatārthatvam। devatārthatve ca cīkīrṣitārthatvam। na ca yajyartho-
'pauti। tasmādatrāpi stutereva devatāsmaraṇaṃ yajeriva prayojanaṃ bhaviṣya-
tīti। viṣama upanyāsaḥ। tatra hi devatāsādhanako yāgaḥ।
ato'jahatsvārthavṛttitvaṃ yujyate yajeḥ। na devatāsaṃskāratve kaścidvirodhaḥ।
iha punaḥ stutiḥ stutyamapekṣate na devatām। evañca devatārthatve
hīyeta stutyarthaḥ। nanu stutibhājo'pi devā iti devatāvidaḥ
﻿<pb n="b342"/>
devatā cetsāmyaṃ paśupuroḍāśena। maivaṃ vocaḥ। ghoṭārūḍhasya vismṛto
ghoṭa iti। stutibhājaśca devatā iti bravīṣi। havirbhājaśca saṃskāraṃ
manyase। puroḍāśe tvavibhāgād‍yuktam। tasmānnātra pūrvapakṣaṃ paśyāmaḥ। aya-
﻿<pb n="b343"/>
mevātra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ। stautiḥ stutyārtheti, na cācikīrṣitaḥ stutyaḥ।
yāgasambandhitvenābhidheyābhedāt। na punaḥ puroḍāśavaddevatābhedā-
diti brūmaḥ। tatra devatāpratyabhijñānamevābhipretam। tacca tatraiva
pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ। atra tvabhidhānābhedamātreṇaivājahatsvārthavṛttimupapadyata
iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate।</p>﻿<pb n="b344"/>
<p>itarastu codayati yadyevaṃ māhendrasya grahṛyajeḥ sannidhau
aindrīstutistatraikābhidhānābhāvāt na cikīrṣitārthā syāt। utkarṣo
vā kalpanīyaḥ। ucyate। notkarṣaḥ kalpanīyaḥ। indra eva
hi mahendraḥ abhinnārthābhidhānaṃ hi sāmānādhikaraṇyamucyate।</p>
<p>nanu ca nīlotpalamiti bhinnārthāvagateḥ kathamabhinnārthābhidhānam;
bhinnārthābhidhāne vā kathaṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyam ? utpalagata-
﻿<pb n="b345"/>
guṇābhidhānāditi brūmaḥ। āgato'si tarhi madīyaṃ panthānam।
tatra prayuktaḥ tada‍‍guṇābhidhānasamartho bhavati। yatra ca śabdaḥ
prayujyate tamācaṣṭe। ata eva ca guṇamabhidhāya guṇini pravartante
ye guṇaśabdāsta iha gṛhyante guṇavacanatayeti samāsapratiṣedha
uktaḥ। tasmātsiddhamekābhidhānam। guṇāvagatirhi sāmānādhikaraṇye
﻿<pb n="b346"/>
vājinasthānīyā। ataścikīrṣitārthatvaṃ stuteraindryāḥ। tadidamayuktam।
nirasto'yamarthaḥ ananvito'pyavasīyata iti। kārye tu kadācidanveti
kadācinneti। avagatau punaḥ na taṭasthaṃ padārthāvabodhanamityuk‍tam।</p>
﻿<pb n="b347"/>
mābhūttadarthāvagatau। kārye punaruttarapadārthapradhānatvāt samāsasya indra eva
kāryabhāk anyathā hyanupapannaiva śabdavidāṃ vāgiyaṃ <quote>“uttarapadārthapradhāno'yaṃ
samāsaḥ ayaṃ pūrvapadārthapradhāna”</quote> iti। kiñcijjño devānāṃ priyaḥ। samāso
hi nāma parasparānugamapūrvakaṃ padārthāntarānugamanam, tatrāpi kadācit
﻿<pb n="b348"/>
pūrvaṃ padaṃ uttaramanveti। kadāciduttaraṃ pūrvam। kimidamanvetīti ?
idamidaṃ idamāśrityāyaṃ padārtho'rthāntarānvayībhavatīti। tataḥ kim ?
idaṃ tato bhavati। nānabhidhānataiva sthāsyati saguṇasyānvayāt।
atha mataṃ arthāntarasaṃbandhaḥ punaḥ arthāntareṇa saṃbadhyata iti।﻿<pb n="b349"/>
uk‍taṃ parasparānvaye samāsaḥ। tato'rthāntarānvayaḥ। tasmānnārthāntarākṣepasya
samāsaḥ। na ca samastasya kevalasyārthāntarasaṃbandhaḥ। ataḥ saguṇadevatā
na kevalenābhadhātuṃ śak‍yate। bhavati vai pradhānasya sāpekṣasyāpi samāsa iti
samāsavidāṃ giraḥ śrūyante। pradhānaṃ cendrārthaḥ। ato dravyasaṃbandhasyāpi
﻿<pb n="b350"/>
mahatvamupapadyate। na samyagavadhṛtaṃ bhavatā samāsavidvacaḥ। padārthā---
ntarasaṃbandhapradhānasya samastasyāpi samāso niruṇaddhīti tasyārthaḥ, na punaḥ
samāsapadanirapekṣasyārthāntarasaṃbandha iti। nanu cāsamarthasamāsā api
vyākhyātṛbhiruditāḥ। satyaṃ, udito yatra tatraiva te bhavantu। atra
punaḥ samarthaḥ padavidhirityetadeva nyāyyam। asāmarthyādarśanāt।
﻿<pb n="b351"/>
nana cedamevāsāmarthyam māhendro grahayajiḥ aindrī stutiriti। evaṃ cāja-
hatsvārthatopapannā। evamitaretarāśrayaṃ prāpnoti। cikīrṣitārthatve mahe-
ndrasya asāmarthyaṃ, asāmarthye cikīrṣitārthatvamiti। itaretarāśrayāṇi
﻿<pb n="b352"/>
na prakalpyanta ityuktam। yadyevamasamarthasamāso'pi na prāpnoti।
prādhānye bhāvārthasya sāmarthyaṃ sāmarthye ca prādhānyamiti। maivaṃ vocaḥ
abhidhānataḥ sāmarthyāvagateḥ tasmāt saguṇaiva devatā। avaśyaṃ
caitadevamavagantavyam। anyathā guṇavacanamasaṃsparśi syāt। na
ca saṃbhavantyāṃ gatau tad‍yuktam। tasmādutkarṣa eva prāpnoti।
bhavatu tarhi utkarṣaḥ। naitāvatā cikīrṣitārthatvaṃ tyak‍tuṃ śak‍yate।
﻿<pb n="b353"/>
atantre hi kramasannidhī vipakṣabhūte sāmarthye। nanu cotkarṣe sati bahūnāṃ
mantrāṇāṃ niṣprayojanatā prāpnoti maṇḍūkasūktādīnām। na niṣprayojanatā,
yasya yatrārthaḥ sa tatra yātīti darśitaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa। kathaṃ punarvācasteme
āśvine ca sāmarthya bhinnārthānāṃ ? vacanādekārthatā bhaviṣyati aindrīvat।
api vā śrutisaṃyogāt। api ca na stautiśaṃsatī cikīrṣitārthau bhavataḥ।
﻿<pb n="b354"/>
kasmāt ? devatāpratyabhijñānābhāvāt। nanu cābhidhānataḥ pratyabhi-
jñānamuditam। tadayuktam yatra hi pramāṇāntareṇa pratyabhijñānamasti
tadevedamiti tatrābhidhānaṃ na bhedārthaṃ bhavitumarhati tathā ca darśitaṃ
---<q>vaśāyāmarthasamavāyāditi</q>। yatra punaḥ abhidhānādeva pratyabhi-
jñānaṃ tatra yāgānvayī stutyanvayīti na śakyate pratipat‍tum।
﻿<pb n="b355"/>
na cānanviyino'bhidhānamastīti tatra tatrok‍tam। tasmānna cikīrṣitā-
rthatvaṃ stauteḥ śaṃsateśca। ato niyogaviṣayataivāvasīyate। ata evāmī
śrutisaṃyogā darśitā bhāṣyakāreṇa stuteḥ prādhānyāvagamahetavaḥ। kathaṃ punaḥ
prādhānyāvagamahetavaḥ saptamīsaṃyogo hi abhidhāne'pi tulyaḥ। na, abhi-
dhānasya parārthatvāt। abhidheyabhāvasthaṃ hyabhidhānaṃ stutau punaḥ stutyārtham।
﻿<pb n="b356"/>
tacca stutyaṃ kavatīṣveva nānyatra pramāṇāntarānavagamāt। ataḥ kavatīṣu
stuvata iti yuktam। na cātra puruṣavaśāt vivakṣātaḥ kārakā-
bhidhānaṃ śakyate vak‍tum। kathaṃ tarhi ? abhidhānata eva। taccā-
bhidhānaṃ kavatīsthamityuktam। tathā dvitīyāśrutisaṃyogaḥ prādhānya-
mutsargāt gamayati। anyato hi guṇabhāvo vaktavyaḥ।
tathā indrasya nu vīryāṇīti nābhidhāne paryavasānamiti kathayati।
﻿<pb n="b357"/>
prathamā punarliḍādyabhihite hi padārtha upapadyate। evamajahatsvārthatā ca stuteḥ
prāpnoti stutyābhidhānāditi pradarśitam। <q>śabdapṛthak‍tvāditi</q> śāstra-
pṛthak‍tvaṃ ca darśayati। tasya viṣayabhūte bhāvārtha upapadyate na tu guṇabhūte,
niyogaśūnyatvāditi pradarśitam। niyogaśūnyatvaṃ ca tṛtīye vakṣyāma
﻿<pb n="b358"/>
ityapyuktam। kiñcāgniṣ‍ṭuti āgneyīvidhānāt pradhānārthataiva gamyate।
guṇapakṣe hi kāryata eva prāpnoti। <q>anyaścārthaḥ pratīyata iti</q>।
anenāpi śāstrabheda eva kathyate। iyāṃstu viśeṣaḥ pūrvatra svataḥ।
iha tu saṃbandhopādhikaḥ। <quote>“pradhānakarmavadabhidhānaṃ”</quote> iti pradhānasyaivocitaṃ
﻿<pb n="b359"/>
nāmeti kathayati। kutaḥ ? bhedāvagamāt। guṇakarmaṇāṃ bhedo nāstīti
somaṃ kīṇātītyatra darśayiṣyāmaḥ। bhedānupāti ca nāma। tasmādanucitaṃ
guṇakarmaṇāṃ bhinnaṃ nāma। phalanirvṛttiṃ ca karmaṇaḥ sakāśāddarśayati
na cikīrṣitāt devatātaḥ। tasmādacikīrṣitārthatvaṃ siddham। prayojanaṃ
tvanyatretyuk‍taṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa।</p>
﻿<pb n="b360"/>
<p><q>vidhimantrayoraikārthyamaikaśabdyāt। kiṃ yadvad‍brāhmaṇe bhāva-
śabdo vidhāyakaḥ tadvanmantreṣvapi, uta tanmantre'vidhāyaka iti</q>।
kimidamupanyastam ? nanu na śrutaṃ bhavatā yadupanyastam। satyaṃ śrutaṃ
kintu asambaddhamiva pratibhāti। kathamasambaddham ? viniyukto hi
mantra iti sthitam। prayogasamavāyī ca mantraḥ smaraṇenopayujyata iti
sthitam। ataḥ kā'tra vidhāyakāśaṅkā ? atha manyase niyoga-
﻿<pb n="b361"/>
śravaṇāt bhavatyāśaṅketi tadapi nirākṛtaṃ <quote>‘ya evaṃ vidvān paurṇamāsīṃ yajata’</quote>
ityekārthatāvagamāt। evaṃ tarhi ekārthatayaiva vidhāyakatāśaṅkā brāhmaṇaprati-
pāditamarthaṃ mantro'bhidhatta iti। ato'bhinnārthatvāt abhinnāthasya vidhāna---
mābhidhānaṃ ca na sambhavatīti pūrvapakṣaḥ। arthataścaikatvaṃ nānātvaṃ na śabdā-
nām। nanu caivamabhidhāyakatvaṃ hīyate mantrāṇāṃ samidādīnāmiva parasparam।
﻿<pb n="b362"/>
ucyate---naitat। tannimittatvādvidheḥ। nimittaṃ hi vidhirna bādhata iti
nyāyavidbhiruk‍tam। ataḥ siddhamaviśeṣāt dvayorvidhāyakatvam।</p>
<p><q>api vā prayogasāmarthyāt</q>। ucyate। abhidhāyakatayā hyekārtha-
tvaṃ mantrasya pratipannam। kasyābhidhāyakatayā ? vihitasya। na ca
vihitābhidhāne vidhānaṃ śakyate। vidhāne hi karmāntarāpattiḥ।
﻿<pb n="b363"/>
karmāntaratve vā anabhidhāyakatvaṃ samidādīnāmiva parasparam। tataśca
viniyogaśruteḥ bādhaḥ। bhavatviti cet na, abhidhāyakatayā hi niyoga-
saṃsparśasiddheḥ। tasmānna niyogāntaramarhati। <q>stutyarthatāyāmapyanarthakya-
miti। keyamakāṇḍe stutyarthatāśaṅkā</q>। ucyate---stutāvapi vihitābhidhānaṃ﻿<pb n="b364"/>
dṛṣṭam। tataḥ kim ? ekavākyatāyāmevaitadupapannaṃ, vihitābhidhānaṃ nāma
na vākyabhede, abhinnaṃ ca vidhivākyānmantravākyam। tasmādābhidhāyakatva-
mupapādayituṃ duśśakam। nanu ca viniyogena vihitābhidhāyakatvam।
ucyate---aidamarthye hi prabhaviṣṇutā viniyogasya nedaṃ kāryatve। satyam।
﻿<pb n="b365"/>
yatra padanibandhanamekavākyatvaṃ tatra śrutyaiva vihitābhidhānam। iha punaḥ
upādānataḥ। tasmānna stutiḥ saṃbhavati। padanibandhanottarakālabhāvitvāt।
ato bhinnavākyānāmapi bhavati vihitābhidhāyakatvam। idaṃ
kāryatve hya‍upādānaṃ bhavati। tasmātsiddhaṃ vihitābhidhānaṃ mantrāṇāṃ
kāryam।</p>
<p><q>taccodakeṣu mantrākhyā। uktaṃ mantragato bhāvaśabdo'bhi-
dhāyaka iti</q>। abhidhāyako na vidhāyaka ityetāvadvak‍tavyam।
﻿<pb n="b366"/>
kiṃ mantraśabdena ? na ca mantraśabdābhidheyatayā । kathaṃ tarhīṣetvetye-
vamādibhiḥ pratīkaiḥ ? tasmānmantraśabdābhidhānamatiricyata itīva prati-
bhāti । kriyamāṇe'pi mantraśabdābhidhāne na mantratvādabhidhāyakatvaṃ,
vidhāyakatvamapi mantreṣu vasantāya kapiñjalanālabhata ityevamādiṣu
dṛṣṭam ।</p>
<p>yadapi bhāṣyakāreṇoktam&mdash;<q>ajñāte mantraśabde tadrato bhāva-
śabdaḥ kathaṃ vicāryo bhaviṣyati ? idamarthato'dhikaraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ draṣṭa-
vyamiti ।</q> etadapyayuktamiva । na mantratvādabhidhāyakatvaṃ; kiṃ tarhi ?
viniyuktatvāditi । viniyogaśca iṣetyevamādibhiḥ pratīkaiḥ ityuktam ।﻿<pb n="b367"/>
anyathāpi cāyaṃ sūtrārthoṃ gacchatyeva। mantraśabdo'bhidhāyakeṣu pūrva-
sminnadhikaraṇe prayuktaḥ। tadvayākhyānārthamabhidhāyakeṣu kiṃ mantraśabdā---
bhidhānamasti। bāḍhamasti। taccodakeṣu mantraśabdamabhiyuk‍tāḥ prayuñjate।
evaṃ ca <quote>“prāyikaṃ”</quote> ityetadapi na vak‍tavyam। mantrābhidhānaprasiddhi-
kathanārthamityetatsūtraṃ na mantralakṣaṇaparam। <quote>“lakṣaṇena tu siddhānāṃ”</quote> ityeva-
mādyasamañjasameva। tasmādavyāpitālakṣaṇadoṣakathanena svakauśalapradarśa-
nārthaṃ lakṣaṇasūtratvamadhyāropyate। atrabhidhīyate---bhāṣyakārasyāpi pūrvoktamantra-
padavyākhyānamevaitadabhiyuktā upadiśanti। <q>mantrā āvartanta iti vadataḥ
﻿<pb n="b368"/>
padārthakathanaparaṃ caitadbhāṣyam। ato yadanyat tallakṣaṇadūṣaṇaparameva।
prāyikametaditi prakaṭitam। ata eva vṛttikārodāharaṇaprapañcoktirapi
naiva mṛṣyate bhāṣyakāreṇa। lakṣaṇābhidhānapakṣe hi lakṣaṇaviśeṣābhidhāna-
mupapadyetāpi। padārthavyākhyāne punaḥ anavasara eva tallakṣaṇaviśeṣābhidhānasya।
taccaitat vṛttikāreṇodāharaṇāpadeśeneti vadatā asaṃbaddhataiva kathitā।
tasmānmantrapadārthakathanamevaitat sūtraṃ na mantralakṣaṇaparam।</p>
﻿<pb n="b369"/>
﻿<pb n="b370"/>
<p><q>śeṣe brāhmaṇaśabdaḥ ।</q> taccodakeṣu mantrākhyeti mantraśabdārthakathanapare
sūtre kaḥ punaḥ prasaṅgaḥ śeṣe brāhmaṇaśabda iti । lakṣaṇapare punaḥ sūtramupapa-
dyata eva, lakṣaṇapare'pyuk‍to doṣaḥ । ato na vidmaḥ kathamidamiti । atro-
cyate&mdash;śabdārthakathanaparamevaitatsūtradvayaṃ vidhimantrayoraikārthyamiti । kimidaṃ﻿<pb n="b371"/>
vidhimantrāvityāśaṅkyate ? astīdaṃ dvayaṃ vede kecinmantrāḥ
kiñcida‍brāhmaṇamiti । yatrābhiyuktā mantraśabdaṃ prayuñjate sa mantraḥ । yatra
ca vidhiriti ca bruvate tad‍brāhmaṇam । vṛttikāramatopanyāsastu pūrvavat
draṣṭavyaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b372"/>
<p><q>anāmnāteṣvamantratvam ।</q> ūhapravaranāmadheyāni cintyante&mdash;kiṃ
mantraśabdābhilapyānyetāni uta neti । nanu taccodakeṣu mantrākhyeti
yatrābhiyuktā mantraśabdaṃ prayuñjate sa mantra ityuktam । na cābhidhāya-
katvaṃ mantratve lakṣaṇam । na cohādīnyabhiyuk‍taiḥ mantratvenābhilapyante
tasmādanupapannaḥ saṃśayaḥ । atrābhidhīyate&mdash;ūhapravaranāmadheyairhi
kratuṣu mantrakāryaṃ kriyate । na cāmantraiḥ mantrakāryaṃ niṣpadyata iti
pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ । rāddhāntavādītu manyate-satyaṃ amantraiḥ mantrakāryaṃ
na bhavati na punaramantrānugṛhītaiḥ mantraiḥ । ūhapravaranāmadheyāni ca mantrāṇā-﻿<pb n="b373"/>
mupakāraṃ kurvanti santyanugrāhakāṇi prayat‍nakaraṇādivat । na
cānugrāhakaṃ mantraśabdābhilapyaṃ prayatnakaraṇamiva । tasmādamantratvam । kaḥ
punarebhiranugraho mantrasyeti ? yathaiva tālvādibhirarthābhidhāne sāhāyyam ।</p>
<p>nanu cohapravaranāmadheyāni svayamabhidhānaṃ kurvanti na sāhāyyam ।
na khalvatra kaścidviśeṣaḥ । kecita pradhānakārye upakurvanti kecidaṅga-
kārye । yathā svamisaṃskārāḥ prayājādayaśca । tasmādupapannamamantratvaṃ
svāmisaṃskārāṇāmiva na prādhānyam । prayojanaṃ bhāṣyoktam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b374"/>
<p><q>teṣāmṛgyatnārthavaśena pādavyavasthā ।</q> kena prasaṅgenedamāyātaṃ ?
anenedamāyātam । mantrabrāhmaṇaśabdayoḥ vedābhidheyasyārthasya vācya&mdash;
tayā niyama uktaḥ । ṛgādiśabdaiśca vyavahāro dṛśyate vedaśabdābhi-
dheyārtha eva । ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmānīti ṛgyajussāmaśabdairevābhidadhati ।
ataḥ ko bhāgaḥ ṛkśabdenocyate ? ko vā yajuśśabdena ? ko vā
sāmaśabdeneti ? tatra ṛkśabdābhidheyapradarśanārthamidamārabdham ।</p>﻿<pb n="b375"/>
<p>yatra pādavyavasthā sa ṛk‍śabdābhidheyo'rtha iti nirūpitam ।
arthagrahaṇaṃ tvanuvāda ityuktaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa । kaḥ punarayaṃ pādo nāma ?
gāyatryādīnāṃ chandasāṃ bhāgasammito'kṣarasamūhaḥ pādaḥ ।<p>
<p><q>gītiṣu sāmākhyā ।</q> pragīte mantraḥ sāmeti vaktavye gītiṣu sāmākhye
tyucyate । kathaṃ nāma rathantarādayaḥ sāmaviśeṣaśabdāḥ gītiviśeṣasya
﻿<pb n="b376"/>
vācakāḥ syuriti । nanu ca gītimātre nābhiyuktāḥ sāma-
śabdaṃ prayuñjate, yato rathantaramadhīṣvetyuktaḥ sarkāmeva gītimadhīte na gīti-
mātram । nākṣarāntareṣvavasthitam । nākṣarāntareṣvapyanyatra vacanāt ।
athāyamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;na ca padaśūnyaṃ gītakamastīti; sarkā hi gītiḥ
sāmaśabdavācyā । gītisvarūpābhivyak‍tyarthamakṣaropādānamiti cet viparītaṃ﻿<pb n="b377"/>
tat, akṣarābhivyañjikā hi gītiriti vakṣyāmaḥ । ato gītimātra-
vacanatve pratibhāmātraṃ sūtrakārasya ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate&mdash;anvayavyatirekāvagamyaṃ hi padapadārthanirūpaṇam ।
tatra yā abhivatī ṛk‍samāmnāye paṭhyate sā na rathantaraśabdābhilapyā । kiñca
rathantarabuddherutpādikā gītiḥ । na punaḥ ṛgeva ṛgādiṣvapi prayujyamānā
adhyetdṛṇāṃ rathantarabuddhimutpādayati । bruvate ca rathantaramanena ślokena
na gītamiti । tasmāt sūktaṃ gītiṣu sāmākhyeti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b378"/>
<p><q>śeṣe yajuḥ śabdaḥ ।</q> gītipādabaddhābhyāṃ yadanyanmantvajātaṃ tadyajuḥ
anayoḥ yallakṣaṇaṃ tacchūnyataiva lakṣaṇaṃ yajuṣaḥ । kathitaḥ trividho mantraḥ
ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmānīti ।</p>
<p><q>nigado vā caturthaṃ syāt ।</q> uktaṃ ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmānīti
trividhā mantrāḥ । ayamaparaḥ caturtho vyapadeśaḥ śrūyate nigadā iti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b379"/>
evamadhyetāro vyapadiśanti nigadā vartante na yajūṃṣi, yajūṃṣi vartante na
nigadā iti । upāṃśutvena prayogo neṣyate nigadānām । kimiti﻿<pb n="b380"/>
neṣyate ? vacanāt । kāryasyāsiddherneṣyata iti syāt, na; vacanapūrvakatvāt
kāryasya । ata evedaṃ caturthaṃ mantrajātamiṣyate । mābhūt kāryavirodho vacanasya﻿<pb n="b381"/>
ajahatsvārthaṃ vacanamiti sthitam । nanu coccairnigadenetyapi vacana-
masti । ayamaparo doṣaḥ avibhāge hi vikalpaḥ prāpnoti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b382"/>
tasmāt siddhaṃ nigado vā caturthaṃ syāditi । atrābhidhīyate । nedaṃ caturthaṃ
mantrajātam । yajūṃṣyeva nigadāḥ apādabaddhatvādapragītatvācca । vyapadeśaścaiva-
mupapadyate । yaduktaṃ vyapadeśādanyatvamiti tat prakarṣābhidhānātparihṛtam । yadu-
ktamupāṃśutvaṃ vacanāditi tadapyuccairnigadeneti prakarṣābhidhānopapatteḥ parihṛtam﻿<pb n="b383"/>
gobalīvardavat । na coccaiṣṭ‍vaina ṛk‍tvaṃ apādabaddhatvādityuktam । tasmāt
siddhaṃ ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmānīti ।</p>
<p><q>arthaikatvādekaṃ vākyam ।</q> uktaṃ triprakāro mantra iti ।
pāṭhādeva jñātaparimāṇaṃ dvividhaṃ mantrajātam । yajūṃṣi punaḥ pāṭhāt
parimāṇataḥ na śakyante jñātuṃ kiyadekaṃ yajuriti।</p>﻿<pb n="b384"/>
<p>nanu viniyogādyajūṃṣyapi jñātuṃ śak‍yante parimāṇataḥ । iṣetvetyā-
c‍chinatti ūrjetvetyanumārṣṭi iti । maivam । viniyogāddhi tādarthyamava-
sīyate na parimāṇam tadartho'yaṃ prayāsaḥ jñātaparimāṇaviniyogādaidamarthyam ।
nanu ceti śabdaḥ pūrvoktasya karaṇatāmāpādayati । kasya pūrvoktasya ? varṇasya
veti na vidmaḥ । na cārthasaṃbandhādṛte varṇo varṇasyānvayī bhavati padaṃ vā padasya ।﻿<pb n="b385"/>
tasmāt tasyaikasya pūrvoktasyetiśabdaḥ karaṇatāmāpādayati । sa tvanyato
vijñeyo varṇapadavākyatayā । na hyarthādṛte varṇavyatirekeṇa śak‍yate varṇasa-
mūhasyeti śabdasaṃbandho vak‍tum । nanu ca brāhmaṇavākyavat mantravākyamapi
ekavāk‍yatayā'vasīyate । satyaṃ, yadi svatantrādarthapratipattiḥ syāt । vini-
yogasavyapekṣaṃ hi mantrāṇāmarthapratipādanasāmarthyamityuktaṃ mantrādhikaraṇe ।﻿<pb n="b386"/>
evaṃ cet ṛco'pi viniyogāpekṣatvādarthasya arthaparattvācca mantrāṇā-
manyata eva parimāṇāvagatiḥ । satyamarthaparijñānamanyataḥ । parimāṇaṃ tu
chandasaḥ sakāśādvijñāyata ityuktam । tasmāt‍kiyadvāk‍yaṃ yajuritye&mdash;
(vama)tāvānasya vyāpāraḥ । sāmāni tu gītakānyabhiyuktaiḥ parimāṇataḥ smaryante
tadidaṃ parimāṇalakṣaṇaṃ yajuṣāmucyate । arthaikatvāt sākāṅkṣatvācceti ।
kimidaṃ arthaikatvaṃ ? anuṣṭheyasya smaraṇam । evaṃ tarhi padaṃ padamātra-﻿<pb n="b387"/>
mekārthamekaṃ vāk‍yaṃ; padena padena hyanuṣṭheyasya smaraṇaṃ na vāk‍yena ।
nanu cānanvitasya padābhidheyatā nāstīt‍yuktaṃ, evaṃ tarhi dvayordvayorekārthatvaṃ
padārthena hi padārtho'nvīyate na padārthasamudāyena । upapadyate caitallakṣaṇam
arthaikatvāt sākāṅkṣatvācceti । evaṃ tarhi prayojanavācyo'yamarthaśabdaḥ
parigṛhyate na pratipādyavācī । kathaṃ tarhi sākāṅkṣatvam ?</p>﻿<pb n="b388"/>
ucyate । dvayordvayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ । evaṃ cedupapannameva sākāṅkṣatvam ।
kintu pradhānapadena sakalaṃ padajātamabhisaṃbadhyate prayojanaṃ ca pradhānāmi
tyucyate । tasmāt prayojanavācye'pi siddhaṃ sākāṅkṣatvam । kimarthamubhayaṃ
sūtritam । uktaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa ।</p>
<p><q>sameṣu vākyabhedaḥ syāt ।</q> yatredānīṃ vidhyantara&mdash;﻿<pb n="b389"/>
vihitaprayojanasaṃbandho nāsti yajuṣaścaikārthatvaṃ viniyogādityuktam;
tatra kiṃ tata eva viniyogādekārthatvaṃ utānyato mṛg‍yam ।﻿<pb n="b390"/>
pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ&mdash;yajuṣa eva ekārthatā yuktā na viniyogataḥ
pārārthyamātraparyavasānādviniyogasya । ya(dya)dīṣetvetyatrādhyāhārādekārthatvaṃ
evamūrjetvetyevamādisahitasyāpi । tasmādekaṃ vāk‍yam pratipattiprayojana
guṇapradhānabhāvo bhaviṣyati ṛcāmiva kāryāntare prayujyamānānāmiti ।﻿<pb n="b391"/>
atrābhidhīyate&mdash;viniyogādevaikaṃ prayojanaṃ yuktam । kasmāt ?
yatra viniyogaḥ tat prayojanaṃ yasmāt । na tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ, śākhā
hi prayojanam । vacanāntaravihitatvānnirvāpavat । satyaṃ prayojanam ।
na tu pratipādyatayā । pratipādyena prayojanena prayojanavanto mantrāḥ ।
tasmādadhyāhārāpekṣatvāt pratipādyasya sarvārthamekaṃ bhaviṣyatīti pradarśitam ।﻿<pb n="b392"/>
rāddhāntavādinastvayamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;adhyāhṛtasyaikasya anekāryatayā guṇa-
pradhānārthatā dṛṣṭārthatā vā kal‍panīyā । taccobhayamap‍yanyāyyam । tasmā-
dyathāviniyogaṃ vāk‍yam । iṣetveti padārthadvayasaṃbandhāt śak‍yata itiśabdena
saṃbandhaḥ pratipat‍tumiti, niyogo hi vāk‍yārthasya karaṇatāmāpādayati
padārthasyeva vibhaktiyogaḥ । tasmādyathāviniyogaṃ vāk‍yabhedaḥ । evaṃ
<quote>‘k‍lṛptīrvācayati’</quote> iti bahūnāṃ viniyuktatvāt tanniṣpattyarthaṃ k‍lṛpteḥ prādhānyaṃ
nādriyate vibhāgavat ।</p>﻿<pb n="b393"/>
<p><q>anuṣaṅgo vāk‍yasamāptiḥ ।</q> saiveyaṃ yajurgatā kathā vartate । nanu
ceyaṃ vṛttā । viniyogataḥ sāmarthyataḥ parimāṇamuk‍taṃ yajuṣaḥ । satyamuktam ।
uktaviṣaya evāyaṃ punarvicāraḥ । kaḥ punarasau । ayamasau, yatra bahūni vāk‍ya-
śeṣāpekṣāṇi vāk‍yāni ekaśca vāk‍yaśeṣaḥ kiṃ yasyānantaraṃ tenaiva saṃbadhyate
uta yāvadbhirākāṅkṣayata iti । kiṃ punaratra yuktam ? pūrvapakṣavādī tvevaṃ﻿<pb n="b394"/>
manyate । ākāṃkṣā sannidhiḥ yogyatvaṃ ca saṃbandhahetuḥ sannidhiścāpekṣikaḥ ।
tasmādanantaraṃ sannihitamucyate'vyavadhānapekṣam । ato[nā]nuṣaṅgaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate&mdash;satyamākāṅkṣā sannidhiḥ yogyatvaṃ ca saṃbandhe hetuḥ
sannidhānaṃ punarnāvyavadhānāpekṣam । kiṃ tarhi ? sajātīyāvyavadhānāpekṣam ।
na cātra sajātīyo vāk‍yaśeṣo vyavadhāyako (dṛśyate)vidyate । śoṣiṇastvasajā-
tīyatvānna vyavadhāyakāḥ । na hi yo yamapekṣate sa tasya vyavadhāyako bhavati﻿<pb n="b395"/>
yathā bahūni ākhyātākāṅkṣāṇi nāmāni । tatra sambandhe
ānantaryamātrānna vyavadhānaṃ kurvanti । atha manyase padadharmo'ya&mdash;
miti na padatvātsaṃbandhaḥ । kiṃ tarhi ? ākāṅkṣitatvādeva ।﻿<pb n="b396"/>
yat‍punaridaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa samudāyāpekṣatayā''nantaryamupanyastam samudāyi-
bhiśca sambandhaḥ kastasyārthaḥ ayamevārtho yo'smābhirvyākhyātaḥ ।
etaduktaṃ bhavati&mdash;padasamudāyasyaiva ekapadasaṃbandhe nānantaryaṃ viśeṣyate ।﻿<pb n="b397"/>
pratipadaṃ ca sambandhaḥ । evañca paurvāparyamap‍yatantram । kiyāṃstu
sannidhiriti yadevoktaṃ yāvadanyatsajātīyaṃ nopanipatatīti tadevedam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b398"/>
<p><q>anuṣaṅgaḥ ।</q> yatredānīṃ śeṣīṇi nirākāṅkṣāṇi śeṣaśca sākāṅkṣaḥ,
tatrāpi saiva kathā asajātīyavyavadhānāt sarvaiḥ saṃbandhaḥ । kimarthaṃ tarhi
punarlikhitam ? tadeva tu na jñāyate । kiṃ śeṣitāmātrameva sajātī-
yatvaṃ uta pradhānapadābhiprāyamiti । tatra pūrveṇa nyāyena śoṣitamātraṃ sa-
jātīyamiti prāptaṃ tadvayudāsāyedaṃ punarlikhitam । ekākhyātasaṃbandhe satīti﻿<pb n="b399"/>
pūrvatra vā'bhinnākhyātasaṃbandhe sati kiṃ bhavatyanuṣaṅgaḥ ? kimida&mdash;
mākhyātagrahaṇam ? pradhānapadapradarśanārthameva । evaṃ tarhi pūrvatrāpi
pradhānapadābhedādevānuṣaṅgaḥ । tasmādanarthakaṃ punarlekhyam ।</p>
<p>atrocyate&mdash;pradhānapadābhedepi nirākāṅkṣeṣu pradhāneṣu ekatvādvāk‍ya-
śeṣasya ekenaiva saṃbandho yuktaḥ śak‍yate ca viśeṣo'vagantuṃ, ānantaryāṃt ।
satyaṃ yatrārthabhedaḥ । yatra tvartha eva na bhidyate tatra pūrvavadevānuṣaṅgaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b400"/>
<p><q>vyavāyānnānuṣajyeta ।</q> yatra punaḥ sajātīyena vyavadhānaṃ tatra
vyavāyānnānuṣaṅgaḥ ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ dvitīyādhyāyasya
prathamaḥ pādaḥ ।<yatrailer>﻿<pb n="b401"/>
<head>bṛhatī</head>
<trailer>dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
<p><q>śabdāntare karmabhedaḥ ।</q> śabdāntare karmabheda iti śrūyate ।
kaḥ punaratra śabdo'bhipretaḥ kiṃ vā karma ? śāstraṃ śabdo'bhipretaḥ,
niyogārthaḥ karma । kathaṃ tarhi anubandhabhedādbheda ucyate karmaṇaḥ ?</p>
﻿<pb n="b402"/>
kimiti vā nocyate ? śāstrāddhi karmaṇo'nubandhaḥ । evañcetaretarāśrayaḥ
tasmācchāstraparimāṇajñānopāyastāvadanyato vaktavyaḥ । tasmācchāstrāntaratve
yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ । atrocyate । dvayamapyatraiva pratipādyate । kathaṃ ?
śāstrāntare sati karmabheda iti vadatā śāstrātkarmabheda ityuktam । nānu-﻿<pb n="b403"/>
bandhāt । kathaṃ punaḥ śāstrāntaraparijñānam? atrāpi kṛtānubandhatvādityu-
ktam । nanu ca karmānubadhyate na śāstram । kena cok‍taṃ neti ? parimāṇa-
parijñāne hi śāstrāsyānubandha upakaroti । na tarhi kṛtānubandhaṃ śāstraṃ bhavati ।﻿<pb n="b404"/>
pratipādakatayā kṛto'nubandhaḥ pratītiryena tat kṛtānubandham । yadvā
kṛtānubandhatvātkarmaṇaḥ । anubandhāntareṇānvayasyānabhidhānāt । anu-
bandhāntaratve śāstrāntaratvaṃ śāstrāntaratve śāstrārthāntaratvam । kathaṃ
tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ? evamatra pūrvapakṣayanti । ayuktamidaṃ anubandha-
bhedāt śāstraṃ bhidyata iti । kasmāt ? dṛṣṭaṃ hi anekānubandhamekaṃ
śāstraṃ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ svargakāmo yajeteti । evaṃ yāgadānahomānu-
bandheṣvapi mābhūdbhedaḥ । nanu ca karaṇetikartavyatāvyavasthānāttatrābhedaḥ﻿<pb n="b405"/>
anubandhāntare'pi tāvadabheda iti pratipannam । avasthānaṃ tu viniyoga-
to'vagamyam । na cāyamekāntaḥ karaṇetikartavyatāvyavasthānādeveti
kevalakaraṇāvasthitānāmapi bahūnāmekaśāstrāvagamyatvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ darśapūrṇa-
māsayoḥ; rājasūye ca utpattāvapi prājāpatyāniti । nanu ca prājāpatyeṣu
saṅkhyayā bhedaḥ bhavatu, anubandhabhedastāvanna bhedakaḥ । asati cānubandhabhede
saṅkhyā bhet‍trīti namo bhedavidbhayaḥ । tasmāt pracayāvagamyo'yamanu-
﻿<pb n="b406"/>
bandhasamudāya ekaśāstrāvagamyaḥ । ekaśāstrāvagabhye ca eko niyogārthaḥ
tadevāpūrvam । yadvā pratyayāvagamyatvāt niyogārthasya sānubandhataiva na
pratīyate । padārthasyeva padārthāntareṇa ।</p>
<p>nanu ca padārtho'pi padārthāntareṇānubaddha eva । parasparānvayitā
hyanubandhaḥ ucyate । anabhijño bhavānanuvandhānvayayoḥ । kaḥ
punaranayoḥ viśeṣaḥ? ayamanayorviśeṣaḥ । kriyākārakaguṇiguṇyaida-
marthyasaṃbandhitā'nvaya ucyate । niyogasya viṣayitāpantiranubandhaḥ ।﻿<pb n="b407"/>
na ca śabdāntarābhidheyo viṣayatāmāpadyate । aviniyuktaviniyogāpekṣitve
cāgṛhyamāṇaviśeṣaṇatvaṃ prayājādīnāmiva । tasmātsiddhamekaśāstrābhidheyatvam ।
yadvā yāgadānahomeṣvayamaparo viśeṣaḥ । anubandhānāṃ nānātvamapi(vai)na
śakyate vak‍tum । parasparānuvādasaṃbhavāt yadāhavanīye juhvatītivat ।
evaṃ guṇakarmasu guṇavidhāneṣu ca draṣṭavyam । pradhānānupraveśāttadvidhānasya ।
﻿<pb n="b408"/>
evañca sarvaphalānubandhaṃ sarvaguṇānubandhaṃ sarvadhātvarthānubandhamekaṃ karma ।
eko niyoga ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate । na ca sarvaviṣaya eko niyogārthaḥ pratipat‍tuṃ
śakyate । bhāvārtha eva hi karmaśabdo bhāvārthāntaranirapekṣo viṣayama-
vacchinatti । karaṇāpattau hi bhāvārthāntarāpekṣā bhāvārthasya na viṣayāpattau ।﻿<pb n="b409"/>
viṣayībhūtasya hi niyogārthaṃ prati sādhanabhāvo'vagamyate na punaḥ tatsādhana-
tayaiva niyogasaṃbandhaḥ । yathā caitadevaṃ tathā ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyāmaḥ । tasmāt
dhātvarthabhedānniyogamedaḥ niyogabhedācca siddhaṃ karmāntaratvam, yadapyuktam
niyogārthasya pratyayavācyatvāt, agṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāt sarvabhāvārthābhi-
saṃbandha iti । tadayuktam । agṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatā hi niyoge na viṣaye ।
﻿<pb n="b410"/>
taduktaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa&mdash;yajirapyevaṃ svoccāraṇāvagamyaviṣaye noccāraṇāntarama-
pekṣate । yā punarekārthatā yāgahomānāmupavarṇitā sā nopapadyate bhinnārthāvagateḥ ।
na ca vidheyārthatve saṃbhavati anuvādatā yuktā । yatpunaridamuktam
darśapūrṇamāsayorivānekānubandhaviṣayatā evāvagamyanta iti । parihṛta-
midamasmābhiḥ । viniyojyatayā tadavasīyate na viṣayatayā ।
﻿<pb n="b411"/>
ata eva cāgneyādayo'bhinnaviṣayā eva na bhinnaviniyojyāḥ । tasmātsiddhaṃ
prativiṣayaṃ śās‍trabhedaḥ tadbhedācca karmabheda iti ।</p>
<p><q>ekasyaivaṃ punaḥ śrutiḥ ।</q> uktaṃ kṛtānubandhatvācchās‍trabhedaḥ
śāstrabhedātkarmabheda iti । yatra punaranubandho'pyekaḥ tatra kathaṃ ? bhavatu
tatraikaṃ śāstram, ekaṃ ca karma । nanu cānarthakaṃ bhavati ।</p>﻿<pb n="b412"/>
kimidamānarthakyaṃ nāma ? yadi tāvannārthapratipādakatvaṃ, tadayuktam, pratyu-
tārthāntaratve'pratipādakaṃ bhavati । atha niṣprayojanatvaṃ, avagamyamānaṃ hi
yadi prayojanaṃ na bhavati mābhūt ko doṣaḥ । tasmādekaṃ karma ।
atrābhidhīyate&mdash;vidyata evānubandhabhedo'trāpi । kutaḥ aviśeṣāt ।
naitacchakyate vak‍tum । asyārthasyetthaṃ punaḥ śrutirvartata iti । yāgadāna-
homādīnāmapi hyarthabhedādevānubandhatā bhidyate taccātrāpi tulyam । nanu
cātraiko yāgārthaḥ pratīyate satyamevaiko yāgaḥ na tu vidheyatayā ।
﻿<pb n="b413"/>
kathaṃ punarekaḥ pratīyamāno'pi vidheyatayā nānātvaṃ bhajate yathā jyotiṣṭoma-
darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ । ādhastyamadhikaraṇamidānīṃ k‍vopayujyate ? viśeṣāddhi
tatrānubandhabhedaḥ । iha tvaviśeṣādityupayogaḥ । ata eva bhāṣyakāreṇa
pūrvapakṣe sa eva śabdaḥ punaḥ punaruccāryata iti vadatā na viśeṣādṛte'nubandha-
nānātvaṃ siddhayatīti pradarśitam । guṇavidhānaṃ punaḥ kimarthamāśāṅkitam ?﻿<pb n="b414"/>
punaḥ śruterudāharaṇaṃ durlabhamiti manvānenedamāśaṅkitam । guṇanā-
nātvāddhi śrutyantarameva bhavati । nāmāni vā bhavantu । tathāpi
śrutyantarameva । parihārastu na kevaladhātvarthavidhāvasati guṇavidhānaṃ nāma vā
na saṃbhavati guṇo hi vidhīyamānaḥ samidho yajatīti kva vidhīyatām ? yadi
tāvatpradhānayāge, guṇāntarāvarodhāt na saṃbhavati । atha samidyāgaeva, yāga-﻿<pb n="b415"/>
vidhānamapi prāpnoti yāgavidhāne ca nivṛttiḥ guṇavidhānasya śruteḥ nāma&mdash;
tāvagamāt । evaṃ pañcasvapi draṣṭavyam । nāmno'nuvādatvāt yajiśrutireva
kevalaṃ viṣayaviśeṣaṇaṃ tasmādetānyevodāharaṇāni punaḥ śruteḥ । na cātra nāma
bhedakaṃ vidhānottarakālabhāvitvānnamabhāvasya । abhedakameva tarhi sarvatra nāma,
vidhānottarakālabhāvitvāt । ucyate । samidādiṣu tu na bhedakam ।
﻿<pb n="b416"/>
jyotiṣṭomādiṣu tu yathā bhedakaṃ tathā tatraiva viśeṣaṃ varṇayiṣyāmaḥ ।
tasmādaviśeṣādanubandhabhedaḥ anubandhabhedācchastrabhedaḥ śāstrabhedātkāryabheda
iti siddham ।</p>
<p><q>prakaraṇaṃ tu paurṇamāsyām ।</q> uk‍taṃ punaḥ śruterapyanubandhānya-
tvamaviśeṣāditi । asyāmidānīṃ punaḥ śrutau ya evaṃ vidvān
paurṇamāsīṃ yajate ya evaṃ vidvānamāvāsyāṃ yajata iti kimanu&mdash;
bandhabhedo vidyate netīti cintyate । pūrvok‍tena nyāyenā&mdash;﻿<pb n="b417"/>
viśeṣādanubandhabhedaḥ । śabdāntaratvaṃ kimityupanyastam ? abhyāsādevā-
viśeṣāditi yuktirgamyate । atrābhidhīyate । ubhayaprakāro'tra bhedaḥ
cintyate karaṇetikartavyatākṛto viṣayakṛtaśca । tatrābhyāsādviṣayakṛtabheda-
siddhiḥ, śabdāntarāt karaṇetikartavyatābhedaḥ tasmādyuk‍tamubhayamupanyaratam ।
