ata eva samapradhānāṅgāṅgibhāvānuvādavidhānāni krameṇopanyastāni ।
﻿<pb n="b418"/>
na vidhānamātrāt samapradhānabhovasiddhiḥ । nāpyanuvādamātrāt guṇapradhāna-
bhāvaḥ । kiṃ rhi ? śabdāntaratvāt guṇapradhānabhāvaḥ, abhidhānā-
ntaratvādityarthaḥ । abhidhānaikyācca samapradhānabhāvaḥ । kiṃ punaraḍga-
pradhānatayā bhedakathane prayojanam ? (na)viṣayato vā bhedakathane kiṃ
prayojanam ? kathaṃ nāma bhedenānuṣṭhānaṃ syāditi । evaṃ cet
atrāpyaṅgapradhānatayā kathaṃ nāmānuṣṭhānaṃ syāditi । nanu cāḍga-
pradhānatā viniyogādevāvagamyate phalavadaphalatayā । kimabhinnasyaiva
viniyogādavagatiḥ ? na brūmo'bhinnasyeti । kintu viṣayamātra-﻿<pb n="b419"/>
bhedādbhinnasyetyucyate । yadi viṣayabheda eva aṅgāṅgitve hetuḥ kimiti na
pradhānāni parasparāṅgam ? samidādīni vā । tasmāt kāryacodanāto bhedo-
'ṅgāṅgitve hetuḥ na viṣayacodanātaḥ ato viṣayatvena bhinnānāṃ kārye śabdā-
ntarataivānubandhabhede hetuḥ bhinnānāṃ ca viniyogāt । phalavadaphalatayā
cāṅgāṅgitvamavagamyate । tasmāt prayogacodanāto bhedo'pyatraiva
pradaśanīyaḥ । taduktam । śabdāntaratvādabhyāsācca samapradhānā-
nīti bhāṣye bahuvacanādviṣayabhedaḥ prātipadikātkāryānyatvam ।﻿<pb n="b420"/>
tadidaṃ lakṣaṇādāvuktaṃ pradhānāpradhānāni parīkṣyante bhinnānyabhinnāni ceti ।
pradhānānītyaṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ apradhānānīti viṣayaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate&mdash;<q>prakṛtānāmanuvaditārau paurṇamāsyamāvāsyā-
saṃyuktau</q>, kutaḥ ? viśe, viśeṣāvagamāt । pūrvasyāḥ śruteriyaṃ punaḥ śrutirgamyate ।
kasmāt ? kālasaṃbaddhā hoyaṃ codanā । yadyatna kālasaṃsparśo'rtho na
gṛhyate tadā tadarthasyāgrahaṇameva । anyathānavagamāt । yadi punaḥ
kālasaṃsparśo na gṛhyate tadā pūrvasyāḥ śruteriyaṃ punaḥ śrutiḥ spaṣṭā ।﻿<pb n="b421"/>
kālayoginī hi sā śrutiḥ । atha kasmānna viparītaṃ ? agnyāderabhyadhikasyā-
vagamāt । tasmādiyameva punaḥ śrutiḥ tato'nuvādaḥ anuvādatvācca kārye
śabdāntaratvādbhedaḥ । atrāgneyādīni payo'ntāni pradhānāni prayā-
jādīnyaṅgāni । kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ ? anuvāda eva prayājādīnyaṅgāni na
punarvidhāvapi । kathaṃ vā vidhipakṣe'ṅgāṅgitā śaṅkayate ? । evamā-﻿<pb n="b422"/>
śaṅkyate । tayorhi karmaṇorvacanāntareṇa kālavidhānaṃ <quote>“paurṇamāsyāṃ paurṇamāsyā
yajeta,”</quote> <quote>“amāvāsyāyāmamāvāsyayā yajeta”</quote> iti । tataḥ kiṃ ? idaṃ tato
bhavati, aṣṭānāṃ yāgānāṃ darśapūrṇamāsaśabdavācyatā bhavati āgneyādiguṇa&mdash;
vidhipakṣe vā dvayoreva । ataśca tayoḥ phalasaṃbandhaḥ । teṣāṃ vā । prayājādīnā-
maṅgataiva । tasmādanupapannāmidaṃ vidhau samaprādhānyam anuvāde'ṅgāṅgiteti ।﻿<pb n="b423"/>
ucyate । na kālavidhirdvayoḥ saṃbhavati । prayogaśeṣatā hi
paurṇamāsyāṃ paurṇamāsyā yajeta iti pratīyate na viṣayaśeṣatā । yadyapya-
nayorutpattikālayogābhāvena darśapūrṇamāsapadavācyatā nāsti tathāpi darśa-
pūrṇamāsābhyāmiti ṣaṇṇāṃ darśapūrṇamāsaśabdatā kena vāryate । anabhijño
bhavān vidhyanuvādaśabdasāmarthyasya devānāṃ priyaḥ । yathā'nuvādaṃ
hi śakyate saṅkhayā'vagantum । tātparye ca viśeṣataḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b424"/>
atātparye ayathānuvāde ca na saṅkhayāyoginaḥ upapadavaśānniyamaḥ﻿<pb n="b425"/>
śakyate'vagantuṃ rājasūyavat । tasmānna saṅkhayā nāpyupapadaṃ viśeṣāvagatau
hetuḥ ato dvayaṃ dhātvarthānusāri tatra bhavatīti yuktamuktam । tatretare guṇa-
vidhaya iti yaduktamupanyāse tadidamucyate । atha kasmānnāgneyādīni
guṇavidhānāni । etau ca karmavidhī । śakyate saṅkhayānusāritayā
dvayoḥ prādhānyaṃ vak‍tuṃ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ svargakāmo yajeteti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b426"/>
<p><q>codanā vā guṇānām ।</q> naitatsaṃbhavati । yadi tāvatpaurṇamā-
syāmaṣṭākapāle bhavatīti saṃbandho vivakṣitaḥ, na tāvadayamarthaḥ aṣṭokapolaḥ
sattayā saṃbadhyata iti bhavatyarthena na saṃbadhyata ityarthaḥ । athog‍neyaḥ
paurṇamāsyāṃ bhavatīti vivakṣyate tadāpyāgneyapuroḍāśayorasaṃbandha eva ।
pūrveṇa sahosya pakṣasya ko viśeṣaḥ ? ayamasti viśeṣaḥ guṇa-﻿<pb n="b427"/>
pradhānavivakṣā'tra । bhavatu yatheṣṭam tathāpi parasparasaṃbandho naiva
śakyate vidhātum । atha paurṇamāsyāmaṣṭākapālasyāgneyatā vidhīyate
atha tasyāmāgneyasyāṣṭākapālateti । idamapi pakṣadvayaṃ avivakṣotsaṅkalanāyai-
﻿<pb n="b428"/>
vobhayatra paurṇamāsīpadasaṃbandho duśśakaḥ । yadapi padadvayaṃ
agniprajāpativat paurṇamāsīsaṃbandhitayā vidhīyata ityupanyastam
tatrāpi saṃbhavati padadvayavidhānam । arūpatā tu pūrvavadevāg‍neyāṣṭāka-
pālayoḥ saṃbandhābhāvāt ।</p>﻿<pb n="b429"/>
<p>athāgnīṣomīyavat saṃbaddhayorvidhānamityucyate, kauryatvātsaṃbandhasya na
vidhānādṛte siddhiḥ agnīṣomau tu prasiddhau dvandvatayā mitrāvaruṇavat ।
athātrāpi pūrvakṛtaḥ saṃbandhaḥ kenacit parigṛhyate tathāpi saivā-
rūpatā ihāvidhānāt । athāg‍neya iti siddhavadvidhāya
punarāg‍neyatocyate । na ca sakṛduccaritasya arthadvayaṃ(vidhānaṃ)saṃbhavati ।
﻿<pb n="b430"/>
atha rātrisatravadagnireva devatā kalpyate, na; pramāṇābhāvāt । rātrisatre
tarhi kathaṃ ? tatrārthavādānupapatteḥ; iha ca dravyamātratayopapattiḥ । na dravyaṃ
devatāmapekṣate । devatā hi dravyāpekṣiṇī dravyasaṃbandhitayaiva devatetyucyate ।
tasmāddevatāvidhānārthaṃ dravyadevatāsaṃbandho vidhātavyaḥ sa cedvidhīyate
siddhaṃ karmāntaratvam । na ca karma karmāntarasya rūpaṃ bhavatīti﻿<pb n="b431"/>
arūpatvāditi siddho hetuḥ । atha yaduk‍taṃ lakṣaṇeti pramāṇāntarāvagamānna
doṣaḥ । <quote>“vyapadeśaśca tadvat”</quote> iti prayājādibhyaḥ āg‍neyādīnāṃ śabdā-
ntarābhideyatāṃ kathayati śabdāntaratvācca siddho guṇapradhānabhāvaḥ । tadvacca
﻿<pb n="b432"/>
liṅgadarśanamiti । kathaṃ punaḥ bahuṣvabhidheyeṣu ekavacanaṃ paurṇamāsīmiti ?
kiṃ kurmaḥ ? kamupālabhemahi ? nityo'yaṃ vaidikaprayogaḥ । tatra tatra bahupve-
kavacanamiti jñātamasmābhiḥ । jñānamevedamasiddham । ekavacanaśravaṇā-
dyajirupapadaṃ caikasyaiva pratipādakamiti yuk‍tamabhyupagantum । satyaṃ yuk‍taṃ,
na tu tadiha śakyate yajyarthatulyatvāt paurṇamāsyarthatulyatvācca । agṛhya-
māṇaviśeṣatve cāpratipattirvā syāt । sarvāvagatirvā । tatra kiṃ yuktam ?
nāpratipattiryuktā, avagamaviśedhāt sarvāvagateḥ svavagamānugrahaḥ ।﻿<pb n="b433"/>
nanu cātrāpyekāvagamavirodhaḥ । parihāryavirodhastvasau । pracayāvagamāt ।
apratipattau tu aparihāryo'vagamavirodhaḥ । tasmātsūk‍taṃ samudāyābhiprāya&mdash;
mekavacanamiti । yad‌dvivacanavirodhādvidhānapakṣe darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti
samaprādhānyamiti tadayuktamivedānīṃ pratibhāti । atrāpi kāladvayā&mdash;
vacchinnapracayāvagamāt śakyaparihārametad‌dvitvam । tasmādvidhāna-
pakṣe'pyaṅgaṅgitaiva nyāyyā । atrābhidhīyate । saivātrānabhijñatā'parādhyate ।
kathaṃ ? bahūṣu dhātoḥ prātipadikasya vā prayogaḥ tantramekaśeṣo vā । ubhayatra
darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti vidhipakṣe dvitvavirodhaḥ । kathaṃ? yadi tāvat
tantratvaṃ ṣaṇṇāmeva hi tatpratīyate । na punastrayāṇāṃ, tantradvaye hi
dviruccāraṇaṃ syāt ।</p>﻿<pb n="b434"/>
na ca tadapyasti । ṣaṇṇāṃ ca tantratve pracayadvayāvagatau pramāṇāntaraṃ 
mṛgyam । ekābhidhānāddhayekapracayāvagatiḥ । ākhyātānusāri
ca nāmadheyamityuk‍taṃ bhāvārthādhikaraṇe <quote>‘sthita etasminnadhikaraṇa’</quote>
iti vadatā । tasmāt kāladvayamapyasmin pakṣe pravṛttimātraupayikaṃ
nāmnaḥ na punaravacchedāyālam । agnihotravat । tadanvayiravārthābhidhānaṃ
darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti yāgamātranāmatayā pratipattavyam । evamekaśeṣo-
'pyayaṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ na trayāṇāṃ trayāṇāmiti । tasmāt pracayadvayāvagati-﻿<pb n="b435"/>
rdurlabhā vidhipakṣe । anuvādapakṣe punaḥ trayāṇāṃ trayāṇāṃ tantraikaśeṣayoḥ
siddhayoḥ pracayadvayāvagatau satyāṃ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti pracayadvayasyaivā-
yamekaśeṣaḥ tantratvaṃ ceti siddho guṇapradhānabhāvabhedaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>paurṇamāsīvadupāṃśuyājaḥ syāt ।</q> uk‍taṃ caturdaśa paurṇamā-
syāmāhutayo hūyante trayodaśāmāvāsyāyāmiti । tatra yadyeka upāṃśuyājaḥ
tadaitadupapadyate । atha trayāṇāmanuvādakamupāṃśuyājamantarā yajatīti, caturdaśa
paurṇamāsyāmāhutayo hūyante trayodaśāmāvāsyāyāmiti na ghaṭate tatprasaṅgādi-
damadhikaraṇamārabdham ।</p>﻿<pb n="b436"/>
<p>kathaṃ punaratra saṃśayaḥ ? tatrāpyāg‍neyādaya iva viṣṇurupāṃśu yaṣṭavya
ityevamādayaḥ śrūyante । kimeṣāmupāṃśuyājamantarā yajatīti samudāyānu-
vādaḥ uta vidhiriti । nanu caikamidaṃ vākyaṃ, kathamatra saṃśayaḥ । nahye-
kasmin vākye bahavo vidhayaḥ saṃbhavanti । tadeva tvekavākyatva-
mākṣipyate । kathaṃ ? jāmi vā etadyajñasya kriyata ityupakramo'yaṃ viṣṇu-
rupāṃśu yaṣṭavya ityevamādīnāṃ sādhāraṇa iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate ।﻿<pb n="b437"/>
bhavati ca sādhāraṇo vākyaśeṣaḥ । varṣiṣṭhādiṣu darśanāt । yad‌brāhmaṇā-
nīti cātideśadarśanāt । tasmādupapannaḥ saṃśayaḥ । tatra tāvatpūrvapakṣa-
vādī manyate sādhāraṇo'yaṃ vākyaśeṣo nyāyyaḥ iti । kutaḥ ? rūpāvacanāt
<q>nanūpāṃśuyājamantarā</q> yajatīti rūpamasti । <q>nedaṃ rūpaṃ karmaṇaḥ ।</q> prayuvate
syādapi । evaṃ tarhyupāṃśuguṇaḥ śrūyate । nātra guṇavidhiḥ śakyate'dhvavasātuṃ
yājayogāt avayavārthavatve hi asyopāṃśuyāga iti rūpaṃ rūpavido manyadhyate ।
﻿<pb n="b438"/>
tasmādarūpatvāt ayamanuvādaḥ । evaṃ ca paurṇamāsyāṃ yajan‍nityanena trayā-
ṇāmevaitatkālavidhānam । tataścaturdaśa paurṇamāsyāmiti duḥstham । kiṃ punaḥ
kāraṇaṃ guṇavidhipakṣa evaitadrūpam na punarnāmadheyapakṣe; śabdāntaramapi
hyupapannaṃ nāmadheyapakṣe śakyate vak‍tum । guṇavidhipakṣe punaḥ yajyartha eva
yajiḥ । nanu ca nāmadheyapakṣe'pi yajyartha evāyam । satyaṃ yajyartho na yajiḥ ।
kiṃ tarhi upāṃśuyājaḥ śabdaḥ । yajyarthasya hi yajeḥ kutvaṃ smaranti na punarya-
jyarthāvayavasya । tasmādupapadyata evopāṃśuyāja iti nāmadheyam । yatra puna-
ravayavayogāparityāgena yajirnāmatāṃ pratipadyate tatra bhavatyeva kutvam ।
﻿<pb n="b439"/>
tathā cāpavādaṃ smarati bhagavān pāṇiniḥ <quote>‘prayājānūyājau yajñāṅge’</quote> iti
nopasargā avayavāpahnavaṃ kartuṃ samarthāḥ । ānarthakye(nā)pyupasargatvasya
saṃbhavāt । nanu ca kriyāyoge satyānarthakye(nā)pyupasargatvam । astyeva
ayaṃ kriyāyogo yāja iti karmaṇa evaite nāmanī prayājānūyājāviti ।
ata eva copāṃśuyāja iti nāpavādaṃ smṛtavān śabdarūpavit ।</p>
<p><q>codanā vā prakṛtatvāt ।</q> atrābhidhīyate । nātrānuvādaḥ
saṃbhavati । kutaḥ ? anūdyamānasyāsaṃbhavāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b440"/>
<p>nanu viṣṇurupāṃśu yaṣṭavya iti yāgacodanāḥ santītyupanyastam,
ayuktaṃ tadupanyastam । kutaḥ ? nahi vidhyantaraṃ asmin vākye
saṃbhavati । spaṣṭe hi vidhibhede vākyaśeṣasya sādhāraṇatopapadyate na punaḥ
sādhye । vākyaśeṣasya sādhāraṇyādvidhitvaṃ vidhitve sādhāraṇyamiti
itaretarāśrayam । saṃbhavati ca vākyaśeṣatayā viṣṇvādīnāmarthavattā
upāṃśuyājamantarā yajatītyanena saṃbandhāviśeṣāt । saṃbhavati caika-
vākyatve vākyabhedo vikalpārtha eva bhavati ।</p>﻿<pb n="b441"/>
<p>nanu ca rūpaṃ nāstītyuktam । vākyāntareṇāgnihotra iva bhaviṣyati ।
dṛśyante ca vākyāntarāṇi <quote>‘paurṇamāsyāṃ yajan’</quote>, <quote>‘sarvasmai vā etadājyaṃ’</quote>
iti ca । kiñca na viṣṇurupāṃśu yaṣṭavya iti yāgavidhirgamyate upapadaśrava-
ṇāt raktapaṭavat । nanu copāṃśuyājamantarā yajatītyatrāpyupapadaśravaṇam ।
satyam । bhāvārthatā tvatra vidhiviṣayatayā'vagamyamānā na viniyoge-
nākṣep‍tuṃ śakyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b442"/>
<p>pradarśitaṃ bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdā iti । tacchūnye punarviniyogānusārī
vidhirbhavatīti viśeṣaḥ । taduktaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa-sa tu vidhīyata
upāṃśutvādisambandha iti । nanu cātra guṇavidhānaṃ pratīyate । netyucyate ।
arthavādato guṇaprāpteraguṇavidhisvarūpatvācceti pratyuk‍tam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b443"/>
kathamekavākyatvamiti ? ko'bhiprāyaḥ pṛcchataḥ ? ayamabhiprāyaḥ
parasparāsaṃbandhādviṣṇvādīnāṃ asaṃbaddhānāṃ ca padāntarasaṃbandhastantreṇaiva bhavati ।
yathāha bhagavān । astyatropādhyantaram । kiṃ tata ? prādhānye
satīti vaktavyam । iha punarupāṃśuyājamantarā yajatīti pradhānaṃ
tatprādhānye ca viṣṇurityevamādīnāṃ aruṇādīnāmivaikavākyatā
nyāyyetyuktam । kaḥ<q>punaratrārthavāda</q> iti ? kenābhiprāyeṇāyaṃ
praśnaḥ ? śrūyatām । yenābhiprāyeṇa, antarā yajatītyantarālakāla-
sambandhastāvatprāpta eva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b444"/>
<p>kiṃ punararthavādena kriyate । yadi hyarthavādādevāyamartho labhyate rātri-
satrapratiṣṭhāvat tadā yukto'rthavādaḥ । iha punaḥ antarā yajatītyantarāla-
sambandhabhāvāt kimarthavādeneti manvānasya praśnaḥ । uttaravādī tu jāmitā-
doṣasaṅkīrtanāt tannirharaṇaprayojanādapi bhavatyevārthavatteti pradārśitavān ।
aucityena stutiruktā । na cāprāptānāmaucityamastīti manvānaḥ
kathaṃ punaḥ viṣṇvādaya iti pṛṣṭavān । ayaṣṭavyānveti na stutau
pramāṇāntarāpekṣetyuttaravādino'bhiprāyaḥ । nanu ca nirālagbanataivaṃ prāpnoti
﻿<pb n="b445"/>
mṛgyatāṃ stutyuttarakālaṃ avalambanaṃ mukhyayā gauṇyā va vṛttyā na puna-
rnimittāpekṣaṃ kāryaṃ kāryatāvagatirbhavatyeva । (yadi bhavati) bhavatu kāryā-
nnimittāvagatiḥ, tathāpi nimittabhāvo vaktavyaḥ । so'bhidhīyate । atra
kecidāhuḥ viṣṇvādayaḥ prāptā eveti । kutaḥ ? śākhāntaravidhānāditi ।
sarvaśākhāpratyayamekaṃ karmeti cok‍tam । athāpi śākhāntare prāptirnopala-
bhyate । tathāpi yāgasya coditatvāt devatākāṅkṣatvācca tasya
devatāviśeṣāpekṣāyāṃ vākyaśeṣato'pyavagatirbhavatyeva । kataṃ punarvā-
﻿<pb n="b446"/>
kyaśeṣabalena devatopatiṣṭhate ? ucyate । upāṃśuyājavākye upāṃśutvaṃ kīrtya-
mānaṃ tāvat taddharmatvena svīkriyate । anyathā hi tatpākṣikaṃ syāt nityavacca
tadanūdyate । tatra yau pramāṇāntareṇopāṃśuyājadharmāṇau viṣṇuprajāpatī pratītau
tāveva buddhisthau svadharmadarśanādbhavadaḥ iti tayorevānvitābhidhānānupraveśa
iti । nanu yatkiñcitprājāpatyamiti vākyaśeṣopanyāso na yuktaḥ, upāṃśu-
tvasamānyaṃ copanyasya viṣṇormantrābhidhānamapyatiricyate । ucyate । naive-
daṃ pūrvok‍tasya pramāṇāntaratayopanyasyate dvayamapi, kintu tasyaiva dāḍharyārthaṃ
﻿<pb n="b447"/>
viṣṇormantraviśeṣāmnānamevamupapadyate । prajāpateśca vākyāntare vīpsā ।
ag‍nīṣomīyayostu vidhāyakaṃ udāhriyata eva । <quote>‘tāvabratāmagnīṣomāvājyarayaiva
nāvupāṃśu paurṇamāsyāṃ yajam’</quote> iti । kimidamagnīṣomayorvidhāyakaṃ iti ?
kiṃ jātam ? idameva jātam viṣṇvāderaprāptiḥ । aprāptaviśeṣaṃ hi
vākyamarthavādādviśeṣaṃ labhate vihitaviśeṣaṃ punarnirākāṅkṣatvāt na sambadhyate ।
evaṃ tarhi agnīṣomīyayostu kathaṃ ? yasmādvidhāyake vākye udāhriyete
tāvabratāmiti । kasya vidhāyake ? paurṇamāsyāṃ yajanniti kālasya ।﻿<pb n="b448"/>
yaduk‍tamarūpatvāditi parihṛtaṃ tat vacanāntaravihitatvādrūpasyeti । tadidaṃ
pradarśyate bhāṣyakāreṇa paurṇamāsyāṃ yajannityevamādinā । kimidaṃ
agrayaprāye likhitamiti ? idamidaṃ pradhānaprāye darśanamupāṃśuyājasyetyarthaḥ ।
nanu cānuvādapakṣe'pi prādhānyaṃ kena vāryate paurṇamāsyāṃ yajanniti kālayogāt ।﻿<pb n="b449"/>
athāyamabhiprāyaḥ ag‍nīṣomāvityarthavādadarśanāt tasyaiva kālayoga
iti । tadayuktam । agṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvātkālasya upāṃśuyāja-
mityarthavādasya ca daṇḍinyāyāderapyupapatteḥ agrayaśabdasya caikenā-
pyupapannatvāt । varṇyate tarhyayamabhiprāyaḥ viṣṇurupāṃśu yaṣṭavya ityetasmin
vidhāne guṇabhūtasya ca yajeḥ vidhiḥ; tataśca nādhikārayogyatā karmaṇaḥ ।
ak‍taṃ na saṃskārā adhikāramarhantīti । ataścāgrayaprāye darśanaṃ nopapadyata
iti । antarā yajatīti punarbhāvārthasya prādhānyāvagateḥ adhikārayogyaprāya-
(agraya)darśanamupapannaṃ bhavati । tasmānnānuvādo'yam । kintarhi ? vidhiḥ
evaṃ caturdaśapaurṇamāsyāmāhutayo hūyanta iti iti sustham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b450"/>
<p><q>āghārāgnihotramarūpatvāt ।</q> uktaṃ bhāvārthāḥ karmaśabdāḥ
niyogasya viṣayatāṃ pratipadyanta iti । yatredānīṃ guṇavidhayaḥ tatra kathaṃ
bhāvārthatvaṃ ? tasmāt sarvatrākhyātārthavidhānaṃ prāptaṃ dadhnā juhotītyeva-
mādipu । yadyevaṃ kathaṃ tadā agnihotraṃ juhotīti samudāyānuvādāśaṅkā ।
sarvatra hi dhātvarthavidhānam । aviśeṣāc‍ca karmabheda iti । atrocyate ।
﻿<pb n="b451"/>
dadh‍nā juhotīti guṇavati (guṇa)śabdo vartate । tataḥ kim ? idaṃ
tato bhavati । guṇavadvidhānaṃ prāptaṃ dadh‍nā juhotītyevamādiṣu । guṇava-
dvidhāne hi aparityaktabhāvārtha eva vidhiḥ । evaṃ ca sati śakyate-
'gnihotraṃ juhoti iti punaḥ śrutirvak‍tuṃ dadh‍nā juhotītyevamādīnāṃ nirguṇa-
tvādagnihotrapadārthasya । nanu ca guṇavacanatā vidyate'gnihotrapadasya ।
satyaṃ vidyate । na juhotītyasya sakalenāgnihotrapadenāyaṃ tadvān pratīyate ।
matvarthaścāyamagnihotrapadārthaḥ । ato na matvarthena tadvān pratipat‍tuṃ śakyate ।
ata eva śabdavidbhiruditaṃ na matubantānmatubutpadyata iti । tasmānnaṣṭāvayavaṃ
﻿<pb n="b452"/>
nāmaivaitat vaiśvadevaśabdavat । ataḥ samudāyānuvādaḥ agnihotraṃ juho-
tīti । nanu ca guṇavān vihito na guṇaḥ abhāvārthatvāt guṇasya ।
mābhūd‍guṇavidhānam tadviśipṭatā nāpanhotuṃ śakyate viśiṣṭasaṃpattyarthama&mdash;
bhāvārthasyāpyupādānaṃ na viruddhayate । yasya punaḥ agnihotraṃ juhotīti
vidhiḥ tasya dadh‍nā juhotīti vihitasyaiva guṇavattā pratīyate । tataśca
guṇamātrāvaśeṣādavidhāyakānyetāni vākyāni bhavanti guṇavataśca kevalasya
vihitatvāt । upādānamapi guṇānāṃ na siddhayati guṇavatpratītirhi
vidhiśūnyaiva tadā । atha guṇavidhānamapyāśrīyate bhāvārthebhyaḥ kriyā
pratīyata iti viruddhaṃ nāmanāmivyavahārocchedaśca । bhavatviti cet ।
﻿<pb n="b453"/>
nākarmaṇi niyogaḥ śakyeta'vagantum । tasmān‍nyāyyaṃ vacanaṃ bhāvārthebhyaḥ
kriyā pratīyate iti । nyāyyaṃ cābhyupagamena na śakyate bādhitum ।
ato dadh‍nā juhotītyeva vidhānamabhyupagantuṃ yuktam । upādānenāpi tāvat
guṇaśruterarthavattā bhavatviti । vihiteṣu guṇavatsu nirguṇā punaḥ śrutiḥ ।
kathaṃ punarguṇavatsu nirguṇā punaḥ śrutiḥ ? bhāvārthamātraparyavasāyī vidhirityu-
ktam । tasmādvidheyatvena punaḥ śrutiḥ vidhyapekṣaścāyamanuvādo nābhidhānā-
pekṣaḥ । nanu ca nāviniyuktamupādīyate । kena cok‍taṃ na vini-
yukto guṇa iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b454"/>
<p>anabhijño bhavān । etaduk‍taṃ bhavati&mdash;nāviniyuktaṃ vidhīyate
nāvihitamupādīyata iti। vidhyartha eva hi viniyogo na
viśeṣaṇārthaḥ tadvattā ca viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatāmādāyeti naidamarthyam ।
nanu gomāniti gavāṃ gomadarthatā pratīyate । naivam । śarāvatyādiṣva-
darśanāt । tasmād‌gomati pramāṇāntaratastādarthyaṃ mṛgyam । ṣaṣṭhayā
tādarthyamiti cenna mātṛmāt pitṛmānityanaikāntyāt । ucyate ।
aviniyuk‍tepi śeṣatā nāsti । asati ca śeṣatve aidamarthyaṃ mābhūta ।
﻿<pb n="b455"/>
upādānaṃ punaḥ vi(śiṣṭā)śeṣaṇatvāvagamapūrvakameva yathā paś‍vekatvasya paśunā
yajeteti ।</p>
<p>nanu ca tadekatvaṃ viniyuktapaśuviśaṣaṇam । ata upādīyate
viniyuktasyopādeyatvāt । dadhyādestu kathamupādānam ? dadhyādyapi
viniyuktaviśeṣaṇameva । karmaṇo viniyuktatvāt phale । evaṃ tarhi
upādānaśeṣaṃ dadhyādi । bhavatu na kaściddoṣaḥ । yathaiva hi dravya-
saṅkhyāliṅgaśūnyaṃ viniyuktamapi nopādātuṃ śakyata ityekatvādayaḥ
upādīyante । evaṃ karmāpi na kārakaviśeṣaśūnyamastīti dadhyād‌yu-
pādānasiddhiḥ । yadyevaṃ kimiti tarhyanyopādāne vaiguṇyāśaṅkā ? upādāne
śeṣamapi śeṣamevetyadoṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu cāsmin pakṣe paśvādīnāmapi naiva vidhānam । omityucyate
﻿<pb n="b456"/>
kathaṃ tarhi paś‍vekatvamiveti pradarśitam । abhyupagamyaitatpradarśitam ।
yathā satyapi guṇavidhāvaviniyuk‍tasyaiva paś‍vekatvasyopādānaṃ tadvaddadhyāderiti ।
tadevedamāpatitaṃ ghoṭārūḍhasya vismṛto ghoṭa iti । vidheścāviṣayā guṇāḥ
vidhinā copādīyanta ita ।</p>
<p>atrābhidhīyate । mugdhaḥ khalvasi kāryopādānaviśeṣajñāne । yatra
niyuṅk‍te tatkāryam । tatsiddhaye yadupādīyate tadupādānam । viniyoge
cāviṣayatā nāmārthasyok‍tā । na punarakārakatāpi । nanu copādānamapi
vidhervyāpāra iti eva vyāpāratvācca kimiti niyogaviṣayatāṃ na pratipadyate ।
﻿<pb n="b457"/>
anubandhāvaskandāt । anyathā hi bhedābhedau śāstrasya durbhaṇau
syātām । tasmādviśeṣāvagatireva viśeṣasyopādānamākṣipati na
punarniyogastamāskandati dravyopādānamiva । tasmādidameva nyāyyaṃ dadhnā
juhotīti vidhiḥ agnihotraṃ juhotīti samudāyānuvādaḥ । saṃjñopabandhāditi
kimabhyadhikamucyate । idamabhyadhikam । prakṛtebhyaḥ saṃjñāto'nyatvaṃ
pratīyata ityabhiprāyaḥ । saṃjñāhi śrūyamāṇaiva prakṛtebhyo'nyatvamāpādayati
athaiṣa jyotirityevamādiṣu darśanāt । satyamevaṃ viśeṣāvagatau satyām ।
jyotirādiṣu tu sahasradakṣiṇādiviśiṣṭāḥ karmaviśeṣā avagamyante tatheha
viśeṣāvagatiḥ । nanu vijñāyata evātrājyāghārahomau kriyāntarebhyo viśiṣṭau ।
﻿<pb n="b458"/>
yadyevaṃ lokata eva tarhi vijñātau kimatra vidhiḥ kariṣyatīti
guṇaphalopabandheṣu saṃjñā niṣprayojanaiva । atha viśiṣṭasya saṃjñā vāci-
ketyucyate । uk‍taṃ tarhi prakṛtebhyo na viśeṣāntaramava़gamyata iti ।
api ca kriyāvidhānapakṣe guṇakarmavidhānaṃ prāpnoti dvitīyāntatvānnāmnaḥ ।
ataśca nāmadheyānupapattiḥ । anuvādapakṣe punaḥ vihitapracayāvagamyatvāt
samudāyasya bhavatyavagatau samudāyaḥ sādhyaḥ । ataśca nāmadheye'pyavirodhaḥ ।
agnihotrapadamapi samudāyasya vācakaṃ prāpnoti । neti brūmaḥ । dhātuvadeva
tantreṇa samudāyināmeva vācakam dvitīyaikatvayostu gamyamānapracayaviṣaya-
tayā parihāro'yamaprakṛtatvācceti ko'yaṃ kūṣmāṇḍaḥ । pratyutāprakṛtatvāt 
dravyadevatasya vidhānaṃ prāpnoti aviśeṣādityucyate । na santatādibhyaḥ
kaścidanyo viśeṣo'vagamyate āghāre yena viśeṣāntaraniṣṭhāghārasaṃjñā syāt
tasyāḥ santatādiniṣṭhaiveyaṃ saṃjñā । tataścānuvādaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b459"/>
<p><q>saṃjñopabandhāditi ।</q> paurṇamāsyadhikaraṇe'pyākṣepaparihārau
draṣṭavyau । <q>codanā vā śavdārthasya । na</q> samudāyānuvādau agnihotraṃ juhoti
﻿<pb n="b460"/>
āghāramāghārayatīti । kutaḥ ? prakṛtānāṃ karmaṇāmabhāvāt । kathamabhāvaḥ
guṇavidhānāvagateḥ dadhnā juhotītyevamādiṣu । nanu ca  nākarmaṇi guṇo
vidhātuṃ śakyate । satyam । idameva karma bhaviṣyati agnihotraṃ juhotīti
sāmānyāvagateḥ । viśeṣaniṣṭhatvāt saṃjñāyā na vidhānaṃ sambhavati ।
vidheyatvādeva viśeṣo lakṣyata ityabhiprāyaḥ । labdhe ca viśeṣe guṇayoga-
pravṛttyā nāmadheyatvasiddhiḥ । kathaṃ punarabhāvārthatvāt guṇavidhiḥ ।
bhāvārtha eva hi tarhi śābdo vidhīyate । nanu ca dṛṣṭaṃ kathaṃ bhāvasya
viśeṣaṇam ? kimiti vā na viśeṣaṇam । akriyārūpatvāt dravyasya 
naivātra rūparūpitayā viśeṣaṇam । kathaṃ tarhi ? anubandhatayaiva ।
evamapyanubandho vidhiviṣayo nā[na]nubandhaḥ । tataḥ kim ? idaṃ tato
bhavati yatpūrvok‍taṃ viśiṣṭasyāvihitatvāt viśeṣaṇaṃ upādānaśeṣaṃ bhavati na
﻿<pb n="b461"/>
vidheyamityucyate । yathaiva hi viniyojya(tayā)sthatvāt aviniyojya-
mupādeyaṃ, evameva hi vidheyamapi bhavatīti । idamayuktam । yukto hi
viniyogaḥ । aidamarthyāvagatirhi siddhasādhyatāṃ nāpekṣate । niyogastu
kāryāvagatipūrvaka eva । tasmādupādānamātrameva dadhyādeḥ śakyate
vak‍tum । na punarvidheyatā । nanu cāvidheyatve sādhanāntaranirākaraṇaṃ na
prāpnoti । anivārite ca tasmin dadhyādipadamanarthakaṃ syāt ।
﻿<pb n="b462"/>
kiṃkriyatām ? sasyārtho nāsti kimanyata ānarthakyādityuk‍tam । kastarhi
parihāraḥ ? <q>sūtrakāraṃ pṛccha । yena bhāvārthebhyaḥ kriyā</q> pratīyata
ityuk‍tam । atrābhidhīyate । bhāvārtha evātrāpi vidhīyate dadhnā
juhotīti । iyāṃstu viśeṣaḥ । dhātvarthānubandhāvacchinnaḥ ।
kārakamapi hi kriyāvacche(dakameva)denaiva ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b463"/>
kārakavyāpārāvacche(dakā)da eva dhātavaḥ pravartante । tadapi avibhāgataḥ
kārakaviśeṣaśravaṇe sa eva vibhāgenāvagamyate । tataḥ kiṃ ? vibhāga-
śravaṇe hi vibhak‍tasyaiva vidheyatā avagamyate । na punaravibhak‍tasya
dhātvarthasya । tasmādyatra dhātvarthāvagati(teḥ)statra dhātvarthavidhānam ।
tatsannidhau vibhāgāvagateḥ vibhāgamātravidhānam । ataḥ siddhaṃ tatsannidheḥ
guṇārthena punaḥ śrutiriti । juhoteruccāraṇamanuvādaḥ guṇasambandhārthaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b464"/>
<p><q>yadi juhotītyanuvādaḥ kenedānīṃ guṇo vidhīyata iti ?</q>
ko'yaṃ praśnaḥ । nanu ca vidhidvayamapyabhyupagatameva agnihotraṃ juhotīti
dadhnā juhotīti ca । tadevedaṃ nopapadyata ityabhiprāyaḥ । kathamanupapattiḥ ?
ekaiveyaṃ kartavyatā'vibhak‍tā । vibhaktau tvanubandhau । na cānubandho dadhyādiḥ
vidheyaḥ । kiṃ tarhi anubandhaḥ । ekatvācca vidhidvayasyāviṣayaḥ ।
tasmādekaṃ vākyaṃ vidhiśūnyam । tacca āśritatvāt guṇasaṃbandhyeveti ।
punarapyavivakṣaiva guṇānubandhasya vākyārtho yaḥ taṃ vidhātumityanubandha-
vistārāt bhāvavistāra ityuk‍tam । tasmādviniyoga eva
﻿<pb n="b465"/>
vidherapi viṣayopapattiḥ । <q>yaduktaṃ nāstyāghārasya prakṛtadravyadevatamiti
kimevaṃ sati dravyadevateneti ।</q> vidhāyakādeva (vi)śeṣāvagatirityu-
k‍tam । na ca nāsti vacanāntaravihitaṃ astyeveti siddhaṃ nānuvādā&mdash;
viti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b466"/>
<p><q>dravyasaṃyogāccodanā paśusomayoḥ ।</q> kiṃ punaḥ pūrvādhikaraṇenāsya
vaiṣamyam । idamasti vaiṣamyam&mdash;rasahṛdayādibhyo dravyāntaraṃ paśusomau ।
evaṃ tarhi pūrvapakṣa eva nāsti । na ca nāsti, kramasamuccayau hi pūrvapakṣahetubhūtau
﻿<pb n="b467"/>
ekārthatvādavadānadevatā vikalpyanta iti pūrvapakṣavādī manyate । na
cātyantāsaṃbaddhamevedaṃ hṛdayādibhyaḥ paśutvam । na ca somādrasaḥ
tasmādanuvādo nyāyya iti manyate । kathaṃ punaḥ aindravāyavaṃ gṛhṇātīti
hṛdayasyāgne'vadyatīti yāgacodanā । grahaṇe tāvat dravyadevatāsaṃyogāt
nirvapativat gṛhṇātirbhaviṣyatītyabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b468"/>
avadyatau tu kathaṃ ? atrāpi yāgagatasaṃskāradarśanāt phalacamasa&mdash;
vat karmacodanā bhaviṣyatītyamiprāyaḥ । yuk‍taṃ phalacamase nirjñātayāgaśe-
﻿<pb n="b469"/>
ṣasya, avadyatau punarmṛgyo'sau । saṃskārāditi cenna ; vatsamāla-
bhetetyanaikāntyāt । nanu cāprayojanavataḥ saṃskāro na bhaviṣyatīti
yuk‍taiva karmakalpanā । varaṃ tṛtīyārthe ṣaṣṭhī na punaḥ karmakalpanā ।
﻿<pb n="b470"/>
keyamanupāsitaguroḥ svapratibhāvataḥ ṣaṣṭhīkalpanā । bhavantu saṃskārā
avadyaticodanāḥ agnīṣomasaṃbandhāttu yāvatsaṃskāraṃ yāgacodanāḥ
saṃpadyante । tataśca pracayānuvādaḥ ālabhatiriti siddham । tataśca
kramasamuccayadarśanamupapannārthaṃ bhavati । nacānuvāde lakṣaṇādoṣaḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b471"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyate । naitacchabdādavagantu śakyate । somena yajeteti
somalatāviśiṣṭo yajirgamyate । rasadravyakāśca gṛhṇātayaḥ । (arthāt)
ato rūpāntarāvagamānnānuvādaḥ śakyate'vagantum । anuvāde sati lakṣaṇā
tataścānuvāda itītaretarāśrayaḥ । karmāntare punaḥ svato'rthāntarāvagamā-
n‍nyāyyam । eṃva(vai)paśāvapi । paśuśabdo hi pucchavati vartate ।
hṛdayādayastu māṃsasaṃsthānavacanāḥ । tasmānnānuvādaḥ saṃbhavati ।
kramasamuccayadarśanaṃ ca grahaṇādīnāṃ karmāntaratve'pi naiva viruddham ।
﻿<pb n="b472"/>
kintu somena yajena paśumālabheta iti yadaine karmacodane tadā'vadyati-
gṛhṇātyoḥ saṃskārakarmataivāvasīyate । kasmāt ? tadā hi gṛhyamāṇa-
pradhāno gṛhṇātiḥ[na] gṛhyamāṇaguṇā śakyate kalpayitum । nāpi
nirvapativat yāgavidhānārthaṃ prāptānuvādaḥ śakyate vak‍tum । nanu ca
dravyadevatāsaṃbandhāt na gṛhṇātimātraparyavasāyinī codanā śakyate
vak‍tum sauryaṃ caruṃ nirvapeditivat । na ca somena yajeteti devatā prāptā
yā'nūdyeta saṃskāraṃ vidhātum ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b473/>
na ca saṃskāre devatā kārakabhāvaṃ pratipadyate yāgasyaiva hi kārakaṃ devatā
na grahaṇādeḥ । ato'prāptadravyadevatāsaṃyogāt karmāntarāṇyevaitāni ।
na somena yajetetyatra saṃskāra iti śakyate vak‍tuṃ sauryaṃ caruṃ
nirvapeditivat ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b474"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyate-kutaścidupādānaṃ grahaṇamityucyate । upādānañcātmārthaṃ
vā syāt parārthaṃ vā । tatra devatāśravaṇāt devatārthamiti gamyate । nanu
na jātitaḥ kācit devatā nāma vidyate । yā hi yasya haviṣaḥ saṃba&mdash;
ndhitvena codyate sā tasya devateti । na ca somarasasyendravāyvādayaḥ
prāptaḥ yena tadarthamupādānamityavadhāryate । athātraiva rasasya devatā codyate
na tarhi grahaṇacodanā kintu devatāvidhiparamevaitadvākyaṃ syāt ।
tadā ca kramasamuccayadarśanaṃ nopapadyate । gṛhṇātiśca pramādapāṭhaḥ
kriyānuvādo vā syāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b475"/>
<p>tasmāt devatāviśiṣṭaṃ grahaṇaṃ codyata iti durbhaṇamidam । na
brūmo devatāviśiṣṭaṃ grahaṇaṃ codyata iti । ki tarhi ? indra-
vāyūddeśaviśiṣṭaṃ grahaṇaṃ rasasya । tataḥ kim ? idaṃ tato
bhavati । yāgaśeṣatvād‌dravyasya indravāyvarthatvācca grahaṇasya gṛhyamāṇa-
mukhaṃ ca tādarthyaṃ grahaṇasya । ata indravāyvartho rasa iti gamyate ।
nendravāyū rasārthau yāvad‍grahaṇaṃ ca tādarthyaṃ na yāvadyāga&mdash;
bhāvi । ata eva ca na yāge codanā grahaṇeṣu devatātvaṃ ca
yāgārtharasatādarthyāt । na punaḥ codanātaḥ nātrendravāyvādayo
﻿<pb n="b476"/>
devatātvena codyante । ata kāryatastatra devatātvaṃ nopadeśataḥ ।
upadeśo hi grahaṇasyendravāyvarthatāparyavasāyyeva । tasmādupapannāḥ
saṃskāracodanāgrahaṇādayaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>tadbhedāt karmaṇo'bhyāsaḥ ।</q> evaṃ ca kṛtvā kramasamuccayopapattiḥ ।
uk‍taṃ ca yāvad‍grahaṇabhāvīndravāyvādīnāṃ saṃbandho na yāvadyāgabhāvīti ।
﻿<pb n="b477"/>
yāgaśeṣaścāsau sakalo daśamuṣṭiprabhavo rasaḥ । ato'yāgārthatvā-
dindravāyvoḥ sakalasya ca somarasasya yāgārthatvāt yāvad‍grahaṇa-
bhāvitvācca saṃbandhasya indravāyvāderavaśyamāvṛttyā bhavitavyam । satyāṃ
cāvṛttau siddhaḥ samuccayaḥ । na ca sarvasyaiva somarasasya
anyasyānyasya coheśena grahaṇaṃ bhavati। tasmādavayavaśo grahaṇam ।
tathā ca pātraparimāṇadarśanam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b478"/>
<p>na ca vibhāgena grahaṇaṃ punarekī karaṇam । na ca dṛṣṭe saṃbhavati
adṛṣṭārthatā uddeśasya saṃbhavati । adṛṣṭārthasya vā grahaṇādeḥ(gṛhṇāteḥ)dṛṣṭārthatā
tasmādavayavānāmeva devatoddeśena tyāgaḥ । na caitāvatā karmabhedo
bhavati । somena yajetetyabhinnāvagateḥ । tasmāt sa eva punaḥ
punarāvartata iti siddham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b479"/>
<p><q>saṃskārastu na bhidyeta ।</q> khadirādiṣu punaḥ saṃskāraśeṣabhāvā-
vagamāt yuk‍to vikalpaḥ ।</p>
<p><note n="(1)"> Page 473.</note>athaindravāyavādiṣu prakṛteṣu yāgeṣu latā vidhīyata ityucyate, na
sā śakyā vākyenaindravāyavī vijñātum śrutyā hi rasaḥ aindravāyava iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b480"/>
nanu cedamayuktam । prakṛtidravyatayā hi latāvidhānamanirastaṃ syāt ।
rasakāryavidhānaṃ cāsaṃbhavadevāśāṅkitam । tasmāt vrīhibhiryajetetivat
dravyaprakṛtidravyatayā latāvidhānamupapadyata eva somena yajeteti ।</p>
<p>kiṃ nāma nāśaṅkayate mūḍhamatibhiḥ puroḍāśo hyanirūpitaprakṛti-
dravyaka āg‍neyādiṣu pratīyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b481"/>
<p>tena yuk‍taṃ tatra prakṛtiviśeṣavidhānam । iha punaraindravāya-
vādiṣu somarasa evāvasīyate । kimatra prakṛtidravyavidhānaṃ karipyati ।
tasmādanāśaṅkanīya evāyaṃ pakṣaḥ । havirviśeṣaśaṅkā nopapadyata eveti nirastā
bhāṣyakāreṇa ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b482"/>
<p><q>pṛthak‌tvaniveśitvāt saṅkhayayā karmabhedaḥ syāt ।</q> prājā-
patyāniti prājāpatyaprātipadikāt vibhaktaya utpadyante । yataścotpadyante
tad‌yuk‍taṃ svārthamabhivadanti । taddhitāntaṃ caitat prātipadikam । tataḥ
taddhitāntasyaiva idaṃ bahutvaṃ na kevalasya taddhitārthasya । ataḥ saṃśaya
﻿<pb n="b483"/>
evātra nopapadyate । prājāpatyāḥ saptadaśetyevāvagamyate na punaḥ
saptadaśaprājāpatyā iti । ato vikalpavilasita evātra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>
<p>ucyate । pratyayārthagatamevātra vibhak‍tayaḥ svārthaṃ pratipādayituṃ
kṣamāḥ na prakṛtyarthagataṃ, kutaḥ ? prakṛtyarthasya pratyayārthopasarjanatvāt । pradhānaṃ
hi arthāntareṇa saṃbadhyate, nopasarjanam । nanu caivamapi sandeho
nopapadyate । upasarjanārthasya bhedānavagamāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b484"/>
<p>satyamevametat । pradhānārtha evātra kiṃ bhinnaḥ san upasarjanena
yuktaḥ uta sopasarjano bhinna iti । evaṃ saṃśaye sati pūrvapakṣavādī
manyate bhinnasyopasarjanayogo yuktaḥ prakṛtyarthasya bhedāvagame pramāṇā&mdash;
bhāvāt । bahutvāvagamapūrvikā hyekaśeṣakalpanā । ataḥ pratyayārthasyai-
vaikaśeṣo bhavatu । tadbhedāvagamāt । na punarabhinnasyāpi prakṛtyarthasya ।
tasmādubhayasiddhamekayāgāvadhāraṇameva yuktam । tadidamuktam&mdash;<q>yo hi
bahūn yāgān kalpayati kalpayatyasāvekamiti ।</q> kathaṃ panarasmin pakṣe
anekasmādekādaśāvadānasiddhiḥ ?</p>
﻿<pb n="b485"/>
<p>arthādāvṛttirbhaviṣyati । grahaṇabhedājjyotiṣṭomasyeva । atro-
cyate । na saptadaśabhirekaṃ karmopapadyate । kutaḥ ? ekādaśabhiravadānaiḥ
paśuyāgaḥ siddhayati । sa caikādaśāvadānagaṇaḥ ekasmādeva paśoḥ
siddhayatīti na paśvantaraṃ devatayā saṃbandhayituṃ śakyate । tataśca
prājāpatyāniti bahutvānupapattiḥ ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b486"/>
<p>nanu cok‍taṃ pratipaśvavadānagaṇasya āvṛttiḥ saptadaśānāṃ yāga-
saṃbandhārthaṃ gṛhṇātīnāmiva jyotiṣṭomasya । yuktam jyotiṣṭome gṛhṇātīnā-
mupadeśāt । atra punaḥ kāryato'vadānagaṇaḥ prāpnoti । sa ca
yāgasya saptadaśapaśudravyako'yameko yāgaḥ । yāgasaṃbandhācca haviṣyava-
dānam । ataḥ kenātra pratipaśvavadānagaṇaprāptiḥ haviṣṭvenaikatvāt
paśūnām । havirbhede hi sati havissaṃskārabhede vā pradhānasyā-
vṛttirbhavati iha tad‍dvayaṃ nāsti । nātra saṃskāranibandhanaṃ pṛthaktvam ।
﻿<pb n="b487"/>
havirnibandhano haviḥ saṃskārabhedaḥ । tasmādyāgaikatvapakṣe saptadaśasaṅkhayā&mdash;
nvayo na ghaṭate । kimidamanyāyyamuktam । yāganirūpaṇottarakālaṃ
hi saṃskāraprāptiḥ na saṃskārāpekṣaṃ yāganirūpaṇam । saptadaśapasūdravyaścāya-
meko yāgo nirūpitaḥ evaṃbhūtasya saṃskāro yadi āvṛttyā anāvṛttyā vā na
saṃbhavati bādhyatāṃ nāma kṛṣṇalacarāvi(dam)vāvaghātaḥ। na punastadvaśā-
﻿<pb n="b488"/>
dutpattau vākyārthaḥ śakyate nirūpayitum । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ । kiṃ
sopasarjanasya bhedaḥ utābhinnasyopasarjanayogaḥ ityasmin
saṃśaye vākyaśeṣād‍yuk‍to nirṇaya iti । kasmādvākyaśeṣāt ?
prakṛtivaditi । nāyaṃ vākyaśeṣaḥ । kāryataḥ prāptimaṅgānāṃ
darśayituṃ vākyaśeṣo'yaṃ vyākhyātdṛṇām । na punarupadeśe'ṅgānāṃ
﻿<pb n="b489"/>
na ca kāryata upadeśanirūpaṇam । upadeśāddhi kāryaṃ nirūpyate ।
na cātra saṃśayo vidyate । uktaṃ bhedāvagamapūrvakaṃ ekaśeṣavacanam । pradhānasya
ca vibhaktiyogāt bhedo'vagamyate nopasarjanasyeti । tasmāt pūrvapakṣa
evātra jyāyāniti ekaśeṣavido manyante ।</p>
<p>atrocyate । satyaṃ pratyayārthasya bhedo'vagamyate na punarupa-
sarjanarahitasya । kutaḥ ? prakṛtipratyaryasamudāyādvibhaktyutpatteḥ ।
na vibhaktitaḥ pratyayotpādaḥ । tataḥ kim ? idaṃ tataḥ । prakṛti&mdash;
yuktaṃ hi vibhaktyarthena yujyate na vibhaktyarthayuk‍taṃ prakṛtyā ।
﻿<pb n="b490"/>
tasmāt saptadaśa yāgāḥ pratīyante, na saptadaśadravyako yāgaḥ । ataḥ
karmagataiṣā saṅkhayā, na dravyagatā । evaṃ ca sati naiveyaṃ karmāṇi vidhīyate
yenāruṇavat dravyamukhenopakāritā syāt । ataḥ siddhaṃ pṛthaktvaniveśitvāt
saṅkhayayā karmabheda iti । taccaikapaśūnāṃ pṛthaktvaṃ bahuṣu yāgeṣu avakalpate
naikasminniti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b491"/>
kaḥ punaratra heturabhipreto bhāṣyakārasya ? nanu caikādaśāvadānānu-
papattiḥ । aheturayaṃ na kāryataḥ śāstrāvadhāraṇamiti । ucyate । naiva
kāryeṇa śāstramavadhāryate । śās‍treṇaivedaṃ kāryamavadhṛtam । uk‍taṃ hi sopa-
sarjanasya bhedo'vagamyata iti । evaṃ sati ekādaśāvadānabodho na śakyate
vak‍tum । ekasmāccāsau niṣpannaḥ । kutaḥ ? sopasarjanaḥ pratyayārthaḥ
dvitīyāderupasarjanasaṃbandhānupapattiḥ । ataśca saptadaśasaṅkṣayā paśuṣu
na syāt । upasarjanārthāvacchedo hi saṅkhayāniveśe hetuḥ ।
﻿<pb n="b492"/>
tadanupapattau saṅkhayāniveśānupapattiḥ । na cānyaḥ kaścit avacchedako
vidyate ekarūpaśravaṇāt । nānārūpaśravaṇe hi teṣāmanyatam iti
syādapi saṅkhayāniveśaḥ । na tadasti । tasmāt paśuṣūpapadyate nānyatheti
yuk‍tamuktam ।</p>
<p>1<q>nanvekasminnapi yāge saptadaśabhiravadānagaṇaiḥ pakṣyate vaca-
nāditi ।</q> kimidamuktam ? idamuktam । yadyapi sopasarjanasya
bhedo'vagamyate, tathāpi pradhānabhedādevopasarjanasya bhedo na bhavatu । sābhūt
﻿<pb n="b493"/>
pradhānasyaiva svataḥ kimevaṃ bhaviṣyati ? idameva bhaviṣyati । sapta&mdash;
daśasaṅkhayā haviṣo vikārikā bhaviṣyati, na punaryāgasya । bhavatyevamidaṃ
yadi haviṣaḥ saṅkhayā śrūyate iyaṃ punaḥ paśuṣu śrūyate । ko viśeṣaḥ ?
ayamasti viśeṣaḥ । paśūnāmupasarjanayogāt । tatsaṃbandhāvagatireva
bhinnā'vagamyate na havirmātram । ato yāgabhedaḥ prayojanamuktam ।</p>
<p><q>saṃjñā cotpattisaṃyogāt ।</q> <quote>“athaiva jyotirathaiṣa viśvajyotiḥ
athaiṣa sarvajyotiḥ”</quote> kathaṃ punarevamādīnāṃ</p>
﻿<pb n="b494"/>
karmavacanatā'vasīyate । bhāvārthasāmānādhikaraṇyāddhi nāmadheyatvamuktam ।
na ca tadihāsti । kevalanāmaśravaṇāt । tasmāt kathamatra
saṃśayaḥ ? kiṃ prakṛtasya karmaṇo vācakā uta vakṣyamāṇasyeti ।
ucyate । astyatrāpi sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ bhāvaśabdena । etacchabdāvamarśaḥ
<quote>‘sa ya evaṃ vidvānetena yajeta’</quote> ityevamādiṣu ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b495"/>
tasmādupapannaḥ saṃśayaḥ । atra pūrvapakṣavādī manyate&mdash;darśapūrṇamāsavat
prakṛtānāṃ karmaṇāṃ sākaṃ prasthāyyavadvā prakṛtasya karmaṇo vācakā iti ।
tasmāttasyaivedaṃ punarvacanaṃ guṇāntarasaṃbandhārthamityevaṃ prāptam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b496"/>
<p>atrocyate&mdash;saṃjñāpyutpattyaiva arthāntarāvabodhamutpādayati । kimida-
mutpattyaiveti ? uccāryamāṇaivetyarthaḥ । anyatvaṃ cāvagataṃ viśeṣāntarā-
bhāvāt । punaranyārthatayā na gṛhyeta sākaṃprasthāyyavat । yatra punarviśe&mdash;
ṣo&mdash;vagamyate prakṛtādanyatra kimiti tatrautpattikaṃ bhedavijñānaṃ kathyate ।
asti cāyaṃ sahasradakṣiṇādibhiḥ viśeṣaiḥ viśiṣṭaḥ prakṛtādanyaḥ । tasmāt
karmāntaraṃ saṃjñāta iti siddham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b497"/>
<p><q>guṇaścāpūrvasaṃyoge ।</q> kathaṃ punaratra saṃśayaḥ ? yadā vaiśvadevaśabde-
nāmikṣāsaṃbandho vājiśabdena vājinasaṃbandhaḥ । śabdena ca dek‍topakaroti
iti <quote>‘vidhiśabdasya mantratve bhāvaḥ syāt’</quote> ityatroktam । ato'rthaikye'pi
devatāntaramevaitat । yathā sauryacarāvāditye ca । ucyate । yatra hi śabdā-
deva devatā'vagamyate tatraivam, yatra punaḥ prakṛtopalakṣaṇaparaḥ śabdādiḥ tatra
﻿<pb n="b498"/>
pūrvaśabdabhidheyaiva devatā । anyābhidheyatayaiva lakṣaṇā lakṣayati ।
na svābhidheyatāmāpādayituṃ kṣamā । tasmādupapadyate saṃśayaḥ kimayaṃ
lakṣaṇayā vājibhya ityayaṃ śabdo'nveti utābhidhāneneti । nanu
ca yaugikatvāt vājibhya iti naiva lakṣaṇā śakyate vak‍tum । sāmīpye
tadvati vā lakṣaṇā, na punaḥ yāgāvagatau । nimittāntara&mdash;
balena hi lakṣaṇā'vagamyate । na padādeva । yogastu padāvagamya
﻿<pb n="b499"/>
eva । tasmāllakṣaṇānupapattiḥ । atrābhidhīyate&mdash;kimatra rūḍhiryogo vā
kariṣyati ? parābhidheyatā lakṣaṇāhetuḥ । taccātra vidyata iti pūrvapakṣa-
vādino'bhiprāyaḥ । vyaktiniṣṭhatvādyaugikānāṃ vaiśvadevaśabdācca vyakti-
viśeṣāvagamāt । tasmād‌guṇadvayaviśiṣṭamekaṃ karmeti pūrvapakṣitam ।
siddhāntavādī tu manyate&mdash;yadyapi prakṛtavyaktyavagamo bhavati tathāpi
karmāntaramevaitat । āmikṣopasarjanatayā pratīyamānatvāt viś‍veṣāṃ devānām ।
﻿<pb n="b500"/>
nahyanyopasarjanaṃ anyasaṃbandhitayā śakyate'vagantum ; rājapuruṣaṃ
paśyetivat । tasmādanayorekenāsaṃbandhaḥ । ataḥ saṃbandhadvayā-
vagamādekatve'pi saṃbandhinaḥ karmabhedaḥ । atha kasmād‍yugapat aruṇā-
vatsaṃbandho na bhavati । kimevaṃ ? ekatvenāvagatirbhaviṣyati । satyamevaṃ
﻿<pb n="b501"/> 
yatraikapramāṇāvagamyaḥ saṃbandhaḥ । nānāpramāṇagamye punaḥ anivāryaiva
bhedāvagatiḥ । tasmāt karmāntaram । nānāpramāṇagamyatā śrutyā
vāk‍yena ceti vadatā darśitā । iha tarhi kathaṃ pramāṇabhede'pi dadhnau juhoti
payasā juhoti ityekat‍vaṃ karmaṇaḥ ? anupasarjanatvāvagateḥ । nātra
anyopasarjano homo'nyena saṃbadhyata  iti aviruddhā prakṛtāvagatiḥ ।
ato bhinnānāmapi śāstrāṇāṃ abhinnātmakakāryamiti vaiṣamyam । aprakṛta-﻿<pb n="b502"/>
grahaṇaṃ devatāntaragrahaṇaṃ ca devatāntarasaṃbandhābhiprāyam; na padārthābhiprāyaṃ
padārthābhede'pi bhedāvagamādityuktam । nātra padārthabhedaḥ śak‍yate vak‍tum
annayogādviśveṣāṃ devānām । tasmāt saṃbandhitaivātra bhinnatve heturiti
siddham ।</p>﻿<pb n="b503"/> 
<p>adhikaraṇāntaraṃ veti vadataḥ ko'bhiprāyo bhāṣyakārasya ?
nanu ca guṇārthena punaḥ śrutirityatra naivaitāni karmāntarāṇatyuktam ।
atra vadāmaḥ, ayamabhiprāyo bhāṣyakārasya । atrāpi dadhyupasarjana-
tayā'vagamyate । ato'nubandhāntarasaṃbandhāt naikāvagamyamanubanghaṃ
bhavati । tasmāt pradhānasyāp‍yupasarjanasyevānyasaṃbandhasya nānyena saṃbandha
upapadyate । rāddhāntastu&mdash;satmevaṃ yadyasaṃbaddhasya samarpakaṃ nāsti
vaiśvadevavat, iha cāgnihotraṃ juhotīti sarvānubandhasaṃbandhitayā﻿<pb n="b504"/> 
asaṃbandhamevānubandhāntaramavagamyata iti vaiṣamyam । vikalpopanyāsastu
phalapradarśanaṃ bhedāvagamasiddhayartham । uk‍tena nyāyena na bhedaḥ
siddhayatīti vikalpasiddhiḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b505"/> ﻿<pb n="b506"/>
<p><q>phalaśrutestu karma syāt ।</q> atha kimarthamidamanumānamupanyastam ?
punaśca vikal‍pasamādyā jātayaḥ । asiddhānaikāntikaviruddhābhidhānasyāna-
vasara eva । bhedābhedaparīkṣaṇaṃ hyatra prakṛtam । tacca śabdānta-
rādisamadhigamyam । kimatrānumānena kriyate tad‍dūṣaṇena vā ।</p>﻿<pb n="b507"/> 
tasmādasaṃbaddhamevedaṃ granthakhaṇḍalakaṃ karmabhedābhedavido manyante । ato
yadeva vāk‍yabhedabhayāt karmāntaratvamuk‍taṃ vaktavyaṃ pūrvapakṣe ।
na punaḥ pramāṇāntaramupanyasanīyam । atrocyate&mdash;nanu na śrutaṃ
bhavatā śāstrabhedapratipattiranena lakṣaṇena kriyata iti । na ca śāstrā-
cchāstrabhedo'vagamyate । kiṃ tarhi ? anubandhānyatvāvagamya eva । tasya
cānyatvaṃ pramāṇāntarāvagamyameva । taccedaṃ dadhnā'nubandhaṃ karma na
karmaśāstraṃ bhinattītyuktam । karmavattayā cākarmaṇi vidhānamuktam ।﻿<pb n="b508"/>
evaṃ cet phalānubandhe'pi karmāpannameva guṇarūpaṃ na svataḥ phalena
saṃbandhayituṃ śak‍yate । ataḥ karmaṇā phalasaṃbandhāt karmāntaramidaṃ
phalāntarānubandhāditi pūrvapakṣī manyate ।</p>﻿<pb n="b509"/>
evamap‍yanumānabhāṣyaṃ kathaṃ ? it‍thamidaṃ idamanumānabhāṣyam । kiṃ
kāryataḥ karmāpattiṃ dravyāṇāṃ manyate bhavān ? yadi hi kāryataḥ
karmāpattiḥ syāt akarmabhūtasya kāryayogo na vidyata iti bhavati phalānta-
rānubandhāt karmāntaram । atha tu niyogavaśāt karmāpattiravasīyate
yāvanniyogaviṣayaiva sā bhavati । na hi kāryataḥ sā śak‍yā'vagantum ।﻿<pb n="b510"/>
śeṣavadanumānagamyo hi kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ । tena ca kāraṇamātrāvagatireva na
punaṃrviśeṣasyaiva kāraṇatāvagatiḥ । nanu ca sāmānyato dṛṣṭaṃ karmaṇa eva
phalaṃ prati kāraṇatāmavagamayatītyabhiprāyaḥ kṛṣ‍yādiṣu darśanāt । tadi&mdash;
dānīṃ sāmānyaṃ kimiti na vidmaḥ sādṛśyaṃ tāvat samudṛśena vyavadhīyate﻿<pb n="b511"/>
atha viśeṣamātraṃ, kṛṣyantarameva prāpnotīti । atha sādhanādyanubandhakṛtaṃ
tatpāpi dvayamāpatati sādhanaviśeṣo vā'nubandhatayā gṛhyate ? sādhanamātraṃ
vā ? viśeṣagrahaṇe phaladevatayoranyatvānna sāmānyāvagatiḥ । atha sāmānyaṃ,
na, kriyātvamātrameva tatra avaśiṣyate । tasmiṃśca sāmānye'naikāntikatvaṃ﻿<pb n="b512"/>
viruddhatā ca sarvatra guṇakarmāvagateḥ । tasmānna kāryataḥ
karmāpattirdravyāṇāṃ śak‍yate'vagantum । kiṃ tarhi ? niyogata
eva bhāvāpattiranugamanīyā, sa, cāyaṃ niyogo dadhisādhanaṃ homameva phala-
sambandhitayā'vagamayatīti karmabhedaḥ । anyathā hi homāsaṃbandhānna
dadhnaḥ prāpnoti । evaṃ cātra dadhnaḥ karmāpattiḥ prāpnoti । na ca sā
tasmādvāk‍yādavasīyate । anavagamyamānā phale na saṃbadhyata ityuktam ।﻿<pb n="b513"/>
kimiti vā dadhnā homo nirvartyate yadi na homārthaṃ dadhi syāt । tasmāt
padadvayānvita evāyamarthaḥ phalena saṃbadhyata iti karmāntaratvam । anyathā
hyāśritatvātprayogasyetyayuktiḥ syāt yadi kevalasyāpi phalena saṃbandhaḥ
syāt । ato(dhātu)viśiṣṭabhāvānupraveśitaiva phalasaṃbandhe hetuḥ । kambala-
nirṇejanopanyāsastu na kāryataḥ karmāpattiriti prakaṭayati । kathaṃ tarhi ?
viniyogāt kāryamiti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b514"/>
<p><q>atulyatvāt‍tu vāk‍yayorguṇe ।</q> atrābhidhīyate&mdash;satyaṃ karmatāmā-
pannasya guṇasya vidhānam । na punaḥ karmārthatayaiveti । kasmāt ? kriyākāraka-﻿<pb n="b515"/>
lakṣaṇaṃ hi saṃbandhamāśritya dravyāṇāṃ tadāpattiḥ । na punaḥ
tādarthyaṃ, akarmaṇaḥ akārakatvaprasaṅgāt । ataḥ phalārthataiva kārakabhūtasya
dadhnaḥ pratīyate । homārthatve vāk‍yabhedastvavaivoktaḥ । viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ
kimiti nāśrīyate ? agnihotraṃ juhotīti homāvacchinnasya karmaṇaḥ
prāptatvāt dadhyanubandhasya cāpraptatvāt tāvatā indriyakāmādhikāranirvṛtteḥ na
śak‍yate prāptirbādhitum । nanu cāpṛthagavagamādanubandhadvayasya na pṛthak‍tve-
nāvacchedaḥ śak‍yate'vagantum ।</p>﻿<pb n="b516"/>
<p>ucyate । kimatra pṛthak‍tvenāvacchedaḥ kariṣyati yāvadaprāptaṃ
hi niyogasya viṣaya ityuktam । karmāpatteśca juhotirviṣayaḥ ।
tasmājjuhotyavacchinnavyāpārāśrito dadhivyāpāraḥ phalayā codyate ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b517"/>
kimidaṃ āśrita iti ? kārakatāmāpanna ityarthaḥ । tasmāt
home kārakaṃ phalāya codyate । kena punaḥ phale(na)viniyuk‍taṃ tat ? karma-
vāk‍yena viniyuktam । adhikārānupapattyeti cet । tulyamatrāpi । <q>ata
evoce vṛttikāreṇeti ।</q> vṛttikāravacanaṃ kiṃparaṃ bhāṣyakārasya ? idaṃ-
param । kārakāpattirevāśrayaśabdenocyate nārthāntaramiti pradarśayitum ।
ata evāśritatvātprayogasya ityatrāpi ayamevārthaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b518"/> 
<p><q>bādhyatetarāṃ śrutiriti<note n="(1)"> P. 515</note></q>। kaḥ punaratra tarabarthaḥ । ekatra homo
vidhīyate । anyatra dadh‍yarthaḥ । na kaścidatiśayaḥ pakṣadvaye'pi dṛśyate । 
ucyate । ayamasti viśeṣaḥ dadhipade hi bādhyamāne homapadamapi
bādhitaṃ bhavati । ataḥ tatsaṃbandhena hi tadvidheyamityuk‍tam । āśri&mdash;
tatvātprayogasyeti । tasmāt sambandhibādhe saṃbandhyantarabādhaḥ । so'yaṃ
tarabarthaḥ homamātrabādhe tu na kiñcidbādhitam । kevalasyānavagamāt ।
prāptimātratayā hi kevalāvagatiḥ । <q>kathamiti ? anayā'gnihotreti-
kartavyatayaiveti ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="b519"/> 
<p>nanu coparitanaṣaṭ‍kacinteyam । kimityatropanyasyate ?
astyatropanyāsakāraṇam । kiṃ tat ? idaṃ tat ? guṇaphalasaṃbandhe
hi itikartavyatāsaṃbandho na śak‍yate avadhārayitum । na cetikartavyatā&mdash;
śūnyo'dhikāravidhiḥ । kuta etat ? adhikāraniṣṭho hi vidhiḥ niyogārtha-
sādhyatayā'vagamyate । na ca sādhyamanitikartavyatākamasti, ananu-
gṛhītasya karaṇatvānupapatteḥ । sarvadā hi karaṇaṃ karaṇaṃ syāt । kathaṃ punaḥ na
śak‍yate'vadhārayitum । upadeśatastāvan‍na saṃbhavati । nityānityasaṃyoga-
virodhāt । atideśastarhi bhavatu ? so'pi nopapadyata
ityabhiprāyaḥ । kathaṃ nopapadyate ? dhātvarthasyānyaprayuktatvāt ।﻿<pb n="b520"/> 
tatprayogāśritatvācca guṇaphalasaṃbandhasya । anyaprayogaprayuktasyānyena saṃbandho
na ghaṭate uk‍taṃ yajātithyāyā ityatra । atideśo'pi naivāprayojakasya ।
tasmād‍durbhaṇeyaṃ guṇādhikāracodanā । na cātra prasaṅgaḥ śak‍yate vak‍tum
prāp‍tyabhāvāt । prāptasya hi dharmajātasyānyadīyena dharmajātena kārya-
siddhiḥ prasaṅgaḥ । na cātra prāptirastīti darśitamupadeśātideśayora&mdash;
﻿<pb n="b521"/>
bhāvāt । ataḥ kimatra sannidhiḥ codanāliṅgaṃ vā karoti । atrocyate ।
bhavatvatideśātsaṃbandhaḥ । nanu ca paraprayogāśrayī guṇaprayogavidhirityuktam ।
nāyaṃ doṣaḥ । anyaprayuktasyānyena saṃbandhopadeśo nopapadyata iti । ati-
deśe punaḥ [kāryataḥ saṃbandhamatideśavido manyante । tataḥ kiṃ ? kāryataḥ
saṃbandhe hi viniyogāvagaterna virodhaḥ । yatra hi kāraṇapurassarā kāryāvagatiḥ
sa viniyogasya viṣayaḥ yatra punaḥ] kāryataḥ kāraṇāvagatiḥ so'tideśasya ।﻿<pb n="b522"/>
tasmānna viniyogavaiṣamyāt vighāto yadātithyāyāṃ itivat । tasmāt
sūk‍taṃ <quote>‘anayā agnihotretikartavyatayā’</quote> iti । atha kasmādagnihotra-
mevetikartavyatā na bhavati ? āśraya evānugrāhako dravyāṇām kāryaṃ
sādhayatām, āśritatvāt prayogasyeti darśanam । bāliśabhāṣitametat ।
agnihotrameva karaṇaṃ dadh‍yanuraktamityuk‍tam । kevalasyānavaga-
māt । prayuk‍tistu kevalāśrayaprāp‍tyanusāreṇeti guṇaphalamityucyate ।﻿<pb n="b523"/>
tasmāt ṣaṣṭhīsamāsa evāyaṃ agnihotretikartavyatayeti । atideśaprāptasya ca
dharmajātasya prasaṅgāt kāryasiddhiriti siddhamanāvṛttyaiva anuṣṭhānam ।
<q><quote>“atha vā dadhiśabdasya vivakṣitārthatvāt”</quote></q> iti । kimidaṃ pakṣāntara-
mivopanyasyate । kimiti vā na pakṣāntaraṃ ? tadevaṃ hi dadhyanurak‍taṃ homarūpaṃ
phalāyetyupasaṃhṛtam । yuk‍taṃ caitat । saṃbandhasyānurāgā(bhā)vagamyatvāt ।
ucyate । pakṣāntaraśaṅkānirākaraṇāyaitaddhāṣyam । na pakṣāntarapradarśanārtham ।</q>﻿<pb n="b524"/> 
kā punaratra pakṣāntaraśaṅkā ? dadhnā juhotīti kevalaguṇavidhānāt ।
avagatasya saṃbandhasya vidhānamastviti kecit । teṣāmidamuttaram ।
dadhiśabdasya vivakṣitatvānna saṃbandharayetyarthaḥ । ataḥ siddho guṇavidhi-
phalādhikārasaṃbandhaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>sameṣu karmayuk‍taṃ syāt ।</q> uktaṃ guṇānubandhāt karmaṇaḥ
phalamiti । tadidānīṃ kīdṛśo viṣaya iti ( nirūpyate । ) viṣaya&mdash;
nirūpaṇāyaitadadhikaraṇadvayam । nanu ca bhedābhedacintā atna lakṣaṇe﻿<pb n="b525"/> 
prakṛtā । saiveyaṃ viṣayato nirūpyate । nanu ca viparītamatredaṃ
śāstrabhedo hi guṇaphalasaṃbandho'pi vidyata eva । kathamatra tannirākaraṇādbhedaḥ ।
śāstrabhedakathā ceyāmiti bhāṣyavidaḥ । tasmādasamañjasamidaṃ bhedābheda-
nirūpaṇam । atrocyate&mdash;satyaṃ guṇaviśeṣataḥ śāstrabhedaḥ aprayo-
jakastvāśrayasyeti na bhedena vyapadiś‍yate । dhātvarthānubandhabhede punaḥ﻿<pb n="b526"/> 
saha prayok‍tṛtayā śās‍traṃ bhidyata iti bhedena vyapadeśaḥ । ata eva ca
athāto dharmajijñāseti śās‍treṇa prayok‍tṛtvābhedādabhedaṃ manvānasya ida-
muttaram । ato dhātvarthānubandhabhede guṇānubandhabhede ca viśeṣo'stīti
viṣayavirūpaṇam । kathaṃ punaḥ agniṣṭomasāma kṛtvā yajeta iti﻿<pb n="b527"/>
pūrvāparībhāvaḥ ? kathaṃ vā nāsti ? । savanadvaye hyatīte agniṣṭomasāma-
prayogaḥ । ekaścāyaṃ yajyarthaḥ । tasmādanupapattiḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu ca grahayajāvāpi sa evāyamagniṣ‍ṭut‍saṃjñako yāga ityupapadyate
pūrvāparībhāvaḥ । abhyāso hi sakalasya dhātvarthasya naikadeśasya । ata
eva nopapadyate । sakalasyānuṣṭhānāt । parastādastītyupapadyate iti
cenna । ayathābhūtatvādarthasya । yatra hi yathā pratīyamāna evārthaḥ śabdāt
svabhāvato'pi tathaiva tatrāvipratipattiḥ anyathābhāve tu nautpattikatvaṃ syāt ।
autpattikastu śabdasyārthena saṃbandha iti gaditam । ato nābhyāsavaśāt﻿<pb n="b528"/> 
kṛtvā yajeteti śabdādartha upapadyate । sābhyāsasya hi dhātvarthasya
uttarakālīnatā'vadhāryate । na caitad‍bhāṣyakāreṇāvamṛṣṭam । ucyate ।
anavamarśanīyamevaitat । samānakartṛkatvāpekṣo hyatra pūrvāparībhāvaḥ ।
sa ca pratītāvevopapadyate nānuṣṭhāne । samānakartṛkatvavyāghātāt ।
ekārthānāmanekadhātvarthānāmanuparatyā'nuṣṭhānaṃ samānakartṛtvamucyate । na ca
tatra pūrvamidaṃ kṛtvā paścādidaṃ kartavyamiti śak‍yate vak‍tum । vyavaccheda-
prasaṅgāt ।</p>﻿<pb n="b529"/>
<p>kathaṃ tarhi <quote>‘darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiṣṭ‍vā somena yajeta’</quote> iti ।
adhikāramātraṃ taditi vakṣyāmaḥ । tasmādavagatau pūrvakālatā <quote>‘mukhaṃ
vyādāya svapiti’</quote> itivat prayogasiddheḥ । kathaṃ punaratra guṇaphalā-
śaṅkā ? guṇāśravaṇāt, vāravantīyaṃ kṛtveti sannidhānācca karmaṇaḥ । 
sannihite hi karmaṇi guṇaśrutiḥ tadanubandhaparatāṃ vidherjñāpayatī-
tyuktam । ato dadh‍nendriyakāmavat guṇānubandhāt । evaṃ caita-
syeti mukhyārthaṃ padamanvayi bhavati । nanu vāravantīyaṃ revatīṣu﻿<pb n="b530"/> 
kṛtveti aprāptā revatyo vidhātavyāḥ vāravantīyasambandhitā ca । viśiṣṭa-
yāgavādino'p‍yayaṃ tulyo doṣaḥ । ataḥ saṃbandhavidhānākṣepāt bhavatāṃ
vidhānasiddhiḥ । atrābhidhīyate&mdash;nānyaprayuktāt bhāvārthācchāstrāntara-
midam । kiṃ tarhi ? tathaiva sahaiva prayuk‍tyā bhidyate śāstram । 
etaduk‍taṃ bhavati । karmaṇaḥ sakāśāt phalamiti kutaḥ ? aprāpta-
tvāt revatīnām । na guṇāt phalamiti śak‍yate vak‍tum । nanu
coktaṃ saṃbandhividhānākṣepāt revatīnāṃ vidhānasiddhiriti । satyaṃ siddhayati
na yāgānubandhatayā । guṇānubandhācca bhāvārthāt phalaṃ guṇaphala-
mityucyate na kevalād‍guṇāt phalanāmatvād‍guṇaphalānām । bhāvārtha-﻿<pb n="b531"/> 
viṣayabhāvācca niyogasya । <q>athocyeta&mdash;asyā pūrvā revatīrupādāya tāsu
ca vāravantīyaṃ kṛtvā yajñena yajeteti ।</q> anena pūrvasmāt ko viśeṣa
upanyastaḥ ? aprāptā revatyaḥ kathamupādīyante ? ayamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;revatī-
viśiṣṭaṃ vāravantīyaṃ yāgānubandhatayā pratīyamānaṃ revatīḥ ekatvavat
upādānaśeṣīkaroti । satyamevaitat । (a)tathāp‍yagniṣṭoma sāmeti
nāvakal‍pate । kimiti nāvakal‍pate ? yāgānubandhatayā hi vāra&mdash;
vantīyaṃ (pratī)vidhīyamānaṃ stotraviśeṣasaṃbandhitayā śak‍yate'vagantum ।﻿<pb n="b532"/> 
<p><q>athāg‍niṣ‍ṭomasāmnaḥ kārye bhavatītyucyata iti ।</q> kimida-
magniṣṭomasāmnaḥ kārye bhavatītyucyata iti । ayamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;yāgānu-
bandhitayā pratīyamānaṃ vāravantīyaṃ na kāryāntaraśūnyamanubandhi bhavatīti ।
kāryaviśeṣāpekṣāyāmagniṣṭomasāmaśabdaḥ kāryasamarpako bhavatīti na vāk‍ya-
bhedaḥ । <q>etasyetyetadavivakṣicaṃ syāt ।</q> kimityavivakṣitaṃ syāt ?
yadyayaṃ śabdalabhyo'rthaḥ syāt avivakṣitam । atra punaḥ prakṛta
evāyamagniṣ‍ṭut pratīyate tasyāyaṃ etasyetyanuvādaḥ । ataścāvivakṣāyā-
map‍yadoṣaḥ । tasmāt karmāntaratayopanyāso na ghaṭate, revatyādhāravāravantī&mdash;
yānubandhatabā hi na prakṛto yāgaḥ śak‍yate'vagantuṃ, ṛgantarādhāra-﻿<pb n="b533"/> 
tayāvagateḥ । nanu phalārthatve guṇasya nāyaṃ doṣaḥ godohanavat । tatra
hi camasānubandhaṃ praṇayanaṃ pratīyamānamapi godohanānubandhatayā phalārthatve
guṇānubandhasya na viruddhayate । evamatrāpi ko virodhaḥ, vak‍tavyo vā
viśeṣaḥ । ayamabhidhīyate&mdash;tatra hi ap‍praṇayanārthakāryatayā godohanasya
kevalapraṇayanābhinirvṛttyā na virodhaḥ śak‍yate vak‍tum । iha punaḥ
yāgānubandhatayā pratīyate ayāgārthaṃ ca nirvartayati na prakṛtānubandhitayā﻿<pb n="b534"/> 
śak‍yate'vagantum । prakṛtaṃ hyagniṣṭomasāma vāyavyānavubandham । tasmāt
kāryānubandhayoḥ virodhaḥ । akāryānubandhatvāt vāravantīyasya revatyādhārasya ।
tasmādetasyeti vivakṣitamityuktam । anuvādānupapatteḥ । karmāntaratve﻿<pb n="b535"/> 
punaḥ saha prayuk‍tyā śāstrabhedāt na doṣo bhavatīti । ubhayasmin vivakṣya-
māṇa ityarthaḥ । na kaścideko viniyoga ubhayānubandhitāmāpādayituṃ
kṣamaḥ । kathaṃ tarhi sādhāraṇaguṇavidhānam ? aikarūp‍ye hi tat na
guṇapradhānavyavasthitānām । kathaṃ tarhi aṅgapradhānārthatā barhirādīnām ?
kevalaprayogaśeṣatayā nāvacchedānubandhitayā । iha cānubandhāvacche&mdash;
dānubandhatve virodha uktaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b536"/> 
<p>kathaṃ punaratrāpi prayogānubandhitayaiva na vāravantīyaṃ parigṛhyate । na,
vāk‍yena yāgāvacchinnāvagateḥ । prakaraṇāvagamyā hi prayogānubandhatā । anu-
pādeyagamyā vā vāk‍yādibhirapi, sāmarthyāvagamyā vā । pradhānasambandho
dakṣiṇāvat । iha punaḥ vāk‍yena yāgānubandhataiveti etasyetyavivakṣā ।﻿<pb n="b537"/> 
<note n="(1)"> p. 533</note><q><quote>“atha karmāntare kathamavāk‍yabheda”</quote></q> iti viśiṣṭavidhānasiddheḥ praśno-
nopapadyate । avāntarastotrasaṃbandhaḥ ṛk‍sāmayornopapadyata ityabhiprāyaḥ ।
rāddhāntavādinastarhi ko'bhiprāyaḥ ? ayamabhiprāyaḥ&mdash;revatīvāravantīya-
saṃbandhaḥ stotre na syāt । yadyekabhāvaviśeṣaṇaṃ ṛgdravyaṃ sāma vā syāt । atra
punaḥ revatīvāravantīyasaṃbandhābhinirvṛtto bhāvo bhāvāntarasya viśeṣaṇam । sa ca
bhāvaviśiṣṭo bhāvo vidhīyamāno yajinā viśeṣ‍yata ityadoṣa ityābhiprāyaḥ ।﻿<pb n="b538"/> 
yuk‍taṃ tāvat abhinirvṛttiṃ vadatīti, pūrvakālatāṃ cetyayuktam । na
revatīvāravantīyasaṃbandhottarakālatā yajeḥ । ucyate&mdash;pratipattāveva tadi&mdash;
tyuktamasmābhiḥ । samānakartṛkatvaṃ tu ekaprayogatāmāpādayatīti
siddhaṃ viśiṣṭavidhānam । <q>artha iti prayojanamabhidhīyata</q> iti
niyogārthābhiprāyametat । kathaṃ punaḥ ekaniyogavidhānamiti
taddarśayati&mdash;revatīṣu vāravantīyamiti । nādyāpi ca samāptiḥ ।﻿<pb n="b539"/> 
kriyāpekṣiṇ‍yo hi vinā kriyāṃ na parisamāp‍yante tataḥ kṛt‍veti
kriyāsaṃbandhaḥ । ayamapi ca karotiḥ kṛt‍veti k‍tvāntaḥ san
naiva svakārasaṃbandhaparyavasāyī । kiṃ tarhi ? bhāvārthāntarāpekṣa&mdash;
statkārakaiḥ saṃbandhamanubhavati । bhāvāntaraṃ yajyarthaviśiṣṭaṃ pratīyata
ityupapattyā ekaprayojanasaṃbandha iti na vāk‍yabhedaḥ । guṇa-
phalasaṃbandhe punaḥ viparītametat । atha punaḥ etasyeti śrutyanurodhāt
revatīvāravantīyaviśiṣṭo yāgaḥ prakṛtāgniṣṭudaṅgatayaiva codyate ko doṣaḥ ?﻿<pb n="b540"/> 
na khalu kaściddoṣaḥ । adhikārāntarānarthak‍yaṃ tu bhavati । <q>athaivamucyate
revatīṣu kṛtena vāravantīyena paśukāmo yajeteti ।</q> kimidamarthāntara-
mupanyastam ? idam । bhāva evāyaṃ bhāvāntaramāśritaḥ kasmānna phala sādha&mdash;
yati ? yathaiva hi revatīvāravantīyaviśiṣṭaḥ karotyartho yajaterviśeṣaṇam ।  evaṃ
phalārthaḥ kimiti na bhavati । rāddhāntavādī tu vacanāddate na na godohanavat
praṇayanasya avihitaṃ sādhanaṃ sādhanaṃ bhavati । vihitaṃ hi sādhanaṃ bhavi-﻿<pb n="b541"/> 
tumarhati । kutaḥ ? revatīsthavāravantīyasya kāryāntarāśrayaṇā-
diti prāgap‍yuk‍tameva tat । tadidamuk‍taṃ ṛgantarapragāṇāta
stotrasādhanaviśeṣahānaṃ syāt । tataśca kratorvaiguṇ‍yaṃ bhavet । ayaṃ
cārtho <q>yāvat prakaraṇādaṅgabhāvaḥ</q> ityetena bhāṣyeṇa pradarśitaḥ ।
prakaraṇaṃ hi vāk‍yenāviniyuktasya aidamarthyāyālaṃ bhavitumarhati । tasmānna
gādohanavat kratusādhanasya sataḥ phalārthatā upapadyate kṛtveti bhāvasya ।﻿<pb n="b542"/> 
ataḥ prayok‍tṛśāstrasya bhedaḥ <quote>“yāgaguṇakaṃ revatīṣu vāravantīyaṃ
tada‍guṇako vā yāga”</quote> iti tāvat bhāvadvayasyāsyaikakartṛkatā-
lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ । aṅgāṅgibhāvastu anyato mṛgya iti darśa-
yati । kuto'nyataḥ pratyayasannikarṣāditi pradarśitam । <q>atha
punaḥ viśiṣ‍ṭe yāge vidhīyamāne tadrevatīṣu vāravantīyaṃ katha-
﻿<pb n="b543"/> 
magniṣ‍ṭoma sāma bhavatīti ।</q> yāge hi viśiṣṭe agniṣṭomasāviśeṣaṇatvaṃ
nāpapadyata ityarthaḥ । kāryasamarpaṇādagniṣṭomasāmno na doṣa iti parihāraḥ ।
athedānīmetasyeti kā kathā spaṣṭe'tra śāstrabhede ? etaddharmakasyeti mantavyam ।</p>
<p><q>saubhare puruṣaśruteḥ ।</q> ukto guṇādhikārasaṃbandhaḥ । yadā-
śrito guṇaḥ tatsaṃbandhinyadhikāre guṇādhikāra iti siddhaṃ anyāśrite guṇe﻿<pb n="b544"/> 
anyasya cā'dhikārasaṃbandhe bhāvādeva phalaṃ ityetadapi sthitam । ihedānīṃ
yadāśrito guṇaḥ tatraivādhikāraḥ । kasmādadhikārāntaramidamiti manyate ? ।
viśeṣamapaśyan sarvasya coktahetutvāt । tasmin kāmābhidhā-
nārthā punaḥ śrutiḥ । satyamevaṃ yadāśrito guṇaḥ sa iti,﻿<pb n="b545"/> 
sat‍yāṃ cāprāptau । prāptau punarabhidheyapratyabhijñānaṃ nādhikārāntarāvagatiḥ ।﻿<pb n="b546"/> 
lakṣaṇāśabdena cāsminnadhikaraṇe abhidheyapratyabhijñānamevocyate । na
padārthāntarasamarpaṇam । karmāntarānavagatiriva dadhnā juhotīti । kimartha-
starhi punaḥ śrutiḥ ? vidhānārtheti brūmaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b547"/> 
<p>nanu cādhikāraśrutiriva nidhanaśrutirapi prakṛtābhidhāyinyeva ।
satyamevaṃ yadyekanidhanameva saubharaṃ syāt । vṛṣṭikāmādhikāro'yugapatprayo-
j‍yānekanidhānaṃ tu tat । ataḥ pakṣe'pratyabhijñānāt siddhaṃ nidhanārthā
punaḥ śrutiriti ।</p>
<trailer>iti prabhākaramiśrakṛtau mīmāṃsābhāṣyavivaraṇe
dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>﻿<pb n="b548"/> 
<head>bṛhatī</head>
<head>atha dvitīyādh‍yāyasya</head>
<head>tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><q>guṇastu kratusaṃyogāt ।</q> kiṃ punaratrāpratyabhijñākāraṇaṃ ? kratva-
bhidhānaṃ rathantarasāmākhyaḥ katuḥ nāsti prakṛtaḥ । <q>kathaṃ tarhi saṃśayaḥ ?</q>﻿<pb n="b549"/> 
yadiśabdaśravaṇāt। yadiśabdo hi prasiddhārthatāmāpadayati ato bhavati
saṃśayaḥ। kiṃ yadiśravaṇādupasarjanaparamidamabhidhānaṃ, utābhidhānasāmarthyāt﻿<pb n="b550"/> 
kat‍vantarābhidhānamastviti । kiṃ yuk‍taṃ ? abhidhānasāmarthyamantaraṅgaṃ antaraṅgaṃ
ca bahiraṅgādbalīyaḥ । paripūrṇaṃ hi padaṃ padāntaramākāṅkṣati । anvayānurodhī ca﻿<pb n="b551"/> 
yadiśabdo na svatantraḥ । tasmāt yathā kratvantarābhidhānamupapadyate
tathātasyārtho varṇanīyaḥ । pradarśitāśca prakārāḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b552"/> ﻿<pb n="b553"/> 
<p><q>ekasya tu liṅgabhedāt ।</q> atrocyate&mdash;yadyabhidhānavirodhaḥ
syāt yadyartho na vivakṣ‍yeta na tvatra abhidhānavirodha upapadyate । tarhyupa-
sarjanārthe cāpi nimittatayā parigṛhyamāṇe kratorevābhidhānam । nanu
sāmāntarasaṃbandhe sati kratorabhidhānaṃ na prāp‍noti । maivam&mdash;virodhāpekṣaṃ
hi sāmarthyam । vṛhatā ca rathantarasya kratusaṃbandhe virodhaḥ na sāmamātreṇa ।﻿<pb n="b554"/> 
tasmādanityaḥ śabda itivadupapannamabhidhānam । tadyogācca nimittatvaṃ kratoḥ ।
kathaṃ tarhi upasarjanārthe nimittamityucyate tadanubandhānusāriṇī hi
bhedāvagatiḥ katoḥ । tasmāttannimittamityucyate guṇaphalopabandhavat ।﻿<pb n="b555"/> 
kratoreva hi nimittatvaṃ na tadanubandhasya ।</p>
<p><q>aveṣ‍ṭau yajñasaṃyogāt ।</q> atra vrāhmaṇādiśravaṇaṃ yadyartha&mdash;
yogaśca saṃśayahetuḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b556"/> 
<p>yadi rājasūye brāhmaṇānāṃ prāptiḥ tadā pūrvādhikaraṇavat
abhidhānāvirodhāt nimittārthāni śravaṇāni । atha tu na
prāptiḥ tadā karmāntaravidhānaṃ tadanurodhena ca yadyartho vyākhyeyaḥ pūrvādhi-
karaṇapūrvapakṣavat । kathaṃ punaḥ prāp‍tyaprāptī avagamyate ? rājaśabdasyā-
bhidheyānirūpaṇāt । yadi hi rājaśabdaḥ karmayogāt kartari vartate tadā﻿<pb n="b557"/> 
prāptiḥ । atha kartṛ(ri)yogāt karmābhidhīyate tadā na prāptiḥ tadā pika-
nemasatatāmarasādīnāmiva m‍lecchavyavahārādeva abhidhānāvagatiḥ kaḥ punaratra
nirṇāyakahetuḥ ? pūrvapakṣavādītu manyate karmayogāt kartaryabhidhānam, ārya-
vyavahārāt । m‍lecchānāṃ punarāryavirodhe hyuk‍tamaprāmāṇ‍yaṃ yavavarāhādiṣu । nanu
cāryāṇāṃ mūrdhābhiṣik‍tāḥ śabdavidaḥ kartṛyogāt karmaśabdaṃ smaranti;﻿<pb n="b558"/> 
satyaṃ, vyavahāramūlatvāt smṛteḥ prakṛtiprat‍yayavibhāgārthametadbhaviṣ‍yati ।
prakaraṇānugrahāt yadiśabdopabandhācca nimittārthāni śravaṇāni । kiñca
m‍lecchairapi karmayogāt kartari prayuj‍yata eva । tataḥ kim ? āviprati-
pattiḥ avipratipatteśca na pratipakṣatāṃ kartṛpūrvakaḥ prayogaḥ bhajata
ityabhiprāyaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b559"/>
<p>atrābhidhīyate&mdash;prāpakāṇ‍yevaitāni । kutaḥ ? smṛteḥ।
vipratipattau hi prayogasya smṛtiḥ pramāṇaṃ gavādiṣviva ।
smṛtiśca kartṛyogāt karmaśabda iti । nanu cāpratipakṣaḥ
sārvabhaumaḥ prayoga ityuktam । sati ca pratipakṣe smṛtito nirṇayaḥ ।﻿<pb n="b560"/>
āryaprayogamūlatvācca vyākaraṇarabhṛteḥ prayogadapi virodhaḥ । ataśca virodhe
t‍vanapekṣamiti bādha eva nyāy‍yaḥ । prātipadikārthavibhāgārthatayopapadyata
it‍yuk‍tam । ucyate । na smṛtiravabādhituṃ śak‍yate । mūlābhāvāddhi
s‍mṛterbādhaḥ । asti cedaṃ mūlaṃ mantrāṇāṃ prayogaḥ । nanu ca
sārvabhaumaprayogaḥ āryavyavahāraśca virudhyate । na viruddhayate । andhra&mdash;
prayogamūlāyāmapi s‍mṛtāvupapadyata evāryavyavahāraḥ, sārvabhaumat‍vaṃ ca ।﻿<pb n="b561"/>
tas‍mādvirodhe t‍vanapekṣamityetadap‍yuktamayuk‍tam । apratyakṣatā siddhaiva । naivaṃ
sati sārvabhaumasya prat‍yakṣatopapadyate । kāryakaratvāt prayogopapatteḥ।
﻿<pb n="b562"/>
tasmāt prāpakāṇ‍yetāni vacanāni kṣatriyābhidhānādrājaśabdasya । yaduk‍taṃ
prātipadikārthavibhāgārthā s‍mṛtiriti; na mūle saṃbhavatyanyārthatā sūtrasya
śak‍yate vak‍tum । ataḥ prāpakāṇ‍yetāni ।</p>﻿<pb n="b563"/>﻿<pb n="b564"/>
<p><q>ādhāne'sarvaśeṣatvāt ।</q> kimatra cintyate ? ādhānagato bhedaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b565"/>
kiṃ bhinnamādhānaṃ utābhinnamiti । nanu ca ṣaṣṭhe'p‍yadhikārārthatayā
bheda eva cin‍titaḥ । ya evaṃ vidvānāgnimādhatte iti idameva pratipakṣa-
tayopanyastam । arthākṣepaśca । tasmādvedaṃ nārab‍dhavyam । ekasyaiva nyāyasya
phaladvayamidam । tasmādatrocyate । (bhedā)bhede hyanubandhabhedo hetuḥ ।﻿<pb n="b566"/>
ato brāhmaṇādyanubandhabhedo abhede na yuktaḥ । tatra adhikṛtasyāgnayaḥ
uta sāgnikasyādhikāra ityanyaiva cintā । sa cāyaṃ viśeṣaḥ tatraiva
nipuṇataraṃ varṇ‍yate । iha tu kevalavidhānābhāvāt brāhmaṇādyanubandhabhedādbheda
ityuktam । kaḥ punaratra bhedābhedayoḥ karmaṇi viśeṣaḥ ? yasya
hi yasmin kāle ādhānaṃ vihitaṃ tasya hi tadaivādhānam ।﻿<pb n="b567"/>
nimittārthāyāmapi śrutau tul‍yametat । ubhayaniyamāt । evaṃ tarhi
nakṣatrādyādhānametatkālīnameva trayāṇāmapi kathaṃ syāditi viśeṣaḥ ।
adhikāre punarviśeṣaṃ darśayiṣ‍yāmaḥ । nanu cātmanepadopanyāso&mdash;
'dhikāra evopayuj‍yate kṛtrimādinivṛttyarthaṃ na punaḥ bhedacintāyāṃ,﻿<pb n="b568"/>
pārārthyepi hi ādhānasyānubandhabhedāt siddhayatyeva bhedaḥ tasminnimitta-
tvāt । ucyate&mdash;evaṃ cādhikāravirodho na bhaviṣ‍yatītyabhyuccayo
draṣṭavyaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b569"/>﻿<pb n="b570"/>﻿<pb n="b571"/>
<p><q>ayaneṣu codanāntaram ।</q> saṃjñā cotpattisaṃyogāditi saṃjñā
bhet‍trīti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ।</p>﻿<pb n="b572"/>
<p><q>vikāro vā prakaraṇāt ।</q> sat‍yaṃ saṃjñā bhet‍trī yatra prakṛte karmaṇi
guṇāntarānuk‍te sati guṇāntarānuraktāḥ sādhikārāścodanāḥ śrūyante ।</p>﻿<pb n="b573"/>
tatra saṃjñānyatvataḥ karmānyatvamākhyātasāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ pradarśayadbhiḥ prada-
rśitamasmābhiḥ ।</q></p>﻿<pb n="b574"/>
<p>yacca samāptaṃ ca phale vāk‍yamiti na phalacodanā karmāntaratvamā-
pādayituṃ kṣamā ananubandhatvāt phalānām । kathaṃ tarhi <quote>‘phalaṃ cā-
karmasannidhau’</quote> iti ? asannidhānameva hi tatra kāraṇaṃ na phalam ।
na hyasannihitaṃ karma yajinā viśeṣataḥ pratipādayituṃ śak‍yate । tasmā-﻿<pb n="b575"/>
dvidhānata eva tatra viśeṣo'vagantavyaḥ । iha punaḥ sannihitamastīti
na phalaṃ bhedakamityucyate । saṃjñāntaropalabdhasya prayojanaṃ tatpravṛtti-
nimittaguṇayuktasya kathaṃ nāma vidhānamiti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b576"/>
<p><q>saṃskāraścāprakaraṇe ।</q> <quote>‘vāyavyaṃ ś‍vetamālabheta’</quote> ityasmin
vāk‍ye parasparasvarūpānanvitameva padārthajātaṃ lakṣyate ।  kathaṃ ? aya-
mālabhatirna dravyadevatānvayi । tasmādālabhatervidhānaṃ dravyadevatāpadasaṃbandha-
nirapekṣasya । anuvādo vā, prathamapūrvapakṣavādī anuvādaṃ manyate ।
ś‍vetapadānvayalābhāt । ato yadālabheta tacchvetaṃ iti vāk‍yārthaḥ ।﻿<pb n="b577"/>
vāyavyabrahmavarcasakāmapadayoḥ kā vārtā ? parasparāsaṅgatervāk‍yāntaraṃ aruṇā&mdash;
divaditi manyate । yāvaduk‍taṃ veti brahmavarcasakāmapadānvayā'pi labhyata
ityaparaḥ pakṣaḥ । ś‍vetamālabheta brahmavarcasakāma iti paraṃ vāyavya-
padasyaikasyaivoddhāraḥ । etadeva yuk‍taṃ īṣālambhasyāprakṛtatvāt । atha
liṅartho vihitopalakṣaṇārthaḥ parigṛhyate vidhānaṃ na prāpnoti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b578"/>﻿<pb n="b579"/>
<p><q>yajatistu dravyaphalabhok‍tṛsaṃyogāt ।</q> atrocyate । syādevaṃ
yadi samastapadānvayo na bhavati । bhavati tvasau । kathaṃ ? vāyavyaṃ
ś‍vetamālabheta bhūtikāma iti vāk‍yārtho vidhīyate । kathaṃ tarhyā-
labhatiḥ ? anuvādo'yaṃ anyataḥ prāpteḥ । aprāptasyānvayo na
saṃbhavati । nāvidhīyamānasya svargakāmavat । ato'yamālabhatirityekaṃ
śāstram । asaṃbhavatyanvaye śāstrabhedaḥ praviśa piṇ‍tībhitivat ।﻿<pb n="b580"/>
nanu guṇavidhidūṣaṇapakṣe'nekaguṇavidhānaṃ darśayati । uktaṃ ca na vāyavya-
brahmavarcasakāmau saṃbadhyete iti । ucyate&mdash;nāyamabhiprāyaḥ īṣālabhbhe pada-
dvayavidhānamiti । kathaṃ tarhi ? yadi prāptānuvādena īṣālambhe ś‍veto guṇo
vidhīyate [kiṃ na] prākṛtepi । atha kasmādālambho vāyavye brahmavarcasa-﻿<pb n="b581"/>
kāme vā aprakṛte'pi na vidhīyate ? ko nu khalu nirṇayaḥ
īṣālambhe ś‍vetaguṇavidhānamityatra ? na cālabhbhavyāptau pramāṇamastītyuktam ।
idaṃ cāpara; kathaṃ ālabhate; ananvayamāśaṅkaya taccālabhatyarthaviśiṣṭamiti ।﻿<pb n="b582"/>
kathaṃ tarhi ? idantaduktam । nāyamekasya vāk‍yasyātibhāraḥ yaduta kriyādvaya-
sambandhinarthaṃ vidhirvidadhātīti । aṅgāṅgibhāvasyānyataḥ siddheḥ ।
tasmādālabhatyarthaviśiṣṭamityanvayābhiprāyametat ।</p>﻿<pb n="b583"/>
<p><q>viśaye prāyadarśanāt ।</q> kimidaṃ viśaye prāyadarśanā-
diti ? sūtrasyānākṣiptaviṣayatāṃ darśayati । āgamagamyo'tra&mdash;﻿<pb n="b584"/>
viṣayo na sūtrāt gamyata ityarthaḥ । tathā ca darśitaṃ vṛttikāravacanāt
viṣayamavagacchāmaḥ upapadyate caitaditi । kaḥ punaratra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ﻿<pb n="b585"/>
ālabhatisāmānyāt yajimatā bhavitavyamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । dravya-
devatāsambandhāśravaṇāt na yajimāniti rāddhāntaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>saṃyuktastvarthaśabdena ।</q> kimityadhikaraṇāntaramidaṃ kṛtam ?
arthavādāt devatāsambandhanirākaraṇārtham ।</p>﻿<pb n="b586"/>
viśeṣākāṅkṣayāṃ hi arthavādānnirṇayaḥ । iha tūpadhāne viniyukta-
tvāt dravyastutiparaiva devatāśrutiriti ।</p>﻿<pb n="b587"/>
idamapi pūrveṇa tulyam ।</p>
<p><q>pātrīvate tu ।</q> uktaṃ dravyadevatāsaṃyuk‍taṃ saṃskārakarmavadvāk‍yaṃ
yāgasya codakamiti tadidānīṃ sandihyate । prakṛte yāge dravyadevatā-
saṃskārakarmavadvāk‍yaṃ kiṃ saṃskāramātrasya vidhāyakaṃ uta etadapi yāgasya
vidhāyakamiti । kathaṃ punaḥ spaṣṭe prakṛtayāgavacanatve saṃśayaḥ ?﻿<pb n="b588"/>
saguṇanirguṇaśravaṇāt । saguṇaṃ hi prakṛtaṃ karma nirguṇaṃ ceha śrūyate ।
tasmāt karmāntare utsṛjatiḥ । utsṛjatiparyagnikṛtaśabdau ca
kāryataḥ prāptāvanūdyete । kimidamuk‍taṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa <quote>“api ca tvāṣṭrasyo-
tsarge vidhīyamāne paryagnikṛtasyeti viśeṣaṇaṃ nāvakalpata”</quote> iti । idamuktaṃ
viśiṣṭānuvādalakṣaṇo vāk‍yabheda iti । nanu ca prakṛtaḥ paryagnikṛta﻿<pb n="b589"/>
eva, ko'tra vāk‍yabheda iti । prakṛtatvena hi avivakṣitānvayo labhyate ।
na punarvivakṣāpyutsarge । idamaparaṃ&mdash;kiṃ paryagnikṛta eva pātnīvatatā
vidhīyata iti pātnīvatatvameva vidhīyate । paryagnikṛtatā prāptaiva ।
saiveyamanena prakāreṇa darśitā bhāṣyakāreṇa ।</p>﻿<pb n="b590"/>
atrocyate&mdash;paryagnikṛtasyāyamutsargaścodyate prakṛtasya । nanu ca tvāṣṭaṃ
pātnīvataṃ iti śravaṇāt na pātnīvataśabdena prakṛtābhidhānamupapadyate । ucyate
na nopapadyate । yasya hi samāsenābhidhānaṃ tatra vyastasyābhidhānānupapattiḥ ।
aindrāgna āg‍neyavat । yatra punaḥ vyastayorābhidhāna siddhaṃ prakṛte'pi
tatra nārthāntare buddhirupapadyate । tasmāt saṃskāravidhānamevedamavaccheda&mdash;
phalam । nanu paryagnikṛtavivakṣā utsarge nopapadyetetyuktam ।﻿<pb n="b591"/>
satyaṃ nopapadyate yadi pātnīvataśabdo vivakṣyeta । sa tu prakṛtābhidhānāt
prāptānvayavacana evetyadoṣaḥ ।</p>
<p><q>adravyatvātkevale ।</q> sa evāyaṃ vicāro'nuvartate । kiṃ yaji-
mati tatsaṃskārakarma uta kevalasaṃskāravidhānamiti । tadiha cintyate । kiṃ﻿<pb n="b592"/>
grahaṇamātracodane ete uta yajitī iti । kiṃ yuktam ? yaji-
matī iti । kathaṃ ? aprayojanavataḥ saṃskārābhāvāt । yāgaśabdaśravaṇācca
sāmayuktāt yajimatī ete codane । grahaṇādiśabdaścālabhativat prāpta
evānūdyate sasomaśabdakaḥ । nanu cāṃśau na somayuk‍to yajiḥ
śrūyate । uk‍taṃ niṣprayojanasya saṃskārābhāvāt adābhyasāhacaryācca
tadvadbhaviṣyati iti । nanu ca jyotiṣṭomasyaivāyaṃ yajiranuvādaḥ﻿<pb n="b593"/>
kasmānna bhaviṣyati । aprakṛtatvāt । prakṛte hi viśeṣe sāmānyaśabdo
viśeṣavacano bhaviṣyati nāprakṛte । tasmādyajimatī ete codane ।</p>
<p>atrocyate&mdash;saṃskāramātracodane ete । kasmāt ? tāvanmātra-
śravaṇāt । nanu ca somavān yajiratra śrūyata ityuk‍taṃ; sat‍yaṃ śrūyate ।
anyaparastu saḥ । nanu ca kevalasaṃskāracodane anarthake bhavataḥ, prayojana-
vato'śravaṇāt, sannidhānābhāvācca । atrābhidhīyate । somayuk‍to﻿<pb n="b594"/>
yajiḥ nānyārthatāṃ pratipat‍tuṃ śak‍noti yadi na jyotiṣṭomamanuvadati ।
sa hyupadeśāt somavān । tasmāttat‍sambandhāttat‍saṃskāraḥ । tat‍sāha&mdash;
caryāc‍cāṃśāvapīt‍yuktam ।</p>
<p><q>agristu liṅgadarśanāt ।</q> ya evaṃ vidvānagniṃ cinuta iti
kimayaṃ saṃskāracodanā vā uta yajimat‍karmeti । yajimat‍karmeti brūmaḥ﻿<pb n="b595"/>
<q>yajiśabdasāmānādhikaraṇyāt ।</q> agniṃ cinuta iti prāpteḥ । cinoti-
ridānīṃ kimarthaḥ । ālabhatītivadbhaviṣyatīti cet tat nopapadyate । tatra
hi kāryataḥ prāptirālabhateḥ । iha punarna cinoteḥ anyataḥ kāryatāvagatiḥ ।﻿<pb n="b596"/>
upadeśāditi cenna, vāk‍yabhedaprasaṅgāt । prakaraṇamapīti vāk‍yabhedasavya-
pekṣameva । evaṃ tarhīyaṃ kañcitsaṅghātaṃ kāryaprāptamaṅgīkṛtyānuvādo bhaviṣyati ।
atha vā iṣṭakābhiragniṃ cinuta iti prāptasyāyamanuvādaḥ । tathā ca liṅga-
darśanamuktam ।</p>
<p><q>dravyaṃ vā syāccodanāyāḥ ।</q> atrocyate&mdash;saṃskāracodanaivaiṣā ।
kutaḥ ? saṃskāraśabdaśravaṇāt । agniśabdasya ca jvalane rūḍhatvāt ।﻿<pb n="b597"/>
kathaṃ tarhi agniṃ anuyajatīti ? cayanasaṃskṛte'g‍nau paścādyajatītyarthaḥ ।
<q>cayanamabhinirvṛtyeti yāvat ।</q> atha yalliṅgamuktaṃ tat cayana&mdash;
saṃskṛtāgniyukte draṣṭavyaṃ tāsveva codanāsu ।</p>﻿<pb n="b598"/>
<p><q>prakaraṇāntare prayojanānyatvam ।</q> māsamagnihotraṃ juhotīti
śrūyate । tatra śāstrāntarāmidaṃ agnihotraśāstrāt uta neti cintyate । nanu
ca māsavidhāne'pi śāstrāntaramevaitat । vāk‍yāntaramevedaṃ na śāstrāntaram ।
tulyakāryaguṇāntaravidhānāpekṣaṃ bhavati śāstrāntaraṃ na kevalabhāvavidhānāpekṣam﻿<pb n="b599"/>
kiṃ yuktam ? na śāstrāntaramidaṃ naiyamika evāyaṃ guṇavidhiḥ ।
kutaḥ ? agnihotraśabdapratyabhijñānāt ।</p>﻿<pb n="b600"/>
<p>atrocyate&mdash;prakaraṇāntare prayojanānyatvam । kimidaṃ prakara-
ṇāntara iti ? aprakṛtābhidhāna ityarthaḥ । nātra prakṛtābhidhāyako'yaṃ
juhotiśabdaḥ dadhnā juhoti itivat । nanu cāgnihotrābhidhānāt, naiya&mdash;
mika eva guṇavacanatā'vagamyate । na, juhoterarthāntarāvagateḥ । kathaṃ
punaranyārthāvagatiḥ । upasadbhiścaritveti śravaṇāt । ato juhotya-
rthānusāryayaṃ agnihotraśabdaḥ na viparītaḥ । tasmāt siddhaṃ prakaraṇānta-
rat‍vam । prakaraṇāntaraṃ ca śāstrāntaratvam ।</p>﻿<pb n="b601"/>
<p><q>phalaṃ cākarmasannidhau ।</q> kimidamanyadeva bhedakāraṇam ? neti
brūmaḥ । atrāpyaprakṛtābhidhānataiva pratipādyate । kathaṃ ? pūrvatra upasadbhiśca-
ritvā iti aprakṛtābhidhānatā uktā । idānīṃ punaḥ phalasaṃbandhenāprakṛtā-
bhidhānaṃ pratīyata iti pūrvapakṣavādino'bhiprāyaḥ । karmaṇo vidheyatvāt ।﻿<pb n="b602"/>
rāddhāntī tu manyate । anyārthe bhavatyapi prakṛtābhidhānam । svārthe
punaḥ na prakṛtābhidhānaṃ pratīyate । phalasaṃbandhe ca svārtho bhāvaśabdaḥ ।
nahyabhāvārthasya vidhānaṃ saṃbhavatītyuk‍tam । na ca dadhyādivat bhāvānu&mdash;
praveśo'dhikārasya saṃbhavatīti vakṣyāmaḥ । anyathāpi aprakṛtābhidhānaṃ
siddham ।</p>﻿<pb n="b603"/>
<p><q>sannidhau tvavibhāgāt ।</q> uk‍taṃ phalaṃ cākarmasannidhāviti ।
tasyedaṃ pratyudāharaṇam । karmasannidhau phalayogo na śāstrāntaratvamā&mdash;
pādayati । nanu ca vidheyaparatvādbhāvārthasya kiṃ sannidhiḥ kariṣyati ?
satyaṃ vidheyo bhāvārthaḥ । na punaḥ sannidhānamatikrāmati । nanu
atatparatvādabhidhānasya kiṃ sannidhiḥ kariṣyati ? idaṃ kariṣyati ।﻿<pb n="b604"/>
atatpare'pyabhidhāne'nyato buddhiṃ niruṇaddhi । upadeśaparamapyabhidhānaṃ
sannidhau sati na viśeṣāntaramākṣep‍tuṃ kṣamaḥ । tasmād‍yuk‍taṃ sannidhau tva-
vibhāgāditi ।</p>
<p><q>āg‍neyastūktahetutvāt ।</q> aviśeṣāt karmāntaramityāśaṅkitaṃ
pūrvapakṣiṇā । āg‍neyamātraśravaṇāt । avibhāgastu karmaṇo'bhyāso
dviruk‍tena pratīyeta ।</p>﻿<pb n="b605"/>
<p>atrocyate&mdash;rāddhāntavādī tu paurṇamāsīsaṃyuk‍taṃ vidhāyakaṃ manyate । aprati-
pakṣatvāt । vihitasya ca punarvacanaṃ na śakyate'rthāntaratayā pratipat‍tum । abhyā-﻿<pb n="b606"/>
sādhikaraṇe punarvidhānāviśeṣādityuktam । nanu ca niṣprayojanaṃ punarvacana-
mityuktam । na prayojanavaśādarthāntarapratipattiḥ avagamo hi tatvānyatve
hetuḥ na cānarthakyam । aindrāgnavithānaṃ prayojanamityuktam ।</p>
<trailer>iti vṛhatyāṃ dvitīyādhyāyasya
tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
﻿<pb n="b607"/>
<head>atha caturthaḥ pādaḥ</head>
<p><q>yāvajjīviko'bhyāsaḥ ।</q> yāvajjīvamagnihotraṃ juhotītyatra cintyate
kiṃ kāmyācchāstrāntaraṃ uta ekamiti । kiṃ prāptaṃ ? karmaṇaḥ prāptatvāt 
guṇavidhiḥ । tataścaikaṃ śāstram । kaḥ punaratra guṇo vidhī&mdash;
yate ? jīvanaṃ tāvat prāptatvādavidheyam । evaṃ tarhi jīvanena
﻿<pb n="b608"/>
lakṣitaḥ kālaḥ । nanu cāsāvapi nityaprāpta eva ; na, yāvadanubandha-
tayā'prāpteḥ । tasmāt kālavidhiḥ । ko'yaṃ kālo nāma ? yaḥ
kālavidbhiruk‍taḥ । ke te kālavidaḥ ? ye jyotirvidaḥ ।
tathā ca liṅgadarśanam । tasmādekaṃ śās‍tramiti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b609"/>
<p><q>karturvā śrutisaṃyogāt ।</q> atrocyate&mdash;adhikāracodanaiṣā na
kālavidhiḥ । ataśca kāmyāt śāstrāntaratvam । kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ adhikāra-
cādanaiṣā na kālavidhiriti ? kālavidhau hi padadvayamapi lakṣaṇa-
﻿<pb n="b610"/>
yā'nvapi bhavati । adhikāropadeśe tu śrutyā । na ca saṃbhavantyāṃ
﻿<pb n="b611"/>
śrutau lakṣaṇāśrayaṇe kāraṇamasti । tasmādadhikāracodanaivaiṣā । adhikāracodanāyāṃ
﻿<pb n="b612"/>
ca prayogāntarasiddhiḥ । evaṃ ca kṛtvā liṅgadarśanāni ghaṭante ।
jarāmaryavādo'pyupapadyata ityuktam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="b613"/>
<p><q>nāmarūpadharmaviśeṣapunarukti ।</q> atra bhedapramāṇābhāsāni
pūrvapakṣe upanyasya rāddhānte kecit granthasaṃbandhitayā,
kecit svādhyāyasaṃbandhitayā, kecit karmāntarāśrayatayā,
kecit yadeti kālayogādityevamādibhiḥ parihāraiḥ parihṛtāti ।
﻿<pb n="b614"/>
tasmādvākyāntarāṇyevaitāni na śās‍trāntarāṇīti siddham ।</p>
<trailer>iti bṛhatyāṃ dvitīyādhyāyasya
caturthaḥ pādaḥ</trailer>
